cit pratyapaśyāma śubham vā yadi vā aśubham apayānam tatas cakruḥ sahitāḥ sarva vājibhiḥ kauraveṣu ca yāteṣu tadā rājan dinakṣaye jayam su manasaḥ prāpya pārthāḥ sva śibiram yayuḥ vāditra śabdaiḥ vividhaiḥ siṃhanādaiḥ ca nartitaiḥ kṛte avahāre taiḥ vīraiḥ sainikāḥ sarve eva te āśiṣaḥ pāṇḍaveyeṣu prāyujyanta nareśvarāḥ tatas kṛte avahāre ca prahṛṣṭāḥ kuru pāṇḍavāḥ niśāyām śibiram gatvā nyaviśanta nareśvarāḥ yakṣa rakṣaḥ piśācāḥ ca śvāpadāni ca saṃghaśas dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca ekaḥ ca imām mahīm jitvā cakre bali bhṛtaḥ nṛpān ekaḥ kirāta rūpeṇa sthitam śarvam ayodhayat saṃjayaḥ uvāca dīna svarāḥ dūyamānāḥ māninaḥ śatrubhiḥ jitāḥ bhagna daṃṣṭrāḥ hata viṣāḥ pada ākrāntāḥ iva uragāḥ tān abravīt tatas karṇaḥ kruddhaḥ sarpaḥ iva śvasan karam kareṇa abhipīḍya prekṣamāṇaḥ tava ātmajam yattaḥ dṛḍhaḥ ca dakṣaḥ ca dhṛtimān arjunaḥ sadā sa bodhayati ca api enam prāpta kālam adhokṣajaḥ sahasā astra visargeṇa vayam tena adya vañcitāḥ śvas tu aham tasya saṃkalpam sarvam hantā mahīpate sukha uṣitāḥ te rajanīm hṛṣṭāḥ yuddhāya niryayuḥ atha pratīpa kartāram satatam vijita ātmanām sasmāra vṛṣabha skandham karṇam duryodhanaḥ tadā kārtavīrya samam vīrye karṇam rājñaḥ agamat manaḥ sūtaputram mahā iṣvāsam bandhum ātyayikeṣu iva dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca api adrākṣata tam yūyam śīta ārtāḥ iva bhāskaram kṛte avahāre sainyānām pravṛtte ca raṇe punar katham ca pāṇḍavāḥ sarve yuyudhuḥ tatra sūtajam karṇaḥ hi ekaḥ mahā bāhuḥ hanyāt pārthān sa somakān karṇasya bhujayoḥ vīryam śakra viṣṇu samam matam tathā astrāṇi su ghorāṇi vikramaḥ ca mahātmanaḥ duryodhanam tadā dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavena bhṛśa arditam parākrāntān pāṇḍu sutān dṛṣṭvā ca api mahā āhave aho bata mahat duḥkham yatra pāṇḍu sutān raṇe na atarat rabhasaḥ karṇaḥ daivam nūnam parāyaṇam aho dyūtasya niṣṭhā iyam ghorā saṃprati vartate aho duḥkhāni tīvrāṇi duryodhana kṛtāni aham sahiṣyāmi su ghorāṇi śalya bhūtāni saṃjaya yuddheṣu nāma divyeṣu vartamāneṣu saṃjaya aśrauṣam nihatān putrān nityam eva ca nirjitān na pāṇḍavānām samare kaḥ cit asti nivārakaḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca atikrāntam hi yat kāryam paścāt cintayati iti ca tat idam tava kāryam tu dūra prāptam vijānatā na kṛtam yat tvayā pūrvam prāpta aprāpta vicāraṇe uktaḥ asi bahudhā rājan mā yudhyasva iti pāṇḍavaiḥ gṛhṇīṣe na ca tat mohāt pāṇḍaveṣu viśām pate tvayā pāpāni ghorāṇi samācīrṇāni pāṇḍuṣu tvad kṛte vartate ghoraḥ pārthivānām jana kṣayaḥ śṛṇu sarvam yathāvṛttam ghoram vaiśasam acyuta prabhātāyām rajanyām tu karṇaḥ rājānam abhyayāt adya rājan sameṣyāmi pāṇḍavena yaśasvinā haniṣyāmi ca tam vīram sa vā mām nihaniṣyati bahu tvāt mama kāryāṇām tathā pārthasya pārthiva idam tu me yathāprajñam śṛṇu vākyam viśām pate a nihatya raṇe pārtham na aham eṣyāmi bhārata abhiyāsyati mām pārthaḥ śakra śaktyā vinākṛtam āyudhānām ca yat vīryam dravyāṇām arjunasya ca sauṣṭhave ca astra yoge ca savyasācī na mad samaḥ sarva āyudha mahāmātram vijayam nāma tat dhanuḥ indra artham abhikāmena nirmitam viśvakarmaṇā yena daitya gaṇān rājan jitavān vai śatakratuḥ yasya ghoṣeṇa daityānām vimuhyanti diśaḥ daśa dhanuḥ ghoram rāma dattam gāṇḍīvāt tat viśiṣyate triḥsapta kṛtvas pṛthivī dhanuṣā tena nirjitā dhanuṣaḥ yasya karmāṇi divyāni prāha bhārgavaḥ tat rāmaḥ hi adadāt mahyam yena yotsyāmi pāṇḍavam sa parvata vana dvīpā hata dviṣ bhūḥ sa sāgarā na asādhyam vidyate me adya tvad priya artham viśeṣataḥ na hi mām samare soḍhum sa śaktaḥ agnim taruḥ yathā avaśyam tu mayā vācyam yena hīnaḥ asmi phalgunāt jyā tasya dhanuṣaḥ divyā tathā akṣayyau mahā iṣudhī tasya divyam dhanuḥ śreṣṭham gāṇḍīvam ajaram yudhi tatra aham adhikaḥ pārthāt dhanuṣā tena pārthiva mayā ca abhyadhikaḥ vīraḥ pāṇḍavaḥ tat nibodha me raśmigrāhaḥ ca dāśārhaḥ sarva loka namaskṛtaḥ agnidattaḥ ca vai divyaḥ rathaḥ kāñcana bhūṣaṇaḥ acchedyaḥ sarvatas vīra vājinaḥ ca manaḥ javāḥ kṛṣṇaḥ ca sraṣṭā jagataḥ ratham tam abhirakṣati ayam tu sadṛśaḥ vīraḥ śalyaḥ samiti śobhanaḥ nārācān gārdhra patrān ca śakaṭāni vahantu me rathāḥ ca mukhyāḥ rāja indra yuktāḥ vājibhiḥ uttamaiḥ āyāntu paścāt satatam mām eva bharata ṛṣabha śalyaḥ hi abhyadhikaḥ kṛṣṇāt arjunāt adhikaḥ hi aham yathā aśva hṛdayam veda dāśārhaḥ para vīra hā tathā śalyaḥ api jānīte hayānām vai mahā rathaḥ etat kṛtam mahā rāja tvayā icchāmi paraṃtapa evam kṛte kṛtam mahyam sarva kāmaiḥ bhaviṣyati tatas draṣṭāsi samare yat kariṣyāmi bhārata sarvathā pāṇḍavān sarvān jeṣyāmi adya samāgatān sa upāsaṅgāḥ rathāḥ sa aśvāḥ anuyāsyanti sūtaja nārācān gārdhrapakṣān ca śakaṭāni vahantu te anuyāsyāma karṇa tvām vayam sarve ca pārthivāḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca evam uktvā mahā rāja tava putrāḥ pratāpavān abhigamya abravīt rājā madra rājam idam vacaḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca yathā nṛpati siṃhānām madhye tvām varayati ayam tasmāt pārtha vināśa artham hita artham mama ca eva hi sārathyam rathinām śreṣṭha su manāḥ kartum arhasi asya abhīśu grahaḥ loke na anyaḥ asti bhavatā samaḥ sa pātu sarvatas karṇam bhavān brahmā iva śaṃkaram pārthasya sacivaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ yathā abhīśu grahaḥ varaḥ bhīṣmaḥ droṇaḥ kṛpaḥ karṇaḥ bhavān bhojaḥ ca vīryavān eṣām eva kṛtaḥ bhāgaḥ navadhā pṛtanāpate tābhyām atītya tau bhāgau nihatāḥ mama śatravaḥ asmadīyāḥ ca bahavaḥ svargāya upagatāḥ raṇe tyaktvā prāṇān yathāśakti ceṣṭāḥ kṛtvā ca puṣkalāḥ bhavān ca puruṣa vyāghra sarva loka mahā rathaḥ tasmin jaya āśā vipulā mama madra janādhipa pārthasya samare kṛṣṇaḥ yathā abhīśu vara grahaḥ tena yuktaḥ raṇe pārthaḥ rakṣyamāṇaḥ ca pārthiva yāni karmāṇi kurute pratyakṣāṇi tathā eva te bhāgaḥ avaśiṣṭaḥ karṇasya tava ca eva mahā dyute tam bhāgam saha karṇena yugapad nāśaya āhave sūrya aruṇau yathā dṛṣṭvā tamaḥ naśyati māriṣa tathā naśyantu kaunteyāḥ sa pāñcālāḥ sa sṛñjayāḥ rathānām pravaraḥ karṇaḥ yantṝṇām pravaraḥ bhavān yathā sarvāsu avasthāsu vārṣṇeyaḥ pāti pāṇḍavam tathā bhavān paritrātu karṇam vaikartanam raṇe tvayā sārathinā hi eṣaḥ apradhṛṣyaḥ bhaviṣyati devatānām api raṇe sa śakrāṇām mahīpate kim punar pāṇḍaveyānām mā atiśaṅkīḥ vacaḥ mama tri śikhām bhrukuṭīm kṛtvā dhunvan hastau punar punar avamanyase mām gāndhāre dhruvam mām pariśaṅkase yat mām bravīṣi visrabdham sārathyam kriyatām iti asmattaḥ abhyadhikam karṇam manyamānaḥ praśaṃsasi na ca aham yudhi rādheyam gaṇaye tulyam ātmanā ādiśyatām abhyadhikaḥ mama aṃśaḥ pṛthivīpate paśya vīryam mama adya tvam saṃgrāme dahataḥ ripūn na ca abhikāmān kauravya vidhāya hṛdaye pumān asmadvidhaḥ pravarteta mā mā tvam atiśaṅkithāḥ dhanuḥ paśya ca me citram śarān ca āśīviṣa upamān ratham paśya ca me kḷptam sat aśvaiḥ vāta vegitaiḥ gadām ca paśya gāndhāre hema paṭṭa vibhūṣitām dārayeyam mahīm kruddhaḥ vikireyam ca parvatān śoṣayeyam samudrān ca tejasā svena pārthiva na hi pāpīyasaḥ śreyān bhūtvā preṣya tvam utsahe yaḥ hi abhyupagatam prītyā garīyāṃsam vaśe sthitam brāhmaṇāḥ brahmaṇā sṛṣṭāḥ mukhāt kṣatram atha urasaḥ ūrubhyām asṛjat vaiśyān śūdrān padbhyām iti śrutiḥ tebhyaḥ varṇa viśeṣāḥ ca pratiloma anuloma jāḥ goptāraḥ saṃgrahītāraḥ dātāraḥ kṣatriyāḥ smṛtāḥ yājana adhyāpanaiḥ viprāḥ viśuddhaiḥ ca pratigrahaiḥ lokasya anugraha arthāya sthāpitāḥ brahmaṇā bhuvi kṛṣiḥ ca pāśupālyam ca viśām dānam ca sarvaśas brahma kṣatra viśām śūdrāḥ vihitāḥ paricārakāḥ brahma kṣatrasya vihitāḥ sūtāḥ vai paricārakāḥ na viṣ śūdrasya tatra eva śṛṇu vākyam mama anagha saḥ aham mūrdhāvasiktaḥ san rājarṣi kula saṃbhavaḥ mahā rathaḥ samākhyātaḥ sevyaḥ stavyaḥ ca bandinām saḥ aham etādṛśaḥ bhūtvā na iha ari kula mardana āpṛcchya tvā adya gāndhāre gamiṣyāmi yathāgatam evam uktvā nara vyāghraḥ śalyaḥ samiti śobhanaḥ utthāya prayayau tūrṇam rāja madhyāt amarṣitaḥ praṇayāt bahu mānāt ca tam nigṛhya sutaḥ tava abravīt madhuram vākyam sāma sarva artha sādhakam na hi madra īśvaraḥ rājā kuryāt yat anṛtam bhavet ṛtam eva hi pūrvāḥ te vahanti puruṣa uttamāḥ śalya bhūtaḥ ca śatrūṇām yasmāt tvam bhuvi mānada yat eva vyāhṛtam pūrvam bhavatā bhūri dakṣiṇa vṛṇīmaḥ tvām haya agryāṇām yantāram iti saṃyuge yathā hi abhyadhikam karṇam guṇaiḥ tāta dhanaṃjayāt bhavān api adhikaḥ kṛṣṇāt aśva yāne bale tathā yathā aśva hṛdayam veda vāsudevaḥ mahā manāḥ dviguṇam tvam tathā vettha madra rāja na saṃśayaḥ śalyaḥ uvāca viśiṣṭam devakīputrāt prītimān asmi aham tvayi eṣa sārathyam ātiṣṭhe rādheyasya yaśasvinaḥ yudhyataḥ pāṇḍava agryeṇa yathā tvam vīra manyase utsṛjeyam yathāśraddham aham vācaḥ asya saṃnidhau saṃjayaḥ uvāca bhūyas eva tu madra īśa yat te vakṣyāmi tat śṛṇu yat uktavān pituḥ mahyam mārkaṇḍeyaḥ mahān ṛṣiḥ tvam nibodha na ca api atra kartavyā te vicāraṇā devānām asurāṇām ca mahān āsīt samāgamaḥ babhūva prathamaḥ rājan saṃgrāmaḥ tārakā mayaḥ tārākṣaḥ kamalākṣaḥ ca vidyunmālī ca pārthiva tapasā karśayām āsuḥ dehān svān śatru tāpana teṣām pitāmahaḥ prītaḥ vara daḥ pradadau varān tān abravīt tadā devaḥ lokānām prabhuḥ īśvaraḥ varam anyam vṛṇīdhvam vai yādṛśam saṃprarocate tatas te sahitāḥ rājan saṃpradhārya asakṛt bahu asmākam tvam varam deva prayaccha imam pitāmaha vayam purāṇi trīṇi eva samāsthāya mahīm imām vicariṣyāma loke asmin tvad prasāda puraskṛtāḥ ekībhāvam gamiṣyanti purāṇi etāni ca anagha samāgatāni ca etāni yaḥ hanyāt bhagavan tadā eka iṣuṇā deva varaḥ sa naḥ mṛtyuḥ bhaviṣyati te tu labdha varāḥ prītāḥ saṃpradhārya parasparam viśvakarmāṇam ajaram daitya dānava pūjitam tatas mayaḥ sva tapasā cakre dhīmān purāṇi ha trīṇi kāñcanam ekam tu raupyam kārṣṇāyasam tathā kāñcanam divi tatra āsīt antarikṣe ca rājatam āyasam ca abhavat bhūmau cakra stham pṛthivīpate ekaikam yojana śatam vistāra āyāma saṃmitam gṛha aṭṭa aṭṭālaka yutam bṛhat prākāra toraṇam guṇa prasava saṃbādham a saṃbādham anāmayam prāsādaiḥ vividhaiḥ ca eva dvāraiḥ ca api upaśobhitam pureṣu ca abhavan rājan rājānaḥ vai pṛthak pṛthak kāñcanam tārakākṣasya citram āsīt mahātmanaḥ rājatam kamalākṣasya vidyunmālinaḥ āyasam trayaḥ te daitya rājānaḥ trīn lokān āśu tejasā ākramya tasthuḥ varṣāṇām pūgān nāma prajāpatiḥ teṣām dānava mukhyānām prayutāni arbudāni ca koṭyaḥ ca aprati vīrāṇām samājagmuḥ tatas tatas sarveṣām ca punar teṣām sarva yoga vahaḥ mayaḥ yaḥ hi yam manasā kāmam dadhyau tripura saṃśrayaḥ tasmai kāmam mayaḥ tam tam vidadhe māyayā tadā tārakākṣa sutaḥ ca āsīt hariḥ nāma mahā balaḥ sa tuṣṭam avṛṇot devam vāpī bhavatu naḥ pure śastraiḥ vinihatāḥ yatra kṣiptāḥ syuḥ balavattarāḥ sa tu labdhvā varam vīraḥ tārakākṣa sutaḥ hariḥ sasṛje tatra vāpīm tām mṛtānām jīvanīm prabho mṛtaḥ tasyām parikṣiptaḥ tādṛśena eva jajñivān tām prāpya traipura sthāḥ tu sarvān lokān babādhire mahatā tapasā siddhāḥ surāṇām bhaya vardhanāḥ nirhrīkāḥ saṃsthitim sarve sthāpitām samalūlupan vidrāvya sa gaṇān devān tatra tatra tadā tadā deva araṇyāni sarvāṇi priyāṇi ca divaukasām ṛṣīṇām āśramān puṇyān yūpān janapadān tathā vyanāśayanta maryādāḥ dānavāḥ duṣṭa cāriṇaḥ te devāḥ sahitāḥ sarve pitāmaham ariṃdama asurāḥ ca durātmānaḥ te ca api vibudha dviṣaḥ aparādhyanti satatam ye yuṣmān pīḍayanti uta aham hi tulyaḥ sarveṣām bhūtānām na atra saṃśayaḥ adhārmikāḥ tu hantavyāḥ iti aham prabravīmi vaḥ te yūyam sthāṇum īśānam jiṣṇum akliṣṭa kāriṇam yoddhāram vṛṇuta ādityāḥ sa tān hantā suretarān iti tasya vacaḥ śrutvā devāḥ śakra purogamāḥ brahmāṇam agratas kṛtvā vṛṣāṅkam śaraṇam yayuḥ tapaḥ param samātasthuḥ gṛṇantaḥ brahma śāśvatam ṛṣibhiḥ saha dharma jñāḥ bhavam sarva ātmanā gatāḥ sarva ātmānam mahātmānam yena āptam sarvam ātmanā yaḥ sāṃkhyam ātmanaḥ veda yasya ca ātmā vaśe sadā te tam dadṛśuḥ īśānam tejaḥ rāśim umāpatim ātmanaḥ pratirūpāṇi rūpāṇi atha mahātmani sarva bhūta mayam ca īśam tam ajam jagataḥ patim devāḥ brahmarṣayaḥ ca eva śirobhiḥ dharaṇīm gatāḥ tān svasti vākyena abhyarcya samutthāpya ca śaṃkaraḥ brūta brūta iti bhagavān smayamānaḥ abhyabhāṣata namaḥ stutāya stutyāya stūyamānāya mṛtyave vilohitāya rudrāya nīlagrīvāya śūline amoghāya mṛga akṣāya pravara āyudha yodhine durvāraṇāya śukrāya brahmaṇe brahmacāriṇe īśānāya aprameyāya niyantre carma vāsase kumāra pitre tryakṣāya pravara āyudha dhāriṇe prapanna ārti vināśāya brahma dviṣ saṃgha ghātine vanaspatīnām pataye narāṇām pataye namaḥ gavām ca pataye nityam yajñānām pataye namaḥ provāca vyetu vaḥ trāsaḥ brūta kim karavāṇi vaḥ satkṛtya śaṃkaram prāha brahmā loka hitam vacaḥ tava atisargāt deveśa prājāpatyam idam padam mayā adhitiṣṭhatā dattaḥ dānavebhyaḥ mahān varaḥ tān atikrānta maryādān na anyaḥ saṃhartum arhati tvām ṛte bhūta bhavya īśa tvam hi eṣām pratyariḥ vadhe sa tvam deva prapannānām yācatām ca divaukasām kuru prasādam deveśa dānavān jahi śūlabhṛt śrī bhagavān uvāca hantavyāḥ śatravaḥ sarve yuṣmākam iti me matiḥ te yūyam sahitāḥ sarve madīyena astra tejasā jayadhvam yudhi tān śatrūn saṃghātaḥ hi mahā balaḥ devāḥ ūcuḥ teṣām iti ha manyāmaḥ dṛṣṭa tejaḥ balāḥ hi te bhagavān uvāca vadhyāḥ te sarvatas pāpāḥ ye yuṣmāsu aparādhinaḥ mama tejaḥ bala ardhena sarvān tān ghnata śātravān devāḥ ūcuḥ sarveṣām naḥ bala ardhena tvam eva jahi śātravān mahādevaḥ iti khyātaḥ tadā prabhṛti śaṃkaraḥ haniṣyāmi rathena ājau tān ripūn vai divaukasaḥ paśyadhvam yāvat adya etān pātayāmi mahī tale devāḥ ūcuḥ tatas vibudha śārdūlāḥ tam ratham samakalpayan vandhuram pṛthivīm devīm viśāla pura mālinīm sa parvata vana dvīpām cakruḥ bhūta dharām tadā mandaram parvatam ca akṣam jaṅghāḥ tasya mahā nadīḥ diśaḥ ca pradiśaḥ ca eva parivāram rathasya hi anukarṣān grahān dīptān varūtham ca api tārakāḥ dharma artha kāma saṃyuktam triveṇum ca api bandhuram oṣadhīḥ vividhāḥ tatra nānā puṣpa phala udgamāḥ pakṣau pūrva aparau tatra kṛte rātri ahanī śubhe daśa nāga patīn īṣām dhṛtarāṣṭra mukhān dṛḍhām dyām yugam yugacarmāṇi saṃvartaka balāhakān śamyām dhṛtim ca medhām ca sthitim saṃnatim eva ca surā ambu preta vittānām patīn loka īśvarān hayān sinīvālīm anumatim kuhūm rākām ca suvratām yoktrāṇi cakruḥ vāhānām rohakān ca api kaṇṭhakam adhiṣṭhānam manaḥ tu āsīt parirathyam sarasvatī nānā varṇāḥ ca citrāḥ ca patākāḥ pavana īritāḥ ratha yaṣṭim viyat kṛṣṭām sthāpayām āsa go vṛṣam brahma daṇḍaḥ kāla daṇḍaḥ rudra daṇḍaḥ tathā jvaraḥ atharva aṅgirasau āstām cakrarakṣau mahātmanaḥ ṛgvedaḥ sāmavedaḥ ca purāṇam ca puraḥsarāḥ itihāsa yajurvedau pṛṣṭharakṣau babhūvatuḥ divyāḥ vācaḥ ca vidyāḥ ca paripārśva carāḥ kṛtāḥ oṃkāraḥ ca mukhe rājan ati śobhā karaḥ abhavat vicitram ṛtubhiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ kṛtvā saṃvatsaram dhanuḥ tasmāt nṝṇām kālarātriḥ jyā kṛtā dhanuṣaḥ ajarā iṣuḥ ca api abhavat viṣṇuḥ jvalanaḥ somaḥ eva ca agnīṣomau jagat kṛtsnam vaiṣṇavam ca ucyate jagat viṣṇuḥ ca ātmā bhagavataḥ bhavasya amita tejasaḥ sa nīlalohitaḥ dhūmraḥ kṛttivāsāḥ bhayaṃkaraḥ āditya ayuta saṃkāśaḥ tejaḥ jvālā vṛtaḥ jvalan duścyāvaḥ cyāvanaḥ jetā hantā brahma dviṣām haraḥ nityam trātā ca hantā ca dharma adharma āśritān janān vibhāti bhagavān sthāṇuḥ taiḥ eva ātma guṇaiḥ vṛtaḥ tasya aṅgāni samāśritya sthitam viśvam idam jagat jaṅgama ajaṅgamam rājan śuśubhe adbhuta darśanam dṛṣṭvā tu tam ratham divyam kavacī sa śarāsanī bāṇam ādatta tam divyam soma viṣṇu agni saṃbhavam tasya vājān tatas devāḥ cakrire vibhoḥ puṇya gandha vaham rājan śvasanam rāja sattama sa śobhamānaḥ vara daḥ khaḍgī bāṇī śarāsanī tam abruvan deva gaṇāḥ yam bhavān saṃniyokṣyate sa bhaviṣyati deveśa sārathiḥ te na saṃśayaḥ tān abravīt punar devaḥ mattaḥ śreṣṭhataraḥ hi yaḥ tam sārathim kurudhvam me svayam saṃcintya māciram etat śrutvā tatas devāḥ vākyam uktam mahātmanā tathā ca kṛtam asmābhiḥ prasannaḥ vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ sārathim tu na jānīmaḥ kaḥ syāt tasmin ratha uttame sa deva yuktaḥ ratha sattamaḥ naḥ durāvaraḥ drāvaṇaḥ śātravāṇām pinākapāṇiḥ vihitaḥ atra yoddhā vibhīṣayan dānavān udyataḥ asau nakṣatra vaṃśaḥ anugataḥ varūthe yasmin yoddhā sārathinā abhirakṣyaḥ tatra sārathiḥ eṣṭavyaḥ sarvaiḥ etaiḥ viśeṣavān kavacāni ca śastrāṇi kārmukam ca pitāmaha tvām ṛte sārathim tatra na anyam paśyāmahe vayam sārathye tūrṇam āroha saṃyaccha paramān hayān iti te śirasā natvā triloka īśam pitāmaham devāḥ prasādayām āsuḥ sārathyāya iti naḥ śrutam na atra kim cit mṛṣā vākyam yat uktam vaḥ divaukasaḥ tatas sa bhagavān devaḥ loka sraṣṭā pitāmahaḥ sārathye kalpitaḥ devaiḥ īśānasya mahātmanaḥ śirobhiḥ agaman tūrṇam te hayāḥ vāta raṃhasaḥ abhīśūn hi triloka īśaḥ saṃgṛhya prapitāmahaḥ tān aśvān codayām āsa manaḥ māruta raṃhasaḥ sādhu sādhu iti viśveśaḥ smayamānaḥ abhyabhāṣata yāhi deva yatas daityāḥ codaya aśvān atandritaḥ paśya bāhvoḥ balam me adya nighnataḥ śātravān raṇe tatas tān codayām āsa vāyu vega samān jave atha adhijyam dhanuḥ kṛtvā śarvaḥ saṃdhāya tam śaram yuktvā pāśupata astreṇa tripuram samacintayat purāṇi tāni kālena jagmuḥ eka tva tām tadā babhūva tumulaḥ harṣaḥ daivatānām mahātmanām tatas deva gaṇāḥ sarve siddhāḥ ca parama ṛṣayaḥ jaya iti vācaḥ mumucuḥ saṃstuvantaḥ mudā anvitāḥ tat sa asura gaṇam dagdhvā prākṣipat paścima arṇave evam tat tripuram dagdham dānavāḥ ca api aśeṣatas mā kārṣīḥ bhasmasāt lokān iti tryakṣaḥ abravīt ca tam tatas prakṛtim āpannāḥ devāḥ lokāḥ tathā ṛṣayaḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ vāgbhiḥ arthyābhiḥ sthāṇum apratima ojasam te anujñātāḥ bhagavatā jagmuḥ sarve yathāgatam kṛta kāmāḥ prasannena prajāpati mukhāḥ surāḥ yathā eva bhagavān brahmā loka dhātā pitāmahaḥ tvam hi kṛṣṇāt ca karṇāt ca phalgunāt ca viśeṣataḥ viśiṣṭaḥ rāja śārdūla nā asti tatra vicāraṇā tasmāt śaktau yuvām jetum mad śatrūn tau iva asurān yathā śalya adya karṇaḥ ayam śvetāśvam kṛṣṇa sārathim pramathya hanyāt kaunteyam tathā śīghram vidhīyatām tvayi karṇaḥ ca rājyam ca vayam ca eva pratiṣṭhitāḥ imam ca api aparam bhūyas itihāsam nibodha me pituḥ mama sakāśe yam brāhmaṇaḥ prāha dharma vid śrutvā ca etat vacaḥ citram hetu kārya artha saṃhitam kuru śalya viniścitya mā bhūt atra vicāraṇā bhārgavāṇām kule jātaḥ jamadagniḥ mahā tapāḥ tasya rāma iti vikhyātaḥ putraḥ tejaḥ guṇa anvitaḥ sa tīvram tapaḥ āsthāya prasādayitavān bhavam hṛdgatam ca asya vijñāya darśayām āsa śaṃkaraḥ īśvaraḥ uvāca kuruṣva pūtam ātmānam sarvam etat avāpsyasi dāsyāmi te tadā astrāṇi yadā pūtaḥ bhaviṣyasi pratyuvāca mahātmānam śirasā avanataḥ prabhum yadā jānāsi deveśa pātram mām astra dhāraṇe tadā śuśrūṣate astrāṇi bhavān me dātum arhati ārādhayitavān śarvam bahūn varṣa gaṇān tadā abravīt tasya bahuśas guṇān devyāḥ samīpatas bhaktimān eṣa satatam mayi rāmaḥ dṛḍha vrataḥ evam tasya guṇān prītaḥ bahuśas akathayat prabhuḥ devatānām pitṝṇām ca samakṣam ari sūdanaḥ etasmin eva kāle tu daityāḥ āsan mahā balāḥ tatas saṃbhūya vibudhāḥ tān hantum kṛta niścayāḥ prasādayantaḥ tam bhaktyā jahi śatru gaṇān iti pratijñāya tatas devaḥ devatānām ripu kṣayam rāmam bhārgavam āhūya saḥ abhyabhāṣata śaṃkaraḥ ripūn bhārgava devānām jahi sarvān samāgatān lokānām hita kāma artham mad prīti artham tathā eva ca rāmaḥ uvāca a kṛtāstrasya deveśa kā śaktiḥ me maheśvara nihantum dānavān sarvān kṛtāstrān yuddha durmadān īśvaraḥ uvāca vijitya ca ripūn sarvān guṇān prāpsyasi puṣkalān avadhīt deva śatrūn tān mada darpa bala anvitān vajra aśani sama sparśaiḥ prahāraiḥ eva bhārgavaḥ saṃspṛṣṭaḥ sthāṇunā sadyas nirvraṇaḥ samajāyata prītaḥ ca bhagavān devaḥ karmaṇā tena tasya vai varān prādāt brahma vide bhārgavāya mahātmane nipātāt tava śastrāṇām śarīre yā abhavat rujā tayā te mānuṣam karma vyapoḍham bhṛgu nandana gṛhāṇa astrāṇi divyāni mad sakāśāt yathā īpsitam tatas astrāṇi samastāni varān ca manasā īpsitān labdhvā bahuvidhān rāmaḥ praṇamya śirasā śivam anujñām prāpya deveśāt jagāma sa mahā tapāḥ evam etat purāvṛttam tadā kathitavān ṛṣiḥ karṇāya puruṣa vyāghra su prītena antarātmanā na asmai hi astrāṇi divyāni prādāsyat bhṛgunandanaḥ nā api sūta kule jātam karṇam manye katham cana sa kuṇḍalam sa kavacam dīrgha bāhum mahā ratham katham āditya sadṛśam mṛgī vyāghram janiṣyati vakṣaḥ paśya viśālam ca sarva śatru nibarhaṇam saṃjayaḥ uvāca tatas śalyaḥ pariṣvajya sutam te vākyam abravīt yat tu karṇam aham brūyām hita kāmaḥ priya apriyam mama tat kṣamatām sarvam bhavān karṇaḥ ca sarvaśas karṇaḥ uvāca īśānasya yathā brahmā yathā pārthasya keśavaḥ śalyaḥ uvāca ātma nindā ātma pūjā ca para nindā para stavaḥ an ācaritam āryāṇām vṛttam etat caturvidham a pramāda prayogāt ca jñāna vidyā cikitsitaiḥ ayam te karṇa sārathyam madra rājaḥ kariṣyati kṛṣṇāt abhyadhikaḥ yantā devendrasya iva mātaliḥ yathā hari hayaiḥ yuktam saṃgṛhṇāti sa mātaliḥ śalyaḥ tava tathā adya ayam saṃyantā ratha vājinām ratha śreṣṭhaḥ dhruvam saṃkhye pārthaḥ nā abhibhaviṣyati saṃjayaḥ uvāca uvāca rājan saṃgrāme saṃyacchantam haya uttamān tam ratham rathinām śreṣṭhaḥ karṇaḥ abhyarcya yathāvidhi saṃpāditam brahma vidā pūrvam eva purodhasā kṛtvā pradakṣiṇam yatnāt upasthāya ca bhāskaram samīpa stham madra rājam samāropayat agratas āruroha mahā tejāḥ śalyaḥ siṃhaḥ iva acalam tatas śalya āsthitam rājan karṇaḥ sva ratham uttamam adhyatiṣṭhat yathā ambhodam vidyutvantam divākaraḥ tau eka ratham ārūḍhau āditya agni sama tviṣau vyabhrājetām yathā megham sūrya agnī sahitau divi saṃstūyamānau tau vīrau tadā āstām dyutimattarau ṛtvij sadasyaiḥ indra agnī hūyamānau iva adhvare sa śalya saṃgṛhīta aśve rathe karṇaḥ sthitaḥ abhavat āsthitaḥ sa ratha śreṣṭham karṇaḥ śara gabhastimān tam ratha stham mahā vīram yāntam ca amita tejasam a kṛtam droṇa bhīṣmābhyām duṣkaram karma saṃyuge kuruṣva adhirathe vīra miṣatām sarva dhanvinām manogatam mama hi āsīt bhīṣma droṇau mahā rathau tābhyām yat akṛtam vīra vīra karma mahā mṛdhe gṛhāṇa dharmarājam vā jahi vā tvam dhanaṃjayam bhīmasenam ca rādheya mādrī putrau yamau api pāṇḍu putrasya sainyāni kuru sarvāṇi bhasmasāt tatas tūrya sahasrāṇi bherīṇām ayutāni ca vādyamānāni arocanta megha śabdāḥ yathā divi abhyabhāṣata rādheyaḥ śalyam yuddha viśāradam codaya aśvān mahā bāho yāvat dhanmi dhanaṃjayam bhīmasenam yamau ca ubhau rājānam ca yudhiṣṭhiram adya paśyatu me śalya bāhu vīryam dhanaṃjayaḥ asyataḥ kaṅka patrāṇām sahasrāṇi śatāni ca adya kṣepsyāmi aham śalya śarān parama tejanān pāṇḍavānām vināśāya duryodhana jayāya ca śalyaḥ uvāca sūtaputra katham nu tvam pāṇḍavān avamanyase sarva astra jñān mahā iṣvāsān sarvān eva mahā rathān api saṃjanayeyuḥ ye bhayam sākṣāt śatakratoḥ yadā śroṣyasi nirghoṣam visphūrjitam iva aśaneḥ rādheya gāṇḍivasya ājau tadā nā evam vadiṣyasi saṃjayaḥ uvāca an ādṛtya tu tat vākyam madra rājena bhāṣitam dṛṣṭvā karṇam mahā iṣvāsam yuyutsum samavasthitam cukruśuḥ kuravaḥ sarve hṛṣṭa rūpāḥ paraṃtapa tatas dundubhi ghoṣeṇa bherīṇām ninadena ca niścarantaḥ vyadṛśyanta sūryāt sapta mahā grahāḥ ulkā pātaḥ ca saṃjajñe diśām dāhaḥ tathā eva ca tathā aśanyaḥ ca saṃpetuḥ vavuḥ vātāḥ ca dāruṇāḥ mṛga pakṣi gaṇāḥ ca eva bahuśas pṛtanām tava aśrūṇi ca vyamuñcanta vāhanāni viśām pate samutpetuḥ vināśāya kauravāṇām su dāruṇāḥ na ca tān gaṇayām āsuḥ sarve te daiva mohitāḥ nirjitān pāṇḍavān ca eva menire tava kauravāḥ tatas ratha sthaḥ para vīra hantā bhīṣma droṇau ātta vīryau nirīkṣya sa śalyam ābhāṣya jagāda vākyam pārthasya karma apratimam ca dṛṣṭvā na aham mahā indrāt api vajrapāṇeḥ kruddhāt bibhemi ātta dhanūḥ ratha sthaḥ dṛṣṭvā tu bhīṣma pramukhān śayānān na tu eva mām sthira tā saṃjahāti samīkṣya saṃkhye ati balān narādhipaiḥ nara aśva mātaṅga rathān śaraiḥ hatān katham na sarvān ahitān raṇe avadhīt mahā astra vid brāhmaṇa puṃgavaḥ guruḥ śikṣā prasādaḥ ca balam dhṛtiḥ ca droṇe mahā astrāṇi ca saṃnatiḥ ca sa ced agāt mṛtyu vaśam mahātmā sarvān anyān āturān adya manye na nūnam astrāṇi balam parākramaḥ kriyā su nītam parama āyudhāni vā hutāśana āditya samāna tejasam parākrame viṣṇu puraṃdara upamam saṃprakruṣṭe rudita strī kumāre parābhūte pauruṣe dhārtarāṣṭre mayā kṛtyam iti jānāmi śalya prayāhi tasmāt dviṣatām anīkam yatra rājā pāṇḍavaḥ satya saṃdhaḥ vyavasthitaḥ bhīmasena arjunau ca vāsudevaḥ sṛñjayāḥ sātyakiḥ ca yamau ca kaḥ tau viṣahet mat anyaḥ tasmāt kṣipram madra pate prayāhi raṇe pāñcālān pāṇḍavān sṛñjayān ca tān vā haniṣyāmi sametya saṃkhye yāsyāmi vā droṇa mukhāya manye na tu eva aham na gamiṣyāmi madhyam teṣām śūrāṇām iti mā śalya viddhi mitra drohaḥ marṣaṇīyaḥ na me ayam tyaktvā prāṇān anuyāsyāmi droṇam prājñasya mūḍhasya ca jīvita ante atas vidvan abhiyāsyāmi pārtham diṣṭam na śakyam vyativartitum vai kalyāṇa vṛttaḥ satatam hi rājan vaicitravīryasya sutaḥ mama āsīt vaiyāghra carmāṇam a kūjana akṣam haima tri kośam rajata triveṇum dhanūṃṣi citrāṇi nirīkṣya śalya dhvajam gadām sāyakān ca ugra rūpān asim ca dīptam parama āyudham ca śaṅkham ca śubhram svanavantam ugram patākinam vajra nipāta nisvanam sita aśva yuktam śubha tūṇa śobhitam imam samāsthāya ratham ratha ṛṣabham raṇe haniṣyāmi aham arjunam balāt tam vā haniṣyāmi sametya yuddhe yāsyāmi vā bhīṣma mukhaḥ yamāya asura sura mahā uragān narān garuḍa piśāca sa yakṣa rākṣasān smarasi nanu yadā paraiḥ hṛtaḥ sa ca dhṛtarāṣṭra sutaḥ vimokṣitaḥ smarasi nanu yadā pramocitāḥ khacara gaṇān avajitya pāṇḍavaiḥ samudita bala vāhanāḥ punar puruṣa vareṇa jitāḥ stha gograhe sa guru guru sutāḥ sa bhīṣmakāḥ kim u na jitaḥ sa tadā tvayā arjunaḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca bhṛśam ati ruṣitaḥ param vṛṣaḥ kuru pṛtanā patiḥ āha madrapam yāhi madra īśa ca api enam karṇaḥ prāha yuyutsayā sa rathaḥ prayayau śatrūn śveta aśvaḥ śalya sārathiḥ tatas prāyāt prītimān vai rathena vaiyāghreṇa śveta yujā atha karṇaḥ sa ca ālokya dhvajinīm pāṇḍavānām dhanaṃjayam tvarayā paryapṛcchat saṃjayaḥ uvāca eva tadā karṇaḥ harṣayan vāhinīm tava ekaikam samare dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavam paryapṛcchata yaḥ mama adya mahātmānam darśayet śvetavāhanam śakaṭam ratna saṃpūrṇam yaḥ me brūyāt dhanaṃjayam anyam tasmai punar dadyām sauvarṇam hasti ṣaḍgavam tathā tasmai punar dadyām strīṇām śatam alaṃkṛtam śyāmānām niṣka kaṇṭhīnām gīta vādya vipaścitām anyam tasmai varam dadyām śvetān pañcaśatān hayān hema bhāṇḍa paricchannān su mṛṣṭa maṇi kuṇḍalān su dāntān api ca eva aham dadyām aṣṭaśatān parān ratham ca śubhram sauvarṇam dadyām tasmai su alaṃkṛtam anyam tasmai varam dadyām kuñjarāṇām śatāni ṣaḍ kāñcanaiḥ vividhaiḥ bhāṇḍaiḥ ācchannān hema mālinaḥ utpannān aparānteṣu vinītān hasti śikṣakaiḥ putra dārān vihārān ca yat anyat vittam asti me hatvā ca sahitau kṛṣṇau tayoḥ vittāni sarvaśas etāḥ vācaḥ su bahuśas karṇaḥ uccārayan yudhi dadhmau sāgara saṃbhūtam su svanam śaṅkham uttamam tāḥ vācaḥ sūtaputrasya tathā yuktāḥ niśamya tu duryodhanaḥ mahā rāja prahṛṣṭaḥ sa anugaḥ abhavat tatas dundubhi nirghoṣaḥ mṛdaṅgānām ca sarvaśas siṃhanādaḥ sa vāditraḥ kuñjarāṇām ca nisvanaḥ prādurāsīt tadā rājan tvad sainye bharata ṛṣabha yodhānām saṃprahṛṣṭānām tathā samabhavat svanaḥ tathā prahṛṣṭe sainye tu plavamānam mahā ratham mā sūtaputra mānena sauvarṇam hasti ṣaḍgavam bālyāt iva tvam tyajasi vasu vaiśravaṇaḥ yathā parāsṛjasi mithyā kim kim ca tvam bahu mūḍha vat apātra dāne ye doṣāḥ tān mohāt na avabudhyase śakyam bahuvidhaiḥ yajñaiḥ yaṣṭum sūta yajasva taiḥ yat ca prārthayase hantum kṛṣṇau mohāt mṛṣā eva tat na hi śuśruma saṃmarde kroṣṭrā siṃhau nipātitau ye tvām na vārayanti āśu prapatantam hutāśane kāla kāryam na jānīṣe kāla pakvaḥ asi asaṃśayam bahu abaddham akarṇīyam kaḥ hi brūyāt jijīviṣuḥ samudra taraṇam dorbhyām kaṇṭhe baddhvā yathā śilām giri agrāt vā nipatanam tādṛś tava cikīrṣitam sahitaḥ sarva yodhaiḥ tvam vyūḍha anīkaiḥ su rakṣitaḥ hita artham dhārtarāṣṭrasya bravīmi tvā na hiṃsayā karṇaḥ uvāca sva vīrye aham parāśvasya prārthayāmi arjunam raṇe tvam tu mitra mukhaḥ śatruḥ mām bhīṣayitum icchasi saṃjayaḥ uvāca iti karṇasya vākya ante śalyaḥ prāha uttaram vacaḥ cukopayiṣuḥ atyartham karṇam madra īśvaraḥ punar yadā vai tvām phalguna vega nunnāḥ jyā coditāḥ hastavatā visṛṣṭāḥ anvetāraḥ kaṅka patrāḥ śita agrāḥ tadā tapsyasi arjunasya abhiyogāt yadā divyam dhanuḥ ādāya pārthaḥ prabhāsayan pṛtanām savyasācī tvām ardayeta niśitaiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ tadā paścāt tapsyase sūtaputra bālaḥ candram mātuḥ aṅke śayānaḥ yathā kaḥ cit prārthayate apahartum triśūlam āśliṣya su tīkṣṇa dhāram sarvāṇi gātrāṇi nigharṣasi tvam su tīkṣṇa dhārā upama karmaṇā tvam yuyutsase yaḥ arjunena adya karṇa siddham siṃham kesariṇam bṛhantam bālaḥ mūḍhaḥ kṣudra mṛgaḥ tarasvī mā sūtaputra āhvaya rāja putram mahā vīryam kesariṇam yathā eva vane sṛgālaḥ piśitasya tṛptaḥ mā pārtham āsādya vinaṅkṣyasi tvam īṣā dantam mahā nāgam prabhinna karaṭāmukham śaśaka āhvayase yuddhe karṇa pārtham dhanaṃjayam bila stham kṛṣṇa sarpam tvam bālyāt kāṣṭhena vidhyasi mahā viṣam pūrṇa kośam yat pārtham yoddhum icchasi sṛgālaḥ iva mūḍha tvāt nṛ siṃham karṇa pāṇḍavam suparṇam pataga śreṣṭham vainateyam tarasvinam laṭvā iva āhvayase pāte karṇa pārtham dhanaṃjayam sarva ambhaḥ nilayam bhīmam ūrmimantam jhaṣa ayutam ṛṣabham dundubhi grīvam tīkṣṇa śṛṅgam prahāriṇam mahā ghoṣam mahā megham darduraḥ pratinardasi yathā ca sva gṛha sthaḥ śvā vyāghram vana gatam bhaṣet tathā tvam bhaṣase karṇa nara vyāghram dhanaṃjayam sṛgālaḥ api vane karṇa śaśaiḥ parivṛtaḥ vasan manyate siṃham ātmānam yāvat siṃham na paśyati apaśyan śatru damanam nara vyāghram dhanaṃjayam vyāghram tvam manyase ātmānam yāvat kṛṣṇau na paśyasi yāvat gāṇḍīva nirghoṣam na śṛṇoṣi mahā āhave ratha śabda dhanuḥ śabdaiḥ nādayantam diśaḥ daśa nardantam iva śārdūlam dṛṣṭvā kroṣṭā bhaviṣyasi nityam eva sṛgālaḥ tvam nityam siṃhaḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ vīra pradveṣaṇāt mūḍha nityam kroṣṭā iva lakṣyase yathā ākhuḥ syāt biḍālaḥ ca śvā vyāghraḥ ca bala abale yathā sṛgālaḥ siṃhaḥ ca yathā ca śaśa kuñjarau yathā anṛtam ca satyam ca yathā ca api viṣa amṛte tathā tvam api pārthaḥ ca prakhyātau ātma karmabhiḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca adhikṣiptaḥ tu rādheyaḥ śalyena amita tejasā guṇān guṇavataḥ śalya guṇavān vetti na aguṇaḥ tvam tu nityam guṇaiḥ hīnaḥ kim jñāsyasi aguṇaḥ guṇān arjunasya mahā astrāṇi krodham vīryam dhanuḥ śarān aham śalya abhijānāmi na tvam jānāsi tat tathā evam eva ātmanaḥ vīryam aham vīryam ca pāṇḍave asti ca ayam iṣuḥ śalya su puṅkhaḥ rakta bhojanaḥ eka tūṇī śayaḥ patrī su dhautaḥ samalaṃkṛtaḥ śete candana pūrṇena pūjitaḥ bahulāḥ samāḥ āheyaḥ viṣavān ugraḥ nara aśva dvipa saṃgha hā eka vīraḥ mahā raudraḥ tanutra asthi vidāraṇaḥ nirbhindyām yena ruṣṭaḥ aham api merum mahā girim kṛṣṇāt vā devakīputrāt satyam ca atra śṛṇuṣva me tena aham iṣuṇā śalya vāsudeva dhanaṃjayau sarveṣām vāsudevānām kṛṣṇe lakṣmīḥ pratiṣṭhitā sarveṣām pāṇḍu putrāṇām jayaḥ pārthe pratiṣṭhitaḥ mām ekam abhisaṃyātau sujātam śalya paśya me pitṛṣvasā mātula jau bhrātarau a parājitau maṇī sūtre iva protau draṣṭāsi nihatau mayā arjune gāṇḍivam kṛṣṇe cakram tārkṣya kapidhvajau bhīrūṇām trāsa jananau śalya harṣa karau mama tvam tu duṣprakṛtiḥ mūḍhaḥ mahā yuddheṣu akovidaḥ bhaya avatīrṇaḥ saṃtrāsāt abaddham bahu bhāṣase saṃstauṣi tvam tu kena api hetunā tau ku deśa ja pāpa deśa ja durbuddhe kṣudra kṣatriya pāṃsana suhṛd bhūtvā ripuḥ kim mām kṛṣṇābhyām bhīṣayan asi na aham bibhemi kṛṣṇābhyām vijānan ātmanaḥ balam vāsudeva sahasram vā phalgunānām śatāni ca striyaḥ bālāḥ ca vṛddhāḥ ca prāyas krīḍā gatāḥ janāḥ yāḥ gāthāḥ saṃpragāyanti kurvantaḥ adhyayanam yathā tāḥ gāthāḥ śṛṇu me śalya madrakeṣu durātmasu brāhmaṇaiḥ kathitāḥ pūrvam yathāvat rāja saṃnidhau śrutvā ca ekamanāḥ mūḍha kṣama vā brūhi vā uttaram madrake saṃgatam na asti kṣudra vākye nara adhame durātmā madrakaḥ nityam nityam ca anṛtikaḥ anṛjuḥ yāvadantam hi daurātmyam madrakeṣu iti naḥ śrutam pitā mātā ca putraḥ ca śvaśrū śvaśura mātulāḥ jāmātā duhitā bhrātā naptā te te ca bāndhavāḥ vayasya abhyāgatāḥ ca anye dāsī dāsam ca saṃgatam puṃbhiḥ vimiśrāḥ nāryaḥ ca jñāta ajñātāḥ svayā icchayā yeṣām gṛheṣu śiṣṭānām saktu mantha āśinām sadā pītvā sīdhum sa go māṃsam nardanti ca hasanti ca nā api vairam na sauhārdam madrakeṣu samācaret madrakeṣu ca duḥsparśam śaucam gāndhārakeṣu ca rāja yājaka yājyena naṣṭam dattam haviḥ bhavet śūdra saṃskārakaḥ vipraḥ yathā yāti parābhavam madrake saṃgatam nā asti hatam vṛścikataḥ viṣam ātharvaṇena mantreṇa sarvā śāntiḥ kṛtā bhavet iti vṛścika daṣṭasya nānā viṣa hatasya ca kurvanti bheṣajam prājñāḥ satyam tat ca api dṛśyate evam vidvan joṣam āssva śṛṇu ca atra uttaram vacaḥ vāsāṃsi utsṛjya nṛtyanti striyaḥ yāḥ madya mohitāḥ mithune a saṃyatāḥ ca api yathā kāma carāḥ ca tāḥ yāḥ tiṣṭhantyaḥ pramehanti yathā eva uṣṭrī daśerake tāsām vibhraṣṭa lajjānām nirlajjānām tatas tatas tvam putraḥ tādṛśīnām hi dharmam vaktum iha icchasi su vīrakam yācyamānā madrakā kaṣati sphijau a dātu kāmā vacanam idam vadati dāruṇam mā mā su vīrakam kaḥ cit yācatām dayitaḥ mama putram dadyām pratipadam na tu dadyām su vīrakam nāryaḥ bṛhatyaḥ nirhrīkāḥ madrakāḥ kambala āvṛtāḥ ghasmarāḥ naṣṭa śaucāḥ ca prāyas iti anuśuśruma evamādi mayā anyaiḥ vā śakyam vaktum bhavet bahu ā keśa agrāt nakha agrāt ca vaktavyeṣu ku vartmasu madrakāḥ sindhusauvīrāḥ dharmam vidyuḥ katham tu iha pāpa deśa udbhavāḥ mlecchāḥ dharmāṇām a vicakṣaṇāḥ yat ājau nihataḥ śete sadbhiḥ samabhipūjitaḥ āyudhānām saṃparāye yat mucyeyam aham tatas saḥ aham priyaḥ sakhā ca asmi dhārtarāṣṭrasya dhīmataḥ vyaktam tvam api upahitaḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ pāpa deśa ja kāmam na khalu śakyaḥ aham tvadvidhānām śataiḥ api saṃgrāmāt vimukhaḥ kartum dharma jñaḥ iva nāstikaiḥ sāraṅgaḥ iva gharma ārtaḥ kāmam vilapa śuṣya ca na aham bhīṣayitum śakyaḥ kṣatra vṛtte vyavasthitaḥ tanutyajām nṛsiṃhānām āhaveṣu anivartinām yā gatiḥ guruṇā prāk me proktā rāmeṇa tām smara sveṣām trāṇa artham udyuktam vadhāya dviṣatām api na tat bhūtam prapaśyāmi triṣu lokeṣu madraka yaḥ mām asmāt abhiprāyāt vārayet iti me matiḥ evam vidvan joṣam āssva trāsāt kim bahu bhāṣase mā tvā hatvā pradāsyāmi kravyādbhyaḥ madraka adhama mitra pratīkṣayā śalya dhārtarāṣṭrasya ca ubhayoḥ punar ced īdṛśam vākyam madra rāja vadiṣyasi śiraḥ te pātayiṣyāmi gadayā vajra kalpayā śrotāraḥ tu idam adyā iha draṣṭāraḥ vā ku deśa ja karṇam vā jaghnatuḥ kṛṣṇau karṇaḥ vā api jaghāna tau evam uktvā tu rādheyaḥ punar eva viśām pate abravīt madra rājānam yāhi yāhi iti asaṃbhramam saṃjayaḥ uvāca māriṣa ādhiratheḥ śrutvā vacaḥ yuddha abhinandinaḥ śalyaḥ abravīt punar karṇam nidarśanam udāharan tathā aham tvām pramādyantam cikitsāmi suhṛd tayā imām kāka upamām karṇa procyamānām nibodha me śrutvā yatheṣṭam kuryāḥ tvam vihīna kula pāṃsana na aham ātmani kim cit vai kilbiṣam karṇa saṃsmare yena tvam mām mahā bāho hantum icchasi anāgasam avaśyam tu mayā vācyam budhyatām yadi te hitam viśeṣataḥ ratha sthena rājñaḥ ca eva hita eṣiṇā śramaḥ khedaḥ ca satatam hayānām rathinā saha āyudhasya parijñānam rutam ca mṛga pakṣiṇām bhāraḥ ca api atibhāraḥ ca śalyānām ca pratikriyā sarvam etat mayā jñeyam rathasya asya kuṭumbinā atas tvām kathaye karṇa nidarśanam idam punar yajvā dānapatiḥ kṣāntaḥ sva karma sthaḥ abhavat śuciḥ rājñaḥ dharma pradhānasya rāṣṭre vasati nirbhayaḥ putrāṇām tasya bālānām kumārāṇām yaśasvinām kākaḥ bahūnām abhavat ucciṣṭa kṛta bhojanaḥ tasmai sadā prayacchanti vaiśya putrāḥ kumārakāḥ māṃsodanam dadhi kṣīram pāyasam madhu sarpiṣī sa ca ucchiṣṭa bhṛtaḥ kākaḥ vaiśya putraiḥ kumārakaiḥ sadṛśān pakṣiṇaḥ dṛptaḥ śreyasaḥ ca avamanyate atha haṃsāḥ samudra ante kadā cit abhipātinaḥ garuḍasya gatau tulyāḥ cakrāṅgāḥ hṛṣṭa cetasaḥ kumārakāḥ tatas haṃsān dṛṣṭvā kākam atha abruvan tān saḥ abhipatya jijñāsuḥ kaḥ eṣām śreṣṭha bhāj iti ucchiṣṭa darpitaḥ kākaḥ bahūnām dūra pātinām teṣām yam pravaram mene haṃsānām dūra pātinām tat śrutvā prāhasan haṃsāḥ ye tatra āsan samāgatāḥ bhāṣataḥ bahu kākasya balinaḥ patatām varāḥ idam ūcuḥ ca cakrāṅgāḥ vacaḥ kākam vihaṃgamāḥ vayam haṃsāḥ carāma imām pṛthivīm mānasa okasaḥ pakṣiṇām ca vayam nityam dūra pātena pūjitāḥ katham nu haṃsam balinam vajra aṅgam dūra pātinam katham tvam patanam kāka saha asmābhiḥ bravīṣi tat atha haṃsa vacaḥ mūḍhaḥ kutsayitvā punar punar prajagāda uttaram kākaḥ katthanaḥ jāti lāghavāt śatam ekam ca pātānām patitāsmi na saṃśayaḥ uḍḍīnam avaḍīnam ca praḍīnam ḍīnam eva ca niḍīnam atha saṃḍīnam tiryak ca atigatāni ca viḍīnam pariḍīnam ca parāḍīnam suḍīnakam atiḍīnam mahāḍīnam niḍīnam pariḍīnakam gata āgata pratigatāḥ bahvīḥ ca nikuḍīnikāḥ uvāca haṃsaḥ tam kākam vacanam tat nibodha me śatam ekam ca pātānām tvam kāka patitā dhruvam ekam eva tu ye pātam viduḥ sarve vihaṃgamāḥ tam aham patitā kāka na anyam jānāmi kam cana atha kākāḥ prajahasuḥ ye tatra āsan samāgatāḥ katham ekena pātena haṃsaḥ pāta śatam jayet haṃsasya patitam kākaḥ balavān āśu vikramaḥ eka pātī ca cakrāṅgaḥ kākaḥ pāta śatena ca petivān atha cakrāṅgaḥ petivān atha vāyasaḥ visismāpayiṣuḥ pātaiḥ ācakṣāṇaḥ ātmanaḥ kriyām atha kākasya citrāṇi patitāni itarāṇi ca dṛṣṭvā pramuditāḥ kākāḥ vineduḥ atha taiḥ svaraiḥ haṃsān ca avahasanti sma prāvadan apriyāṇi ca kurvāṇāḥ vividhān rāvān āśaṃsantaḥ tadā jayam pratyahīyata kākāt ca muhūrtam iva māriṣa atha haṃsaḥ sa tat śrutvā prāpatat paścimām diśam tatas bhīḥ prāviśat kākam tadā tatra vicetasam dvīpa drumān a paśyantam nipatantam śrama anvitam nipateyam kva nu śrāntaḥ iti tasmin jala arṇave mahā bhūta śata udbhāsī nabhasaḥ api viśiṣyate gāmbhīryāt hi samudrasya na viśeṣaḥ kula adhama diś ambara ambhasām karṇa samudra sthāḥ hi durjayāḥ vidūra pātāt toyasya kim punar karṇa vāyasaḥ avekṣamāṇaḥ tam kākam na aśaknot vyapasarpitum atikramya ca cakrāṅgaḥ kākam tam samudaikṣata tam tathā hīyamānam ca haṃsaḥ dṛṣṭvā abravīt idam bahūni patanāni tvam ācakṣāṇaḥ muhur muhur patasi a vyāharan ca idam na naḥ guhyam prabhāṣase kim nāma patanam kāka yat tvam patasi sāṃpratam jalam spṛśasi pakṣābhyām tuṇḍena ca punar punar sa pakṣābhyām spṛśan ārtaḥ tuṇḍena jalam arṇave kākaḥ dṛḍham pariśrāntaḥ sahasā nipapāta ha haṃsaḥ uvāca śatam ekam ca pātānām yat prabhāṣasi vāyasa nānāvidhāni iha purā tat ca anṛtam iha adya te kākaḥ uvāca avamanya bahūn ca aham kākān anyān ca pakṣiṇaḥ prāṇaiḥ haṃsa prapadye tvām dvīpa antam prāpayasva mām yadi aham svastimān haṃsa sva deśam prāpnuyām punar kāka kāka iti vāśantam nimajjantam mahā arṇave padbhyām utkṣipya vepantam pṛṣṭham āropayat śanais āropya pṛṣṭham kākam tam haṃsaḥ karṇa vicetasam ājagāma punar dvīpam spardhayā petatuḥ yatas saṃsthāpya tam ca api punar samāśvāsya ca khecaram gataḥ yathā īpsitam deśam haṃsaḥ manaḥ iva āśu gaḥ ucchiṣṭa bhojanāt kākaḥ yathā vaiśya kule tu saḥ evam tvam ucchiṣṭa bhṛtaḥ dhārtarāṣṭraiḥ na saṃśayaḥ sadṛśān śreyasaḥ ca api sarvān karṇa atimanyase droṇa drauṇi kṛpaiḥ guptaḥ bhīṣmeṇa anyaiḥ ca kauravaiḥ virāṭa nagare pārtham ekam kim na avadhīḥ tadā yatra vyastāḥ samastāḥ ca nirjitāḥ stha kirīṭinā sṛgālāḥ iva siṃhena kva te vīryam abhūt tadā bhrātaram ca hatam dṛṣṭvā nirjitaḥ savyasācinā paśyatām kuru vīrāṇām prathamam tvam palāyathāḥ kurūn samagrān utsṛjya prathamam tvam palāyathāḥ hatvā jitvā ca gandharvān citrasena mukhān raṇe punar prabhāvaḥ pārthasya purāṇaḥ keśavasya ca kathitaḥ karṇa rāmeṇa sabhāyām rāja saṃsadi satatam ca tat aśrauṣīḥ vacanam droṇa bhīṣmayoḥ avadhyau vadatoḥ kṛṣṇau saṃnidhau vai mahīkṣitām putram ca vasudevasya pāṇḍavam ca dhanaṃjayam prakāśena abhivikhyātau tvam tu khadyota vat nṛṣu evam vidvān mā avamaṃsthāḥ sūtaputra acyuta arjunau nṛ siṃhau tau nara śvā tvam joṣam āssva vikatthana saṃjayaḥ uvāca śaure ratham vāhayataḥ arjunasya balam mahā astrāṇi ca pāṇḍavasya aham vijānāmi yathāvat adya parokṣa bhūtam tava tat tu śalya tau ca apradhṛṣyau śastrabhṛtām variṣṭhau vyapeta bhīḥ yodhayiṣyāmi kṛṣṇau saṃtāpayati abhyadhikam tu rāmāt chāpaḥ adya mām brāhmaṇa sattamāt ca avātsam vai brāhmaṇa chadmanā aham rāme purā divyam astram cikīrṣuḥ pṛṣṭaḥ ca aham tam avocam mahā ṛṣim sūtaḥ aham asmi iti sa mām śaśāpa sūta upadhau āptam idam tvayā astram na karma kāle pratibhāsyati tvām pramuñcantam bāṇa saṃghān amoghān marma chidaḥ vīra haṇaḥ sa patrān śara oghiṇam pārthivān majjayantam velā iva pārtham iṣubhiḥ saṃsahiṣye atimānī pāṇḍavaḥ yuddha kāmaḥ amānuṣaiḥ eṣyati me mahā astraiḥ divākareṇa api samam tapantam samāpta raśmim yaśasā jvalantam tamonudam meghaḥ iva atimātraḥ dhanaṃjayam chādayiṣyāmi bāṇaiḥ vaiśvānaram dhūma śikham jvalantam tejasvinam lokam imam dahantam meghaḥ bhūtvā śara varṣaiḥ yathā agnim tathā pārtham śamayiṣyāmi yuddhe pramāthinam balavantam prahāriṇam prabhañjanam mātariśvānam ugram yuddhe sahiṣye himavān iva acalaḥ dhanaṃjayam kruddham amṛṣyamāṇam viśāradam ratha mārgeṣu asaktam dhuryam nityam samareṣu pravīram loke varam sarva dhanurdharāṇām dhanaṃjayam saṃyuge saṃsahiṣye sarvām imām yaḥ pṛthivīm saheta tathā vidvān yotsyamānaḥ asmi tena yaḥ sarva bhūtāni sa devakāni prasthe ajayat khāṇḍave savyasācī kaḥ jīvitam rakṣamāṇaḥ hi tena yuyutsate mām ṛte mānuṣaḥ anyaḥ aham tasya pauruṣam pāṇḍavasya kim tvam mūrkhaḥ prabhaṣan mūḍha cetāḥ mām avocaḥ pauruṣam arjunasya apriyaḥ yaḥ paruṣaḥ niṣṭhuraḥ hi kṣudraḥ kṣeptā kṣamiṇaḥ ca a kṣamāvān hanyām aham tādṛśānām śatāni kṣamāmi tvām kṣamayā kāla yogāt avocaḥ tvam pāṇḍava arthe apriyāṇi pradharṣayan mām mūḍha vat pāpa karman śatruḥ śadeḥ śāsateḥ śāyateḥ vā śṛṇāteḥ vā śvayateḥ vā api sarge duryodhana artham tava ca apriya artham yaśaḥ ṛtham ātma artham api īśvara artham astrāṇi paśya adya mama uttamāni brāhmāṇi divyāni atha mānuṣāṇi āsādayiṣyāmi aham ugra vīryam dvipa uttamam mattam iva abhimattaḥ astram brāhmam manasā tat hi ajayyam kṣepsye pārthāya apratimam jayāya vaivasvatāt daṇḍa hastāt varuṇāt vā api pāśinaḥ sa gadāt vā dhanapateḥ sa vajrāt vā api vāsavāt na anyasmāt api kasmāt cit bibhimaḥ hi ātatāyinaḥ iti śalya vijānīhi yathā na aham bibhemi abhīḥ tasmāt bhayam na me pārthāt nā api ca eva janārdanāt adya yuddham hi tābhyām me saṃparāye bhaviṣyati tasmāt bibhemi balavat brāhmaṇa vyāhṛtāt aham ete hi soma rājānaḥ īśvarāḥ sukha duḥkhayoḥ īṣā dantān saptaśatān dāsī dāsa śatāni ca kṛṣṇānām śveta vatsānām sahasrāṇi caturdaśa tatas abravīt mām yācantam aparāddham prayatnataḥ vyāhṛtam yat mayā sūta tat tathā na tat anyathā anṛta uktam prajāḥ hanyāt tatas pāpam avāpnuyāt tasmāt dharma abhirakṣā artham na anṛtam vaktum utsahe mā tvam brahma gatim hiṃsyāḥ prāyaścittam kṛtam tvayā mad vākyam na anṛtam loke kaḥ cit kuryāt samāpnuhi iti etat te mayā proktam kṣiptena api suhṛd tayā jānāmi tvā adhikṣipantam joṣam āssva uttaram śṛṇu saṃjayaḥ uvāca abhyabhāṣata rādheyaḥ saṃnivārya uttaram vacaḥ yat tvam nidarśana artham mām śalya jalpitavān asi na aham śakyaḥ tvayā vācā vibhīṣayitum āhave yadi mām devatāḥ sarvāḥ yodhayeyuḥ sa vāsavāḥ tathā api me bhayam na syāt kim u pārthāt sa keśavāt na aham bhīṣayitum śakyaḥ vāc mātreṇa katham cana anyam jānīhi yaḥ śakyaḥ tvayā bhīṣayitum raṇe nīcasya balam etāvat pāruṣyam yat tvam āttha mām na hi karṇaḥ samudbhūtaḥ bhaya artham iha māriṣa idam tu me tvam ekāgraḥ śṛṇu madra janādhipa saṃnidhau dhṛtarāṣṭrasya procyamānam mayā śrutam deśān ca vividhān citrān pūrva vṛttān ca pārthivān brāhmaṇāḥ kathayantaḥ sma dhṛtarāṣṭram upāsate tatra vṛddhaḥ purāvṛttāḥ kathāḥ kāḥ cit dvijottamaḥ vāhlīka deśam madrān ca kutsayan vākyam abravīt bahiṣkṛtāḥ himavatā gaṅgayā ca tiraskṛtāḥ pañcānām sindhu ṣaṣṭhānām nadīnām ye antar āśritāḥ tān dharma bāhyān aśucīn vāhlīkān parivarjayet govardhanaḥ nāma vaṭaḥ subhāṇḍam nāma catvaram etat rāja kula dvāram ā kumāraḥ smarāmi aham kāryeṇa atyartha gāḍhena vāhlīkeṣu uṣitam mayā tatas eṣām samācāraḥ saṃvāsāt viditaḥ mama śākalam nāma nagaram āpagā nāma nimnagā jartikāḥ nāma bāhlīkāḥ teṣām vṛttam su ninditam dhānā gauḍa āsave pītvā go māṃsam laśunaiḥ saha apūpa māṃsa vāṭyānām āśinaḥ śīla varjitāḥ nagara āgāra vapreṣu bahis mālya anulepanāḥ āhuḥ anyonyam uktāni prabruvāṇāḥ mada utkaṭāḥ ākrośantyaḥ pranṛtyanti mandāḥ parvasu a saṃyatāḥ teṣām kila avaliptānām nivasan kurujāṅgale kaḥ cit vāhlīka mukhyānām na ati hṛṣṭa manāḥ jagau sā nūnam bṛhatī gaurī sūkṣma kambala vāsinī mām anusmaratī śete vāhlīkam kuru vāsinam śatadruka nadīm tīrtvā tām ca ramyām irāvatīm gatvā sva deśam drakṣyāmi sthūla śaṅkhāḥ śubhāḥ striyaḥ manaḥśilā ujjvala apāṅgāḥ gauryaḥ trikakud āñjanāḥ kevala ajina saṃvītāḥ kūrdantyaḥ priya darśanāḥ mṛdaṅga ānaka śaṅkhānām mardalānām ca nisvanaiḥ khara uṣṭra aśvataraiḥ ca eva mattāḥ yāsyāmahe sukham śamī pīlu karīrāṇām vaneṣu sukha vartmasu apūpān saktu piṇḍīḥ ca khādantaḥ mathita anvitāḥ pathiṣu prabalāḥ bhūtvā kadāsam ṛdite adhvani khala upahāram kurvāṇāḥ tāḍayiṣyāma bhūyasaḥ evam hīneṣu vrātyeṣu vāhlīkeṣu durātmasu īdṛśāḥ brāhmaṇena uktāḥ vāhlīkāḥ mogha cāriṇaḥ yeṣām ṣaṣ bhāga hartā tvam ubhayoḥ śubha pāpayoḥ iti uktvā brāhmaṇaḥ sādhuḥ uttaram punar uktavān vāhlīkeṣu avinīteṣu procyamānam nibodhata tatra sma rākṣasī gāti sadā kṛṣṇa caturdaśīm kadā vā ghoṣikāḥ gāthāḥ punar gāsyanti śākale gavyasya tṛptāḥ māṃsasya pītvā gauḍam mahā āsavam gaurībhiḥ saha nārībhiḥ bṛhatībhiḥ su alaṃkṛtāḥ palāṇḍu gaṇḍūṣa yutān khādante ca eḍakān bahūn vārāham kaukkuṭam māṃsam gavyam gārdabham auṣṭrakam aiḍam ca ye na khādanti teṣām janma nirarthakam iti gāyanti ye mattāḥ śīdhunā śākalāvataḥ sa bāla vṛddhāḥ kūrdantaḥ teṣu vṛttam katham bhavet śatadruḥ ca vipāśā ca tṛtīyā irāvatī tathā candrabhāgā vitastā ca sindhu ṣaṣṭhāḥ bahis gatāḥ āraṭṭāḥ nāma te deśāḥ naṣṭa dharmāt na tān vrajet vrātyānām dāsamīyānām videhānām ayajvanām na devāḥ pratigṛhṇanti pitaraḥ brāhmaṇāḥ tathā teṣām pranaṣṭa dharmāṇām bāhlīkānām iti śrutiḥ brāhmaṇena tathā proktam viduṣā sādhu saṃsadi kāṣṭha kuṇḍeṣu vāhlīkāḥ mṛṇmayeṣu ca bhuñjate saktu vāṭya avalipteṣu śva ādi līḍheṣu nirghṛṇāḥ āvikam ca auṣṭrikam ca eva kṣīram gārdabham eva ca tad vikārān ca vāhlīkāḥ khādanti ca pibanti ca putra saṃkariṇaḥ jālmāḥ sarva anna kṣīra bhojanāḥ āraṭṭāḥ nāma vāhlīkāḥ varjanīyāḥ vipaścitā āraṭṭāḥ nāma vāhlīkāḥ na teṣu āryaḥ dvi aham vaset bahis ca nāma hlīkaḥ ca vipāśāyām piśācakau tayoḥ apatyam bāhlīkāḥ na eṣā sṛṣṭiḥ prajāpateḥ kāraskarān mahiṣakān kaliṅgān kīkaṭa aṭavīn karkoṭakān vīrakān ca durdharmān ca vivarjayet iti tīrtha anusartāram rākṣasī kā cit abravīt eka rātrā śamīgehe mahā ulūkhala mekhalā āraṭṭāḥ nāma te deśāḥ bāhlīkāḥ nāma te janāḥ vasāti sindhusauvīrāḥ iti prāyas vikutsitāḥ ucyamānam mayā samyak tat ekāgra manāḥ śṛṇu ācāram tatra saṃprekṣya prītaḥ śilpinam abravīt mayā himavataḥ śṛṅgam ekena adhyuṣitam ciram dṛṣṭāḥ ca bahavaḥ deśāḥ nānā dharma samākulāḥ aṭatā tu sadā deśān nānā dharma samākulān āgacchatā mahā rāja vāhlīkeṣu niśāmitam vaiśyaḥ śūdraḥ ca bāhlīkaḥ tatas bhavati nāpitaḥ nāpitaḥ ca tatas bhūtvā punar bhavati brāhmaṇaḥ bhavati ekaḥ kule vipraḥ śiṣṭān ye kāma cāriṇaḥ gāndhārāḥ madrakāḥ ca eva vāhlīkāḥ ke api acetasaḥ kṛtsnām aṭitvā pṛthivīm vāhlīkeṣu viparyayaḥ yat api anyaḥ abravīt vākyam vāhlīkānām vikutsitam satī purā hṛtā kā cit āraṭṭā kila dasyubhiḥ adharmataḥ ca upayātā sā tān abhyaśapat tatas bālām bandhumatīm yat mām adharmeṇa upagacchatha na ca eva asmāt pramokṣyadhvam ghorāt pāpāt nara adhamāḥ kuravaḥ saha pāñcālāḥ śālvāḥ matsyāḥ sa naimiṣāḥ kosalāḥ kāśayaḥ aṅgāḥ ca kaliṅgāḥ magadhāḥ tathā cedayaḥ ca mahābhāgāḥ dharmam jānanti śāśvatam nānā deśeṣu santaḥ ca prāyas bāhyāḥ layāt ṛte ā matsyebhyaḥ kuru pāñcāla deśyāḥ ā naimiṣāt cedayaḥ ye viśiṣṭāḥ dharmam purāṇam upajīvanti santaḥ madrān ṛte pañcanadān ca jihmān evam vidvan dharma kathān ca rājan tūṣṇīṃbhūtaḥ jaḍa vat śalya bhūyāḥ tvam tasya goptā ca janasya rājā ṣaṣ bhāga hartā śubha duṣkṛtasya atha vā duṣkṛtasya tvam hartā teṣām arakṣitā rakṣitā puṇya bhāj rājā prajānām tvam tu apuṇya bhāj pūjyamāne purā dharme sarva deśeṣu śāśvate dharmam pāñcanadam dṛṣṭvā dhik iti āha pitāmahaḥ vrātyānām dāśamīyānām kṛte api aśubha karmaṇām kalmāṣapādaḥ sarasi nimajjan rākṣasaḥ abravīt kṣatriyasya malam bhaikṣam brāhmaṇasya anṛtam malam malam pṛthivyāḥ vāhlīkāḥ strīṇām madra striyaḥ malam nimajjamānam uddhṛtya kaḥ cit rājā niśācaram mānuṣāṇām malam mlecchāḥ mlecchānām mauṣṭikāḥ malam mauṣṭikānām malam śaṇḍāḥ śaṇḍānām rājayājakāḥ rāja yājaka yājyānām madrakāṇām ca yat malam iti rakṣa upasṛṣṭeṣu viṣa vīrya hateṣu ca rākṣasam bheṣajam proktam saṃsiddham vacana uttaram brāhmam pāñcālāḥ kauraveyāḥ svadharmaḥ satyam matsyāḥ śūrasenāḥ ca yajñaḥ prācyāḥ dāsāḥ vṛṣalāḥ dākṣiṇātyāḥ stenāḥ bāhlīkāḥ saṃkarāḥ vai surāṣṭrāḥ kṛtaghna tā para vitta apahāraḥ surā pānam guru dāra avamarśaḥ yeṣām dharmaḥ tān prati na asti adharma ā pāñcālebhyaḥ kuravaḥ naimiṣāḥ ca matsyāḥ ca eva api atha jānanti dharmam kaliṅgakāḥ ca āṅgakāḥ māgadhāḥ ca prācīm diśam śritāḥ devāḥ jātavedaḥ purogamāḥ dakṣiṇām pitaraḥ guptām yamena śubha karmaṇā pratīcīm varuṇaḥ pāti pālayan asurān balī udīcīm bhagavān somaḥ brahmaṇyaḥ brāhmaṇaiḥ saha rakṣaḥ piśācān himavān guhyakān gandhamādanaḥ dhruvaḥ sarvāṇi bhūtāni viṣṇuḥ lokān janārdanaḥ iṅgita jñāḥ ca magadhāḥ prekṣita jñāḥ ca kosalāḥ ardhoktāḥ kuru pāñcālāḥ śālvāḥ kṛtsna anuśāsanāḥ pārvatīyāḥ ca viṣamāḥ yathā eva girayaḥ tathā sarva jñāḥ yavanāḥ rājan śūrāḥ ca eva viśeṣataḥ mlecchāḥ sva saṃjñā niyatāḥ na anuktaḥ itaraḥ janaḥ pratirabdhāḥ tu vāhlīkāḥ na ca ke cana madrakāḥ sa tvam etādṛśaḥ śalya na uttaram vaktum arhasi etat jñātvā joṣam āssva pratīpam mā sma vai kṛthāḥ sa tvām pūrvam aham hatvā haniṣye keśava arjunau śalyaḥ uvāca āturāṇām parityāgaḥ sva dāra suta vikrayaḥ aṅgeṣu vartate karṇa yeṣām adhipatiḥ bhavān ratha atiratha saṃkhyāyām yat tvā bhīṣmaḥ tadā bravīt sarvatra brāhmaṇāḥ santi santi sarvatra kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ śūdrāḥ tathā karṇa striyaḥ sādhvyaḥ ca suvratāḥ ramante ca upahāsena puruṣāḥ puruṣaiḥ saha ātma vācyam na jānīte jānan api vimuhyati saṃjayaḥ uvāca saṃjayaḥ uvāca tatas para anīka bhidam vyūham apratimam paraiḥ samīkṣya karṇaḥ pārthānām dhṛṣṭadyumna abhirakṣitam vāditrāṇām ca ninadaiḥ kampayan iva medinīm vepamānaḥ iva krodhāt yuddha śauṇḍaḥ paraṃtapaḥ vyadhamat pāṇḍavīm senām āsurīm maghavān iva dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca katham saṃjaya rādheyaḥ pratyavyūhata pāṇḍavān dhṛṣṭadyumna mukhān vīrān bhīmasena abhirakṣitān pravibhajya yathānyāyam katham vā samavasthitāḥ katham pāṇḍu sutāḥ ca api pratyavyūhanta māmakān sarva bhūtāni yaḥ hi ekaḥ khāṇḍave jitavān purā saṃjayaḥ uvāca śṛṇu vyūhasya racanām arjunaḥ ca yathā gataḥ paridāya nṛpam tebhyaḥ saṃgrāmaḥ ca abhavat yathā kṛpaḥ śāradvataḥ rājan māgadhaḥ ca tarasvinaḥ sātvataḥ kṛtavarmā ca dakṣiṇam pakṣam āśritāḥ teṣām prapakṣe śakuniḥ ulūkaḥ ca mahā rathaḥ sādibhiḥ vimala prāsaiḥ tava anīkam arakṣatām gāndhāribhiḥ asaṃbhrāntaiḥ pārvatīyaiḥ ca durjayaiḥ śalabhānām iva vrātaiḥ piśācaiḥ iva durdṛśaiḥ catustriṃśat sahasrāṇi rathānām anivartinām saṃśaptakāḥ yuddha śauṇḍāḥ vāmam pārśvam apālayan samuccitāḥ tava sutaiḥ kṛṣṇa arjuna jighāṃsavaḥ teṣām prapakṣaḥ kāmbojāḥ śakāḥ ca yavanaiḥ saha nideśāt sūtaputrasya sa rathāḥ sa aśva pattayaḥ āhvayantaḥ arjunam tasthuḥ keśavam ca mahā balam madhye senā mukham karṇaḥ vyavātiṣṭhata daṃśitaḥ rakṣyamāṇaḥ su saṃrabdhaiḥ putraiḥ śastrabhṛtām varaḥ vāhinī pramukham vīraḥ saṃprakarṣan aśobhata ayaḥ ratniḥ mahā bāhuḥ sūrya vaiśvānara dyutiḥ duḥśāsanaḥ vṛtaḥ sainyaiḥ sthitaḥ vyūhasya pṛṣṭhatas tam anvayāt mahā rāja svayam duryodhanaḥ nṛpaḥ citra aśvaiḥ citra saṃnāhaiḥ sodaryaiḥ abhirakṣitaḥ rakṣyamāṇaḥ mahā vīryaiḥ sahitaiḥ madra kekayaiḥ aśvatthāmā kurūṇām ca ye pravīrāḥ mahā rathāḥ nitya mattāḥ ca mātaṅgāḥ śūraiḥ mlecchaiḥ adhiṣṭhitāḥ anvayuḥ tat ratha anīkam kṣarantaḥ iva toyadāḥ sādibhiḥ ca āsthitāḥ rejuḥ drumavantaḥ iva acalāḥ teṣām padāti nāgānām pādarakṣāḥ sahasraśas paṭṭiśa asi dharāḥ śūrāḥ babhūvuḥ anivartinaḥ sādibhiḥ syandanaiḥ nāgaiḥ adhikam samalaṃkṛtaiḥ nṛtyati iva mahā vyūhaḥ pareṣām ādadhat bhayam patti aśva ratha mātaṅgāḥ prāvṛṣi iva balāhakāḥ tatas senā mukhe karṇam dṛṣṭvā rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ paśya arjuna mahā vyūham karṇena vihitam raṇe yuktam pakṣaiḥ prapakṣaiḥ ca senā anīkam prakāśate yathā na abhibhavati asmān tathā nītiḥ vidhīyatām evam uktaḥ arjunaḥ rājñā prāñjaliḥ nṛpam abravīt yathā bhavān āha tathā tat sarvam na tat anyathā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca duḥśāsanam śatānīkaḥ hārdikyam śini puṃgavaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ tathā drauṇim svayam yāsyāmi aham kṛpam draupadeyāḥ dhārtarāṣṭrān śiṣṭān saha śikhaṇḍinā te te ca tān tān ahitān asmākam ghnantu māmakāḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca vyādideśa sva sainyāni svayam ca agāt camū mukham atha tam ratham āyāntam dṛṣṭvā ati adbhuta darśanam ayam sa rathaḥ āyāti śveta aśvaḥ kṛṣṇa sārathiḥ eṣa reṇuḥ samudbhūtaḥ divam āvṛtya tiṣṭhati pravāti eṣa mahā vāyuḥ abhitas tava vāhinīm paśya karṇa mahā ghoram bhaya dam loma harṣaṇam kabandham megha saṃkāśam bhānum āvṛtya saṃsthitam paśya yūthaiḥ bahuvidhaiḥ mṛgāṇām sarvatodiśam balibhiḥ dṛpta śārdūlaiḥ ādityaḥ abhinirīkṣyate paśya kaṅkān ca gṛdhrān ca samavetān sahasraśas sitāḥ ca aśvāḥ samāyuktāḥ tava karṇa mahā rathe udīryataḥ hayān paśya mahā kāyān mahā javān plavamānān darśanīyān ākāśe garuḍān iva dhruvam eṣu nimitteṣu bhūmim āvṛtya pārthivāḥ svapsyanti nihatāḥ karṇa śataśas atha sahasraśas śaṅkhānām tumulaḥ śabdaḥ śrūyate loma harṣaṇaḥ ānakānām ca rādheya mṛdaṅgānām ca sarvaśas bāṇa śabdān bahuvidhān nara aśva ratha nisvanān jyā talatra iṣu śabdān ca śṛṇu karṇa mahātmanām hema rūpya pramṛṣṭānām vāsasām śilpi nirmitāḥ nānā varṇāḥ rathe bhānti śvasanena prakampitāḥ sa hema candra tārā arkāḥ patākāḥ kiṅkiṇī yutāḥ paśya karṇa arjunasya etāḥ saudāminyaḥ iva ambude dhvajāḥ kaṇakaṇāyante vātena abhisamīritāḥ sa patākāḥ rathāḥ ca api pāñcālānām mahātmanām nāga aśva ratha pattyā oghān tāvakān samabhighnataḥ dhvaja agram dṛśyate tu asya jyā śabdaḥ ca api śrūyate adya draṣṭāsi tam vīram śvetāśvam kṛṣṇasārathim nighnantam śātravān saṃkhye yam karṇa paripṛcchasi sārathiḥ yasya vārṣṇeyaḥ gāṇḍīvam yasya kārmukam tam ced hantāsi rādheya tvam naḥ rājā bhaviṣyasi eṣa saṃśaptaka āhūtaḥ tān eva abhimukhaḥ gataḥ karoti kadanam ca eṣām saṃgrāme dviṣatām balī iti bruvāṇam madra īśam karṇaḥ prāha ati manyumān eṣa sūryaḥ iva ambhodaiḥ channaḥ pārthaḥ na dṛśyate śalyaḥ uvāca kaḥ vā anilam nigṛhṇīyāt pibet vā kaḥ mahā arṇavam bāhubhyām uddharet bhūmim dahet kruddhaḥ imāḥ prajāḥ paśya kuntī sutam vīram bhīmam akliṣṭa kāriṇam prabhāsantam mahā bāhum sthitam merum iva acalam eṣa bhīmaḥ jaya prepsuḥ yudhi tiṣṭhati vīryavān eṣa dharma bhṛtām śreṣṭhaḥ dharmarājaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ tiṣṭhati asukaraḥ saṃkhye paraiḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ dṛśyante ete kārṣṇeyāḥ pañca pañca acalāḥ iva ete drupada putrāḥ ca dhṛṣṭadyumna purogamāḥ hīnāḥ satyajitā vīrāḥ tiṣṭhanti parama ojasaḥ te sene samasajjetām gaṅgā yamunā vat bhṛśam dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca tathā vyūḍheṣu anīkeṣu saṃsakteṣu ca saṃjaya saṃśaptakān katham pārthaḥ gataḥ karṇaḥ ca pāṇḍavān na hi tṛpyāmi vīrāṇām śṛṇvānaḥ vikramān raṇe saṃjayaḥ uvāca pārṣataḥ prababhau dhanvī kālaḥ vigrahavān iva sa anugāḥ bhīma vapuṣaḥ candram tārā gaṇāḥ iva atha vyūḍheṣu anīkeṣu prekṣya saṃśaptakān raṇe kruddhaḥ arjunaḥ abhidudrāva vyākṣipan gāṇḍivam dhanuḥ atha saṃśaptakāḥ pārtham abhyadhāvan vadha eṣiṇaḥ vijaye kṛta saṃkalpāḥ mṛtyum kṛtvā nivartanam sa saṃprahāraḥ tumulaḥ teṣām āsīt kirīṭinā tasya eva naḥ śrutaḥ yādṛś nivāta kavacaiḥ saha rathān aśvān dhvajān nāgān pattīn rathapatīn api iṣūn dhanūṃṣi khaḍgān ca cakrāṇi ca paraśvadhān sa āyudhān udyatān bāhūn udyatāni āyudhāni ca ciccheda dviṣatām pārthaḥ śirāṃsi ca sahasraśas nimagnam tam ratham matvā neduḥ saṃśaptakāḥ mudā sa purastāt arīn hatvā paśca ardhena uttareṇa ca dakṣiṇena ca bībhatsuḥ kruddhaḥ rudraḥ paśūn iva atha pāñcāla cedīnām sṛñjayānām ca māriṣa tvadīyaiḥ saha saṃgrāmaḥ āsīt parama dāruṇaḥ kṛpaḥ ca kṛtavarmā ca śakuniḥ ca api saubalaḥ hṛṣṭa senāḥ su saṃrabdhāḥ ratha anīkaiḥ prahāriṇaḥ kosalaiḥ kāśi matsyaiḥ ca kārūṣaiḥ kekayaiḥ api śūrasenaiḥ śūravīraiḥ yuyudhuḥ yuddha durmadāḥ teṣām anta karam yuddham deha pāpma praṇāśanam śūdra viś kṣatra vīrāṇām dharmyam svargyam yaśaskaram guptaḥ kuru pravīraiḥ ca madrāṇām ca mahā rathaiḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha pāñcālaiḥ cedibhiḥ sātyakena ca yudhyamānam raṇe karṇam kuru vīraḥ abhyapālayat karṇaḥ api niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ vinihatya mahā camūm pramṛdya ca ratha śreṣṭhān yudhiṣṭhiram apīḍayat vipatra āyudha deha asūn kṛtvā śatrūn sahasraśas dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca yat tat praviśya pārthānām senām kurvan jana kṣayam ke ca pravīrāḥ pārthānām yudhi karṇam avārayan kān ca pramathya ādhirathiḥ yudhiṣṭhiram apīḍayat saṃjayaḥ uvāca dhṛṣṭadyumna mukhān pārthān dṛṣṭvā karṇaḥ vyavasthitān samabhyadhāvat tvaritaḥ pāñcālān śatru karśanaḥ tam tūrṇam abhidhāvantam pāñcālāḥ jita kāśinaḥ pratyudyayuḥ mahā rāja haṃsāḥ iva mahā arṇavam tatas śaṅkha sahasrāṇām nisvanaḥ hṛdayaṃgamaḥ prādurāsīt ubhayatas bherī śabdaḥ ca dāruṇaḥ nānā vāditra nādaḥ ca dvipa aśva ratha nisvanaḥ siṃhanādaḥ ca vīrāṇām abhavat dāruṇaḥ tadā sa adri druma arṇavā bhūmiḥ sa vāta ambudam ambaram sa arka indu graha nakṣatrā dyauḥ ca vyaktam vyaghūrṇata ati bhūtāni tam śabdam menire ati ca vivyathuḥ yāni ca aplava sattvāni prāyas tāni mṛtāni ca atha karṇaḥ bhṛśam kruddhaḥ śīghram astram udīrayan jaghāna pāṇḍavīm senām āsurīm maghavān iva sa pāṇḍava rathān tūrṇam praviśya visṛjan śarān tatas su puṅkhaiḥ niśitaiḥ ratha śreṣṭhaḥ ratheṣubhiḥ avadhīt pañcaviṃśatyā pāñcālān pañcaviṃśatim suvarṇa puṅkhaiḥ nārācaiḥ para kāya vidāraṇaiḥ cedikān avadhīt vīraḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas tam tathā samare karma kurvāṇam ati mānuṣam parivavruḥ mahā rāja pāñcālānām ratha vrajāḥ tatas saṃdhāya viśikhān pañca bhārata duḥsahān pāñcālān avadhīt pañca karṇaḥ vaikartanaḥ vṛṣaḥ bhānudevam citrasenam senābindum ca bhārata tapanam śūrasenam ca pāñcālān avadhīt raṇe pāñcāleṣu ca śūreṣu vadhyamāneṣu sāyakaiḥ hāhākāraḥ mahān āsīt pāñcālānām mahā āhave teṣām saṃkīryamāṇānām hāhākāra kṛtāḥ diśaḥ punar eva ca tān karṇaḥ jaghāna āśu patatribhiḥ suṣeṇaḥ satyasenaḥ ca tyaktvā prāṇān ayudhyatām pṛṣṭhagopaḥ tu karṇasya jyeṣṭhaḥ putraḥ mahā rathaḥ vṛṣasenaḥ svayam karṇam pṛṣṭhatas paryapālayat dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ sātyakiḥ ca draupadeyāḥ vṛkodaraḥ janamejayaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca pravīrāḥ ca prabhadrakāḥ cedi kekaya pāñcālāḥ yamau matsyāḥ ca daṃśitāḥ samabhyadhāvan rādheyam jighāṃsantaḥ prahāriṇaḥ te enam vividhaiḥ śastraiḥ śara dhārābhiḥ eva ca abhyavarṣan vimṛdnantaḥ prāvṛṣi iva ambudāḥ girim pitaram tu parīpsantaḥ karṇa putrāḥ prahāriṇaḥ tvadīyāḥ ca apare rājan vīrāḥ vīrān avārayan nārācaiḥ saptabhiḥ viddhvā hṛdi bhīmam nanāda ha athā anyat dhanuḥ ādāya su dṛḍham bhīma vikramaḥ sajyam vṛkodaraḥ kṛtvā suṣeṇasya ācchinat dhanuḥ karṇam ca tūrṇam vivyādha trisaptatyā śitaiḥ śaraiḥ satyasenam ca daśabhiḥ sa aśva sūta dhvaja āyudham paśyatām suhṛdām madhye karṇa putram apātayat śubha darśanam eva āsīt nāla bhraṣṭam iva ambujam hatvā karṇa sutam bhīmaḥ tāvakān punar ārdayat kṛpa hārdikyayoḥ chittvā cāpe tau api athā ārdayat duḥśāsanam tribhiḥ viddhvā śakunim ṣaḍbhiḥ āyasaiḥ suṣeṇāya asṛjat bhīmaḥ tam api asya ācchinat vṛṣaḥ punar karṇaḥ trisaptatyā bhīmasenam ratheṣubhiḥ putram parīpsan vivyādha krūram krūraiḥ jighāṃsayā nakulaḥ tam tu viṃśatyā viddhvā bhāra sahaiḥ dṛḍhaiḥ tam suṣeṇaḥ mahā rāja viddhvā daśabhiḥ āśugaiḥ ciccheda ca dhanuḥ śīghram kṣurapreṇa mahā rathaḥ suṣeṇam bahubhiḥ bāṇaiḥ vārayām āsa saṃyuge sa tu bāṇaiḥ diśaḥ rājan ācchādya para vīra hā ājaghne sārathim ca asya suṣeṇam ca tatas tribhiḥ athā anyat dhanuḥ ādāya suṣeṇaḥ krodha mūrchitaḥ avidhyat nakulam ṣaṣṭyā sahadevam ca saptabhiḥ sātyakiḥ vṛṣasenasya hatvā sūtam tribhiḥ śaraiḥ dhanuḥ ciccheda bhallena jaghāna aśvān ca saptabhiḥ atho jighāṃsuḥ śaineyam khaḍga carma bhṛt abhyayāt tasya ca āplavataḥ śīghram vṛṣasenasya sātyakiḥ duḥśāsanaḥ tu tam dṛṣṭvā viratham vyāyudham kṛtam atha anyam ratham āsthāya vṛṣasenaḥ mahā rathaḥ karṇasya yudhi durdharṣaḥ punar pṛṣṭham apālayat duḥśāsanam tu śaineyaḥ navaiḥ navabhiḥ āśugaiḥ visūta aśva ratham kṛtvā lalāṭe tribhiḥ ārpayat yuyudhe pāṇḍubhiḥ sārdham karṇasya āpyāyayan balam dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ tatas karṇam avidhyat daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ bhīmasenaḥ catuḥṣaṣṭyā sahadevaḥ ca pañcabhiḥ nakulaḥ triṃśatā bāṇaiḥ śatānīkaḥ ca saptabhiḥ śikhaṇḍī daśabhiḥ vīraḥ dharmarājaḥ śatena tu ete ca anye ca rāja indra pravīrāḥ jaya gṛddhinaḥ abhyardayat mahā iṣvāsam sūtaputram mahā mṛdhe tān sūtaputraḥ viśikhaiḥ daśabhiḥ daśabhiḥ śitaiḥ tatra astra vīryam karṇasya lāghavam ca mahātmanaḥ na hi ādadānam dadṛśuḥ saṃdadhānam ca sāyakān vimuñcantam ca saṃrambhāt dadṛśuḥ te mahā ratham dyauḥ viyat bhūḥ diśaḥ ca āśu praṇunnāḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ aruṇa abhra āvṛta ākāram tasmin deśe babhau viyat nṛtyan iva hi rādheyaḥ cāpa hastaḥ pratāpavān tān pramṛdnan mahā iṣvāsān rādheyaḥ śara vṛṣṭibhiḥ rāja anīkam asaṃbādham prāviśat śatru karśanaḥ sa rathān tri śatān hatvā cedīnām anivartinām tatas te pāṇḍavāḥ rājan śikhaṇḍī ca sa sātyakiḥ rādheyāt parirakṣantaḥ rājānam paryavārayan tathā eva tāvakāḥ sarve karṇam durvāraṇam raṇe yattāḥ senā mahā iṣvāsāḥ paryarakṣanta sarvaśas nānā vāditra ghoṣāḥ ca prādurāsan viśām pate siṃhanādaḥ ca saṃjajñe śūrāṇām anivartinām tatas punar samājagmuḥ abhītāḥ kuru pāṇḍavāḥ yudhiṣṭhira mukhāḥ pārthāḥ sūtaputra mukhāḥ vayam saṃjayaḥ uvāca vidārya karṇaḥ tām senām dharmarājam upādravat ratha hasti aśva pattīnām sahasraiḥ parivāritaḥ nānā āyudha sahasrāṇi preṣitāni aribhiḥ vṛṣaḥ chittvā bāṇa śataiḥ ugraiḥ tān avidhyat asaṃbhramaḥ nicakarta śirāṃsi eṣām bāhūn ūrūn ca sarvaśas te hatāḥ vasudhām petuḥ bhagnāḥ ca anye vidudruvuḥ draviḍa andhra niṣādāḥ tu punar sātyaki coditāḥ abhyardayan jighāṃsantaḥ pattayaḥ karṇam āhave te vibāhu śirastrāṇāḥ prahatāḥ karṇa sāyakaiḥ petuḥ pṛthivyām yugapad chinnam śāla vanam yathā evam yodha śatāni ājau sahasrāṇi ayutāni ca hatāni iyuḥ mahīm dehaiḥ yaśasā apūrayan diśaḥ rurudhuḥ pāṇḍu pāñcālāḥ vyādhim mantra auṣadhaiḥ iva sa rāja gṛddhibhiḥ ruddhaḥ pāṇḍu pāñcāla kekayaiḥ nā aśakat tān atikrāntum mṛtyuḥ brahma vidaḥ yathā tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ karṇam adūra stham nivāritam karṇa karṇa vṛthādṛṣṭe sūtaputra vacaḥ śṛṇu tathā asmān bādhase nityam dhārtarāṣṭra mate sthitaḥ yat balam yat ca te vīryam pradveṣaḥ yaḥ ca pāṇḍuṣu tat sarvam darśayasva adya pauruṣam mahat āsthitaḥ yuddha śraddhām sa te adya aham vineṣyāmi mahā āhave evam uktvā mahā rāja karṇam pāṇḍu sutaḥ tadā suvarṇa puṅkhaiḥ daśabhiḥ vivyādha ayasmayaiḥ śitaiḥ tatas kṣurābhyām pāñcālyau cakrarakṣau mahātmanaḥ jaghāna samare śūraḥ śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ ratha abhyāśe cakāśete candrasya iva punarvasū yudhiṣṭhiraḥ punar karṇam avidhyat triṃśatā śaraiḥ bhittvā bhallena rājānam viddhvā ṣaṣṭyā anadat mudā tatas pravīrāḥ pāṇḍūnām abhyadhāvan yudhiṣṭhiram sūtaputrāt parīpsantaḥ karṇam abhyardayan śaraiḥ sātyakiḥ cekitānaḥ ca yuyutsuḥ pāṇḍyaḥ eva ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca draupadeyāḥ prabhadrakāḥ yamau ca bhīmasenaḥ ca śiśupālasya ca ātmajaḥ kārūṣāḥ matsya śeṣāḥ ca kekayāḥ kāśi kosalāḥ ete ca tvaritāḥ vīrāḥ vasuṣeṇam avārayan janamejayaḥ ca pāñcālyaḥ karṇam vivyādha sāyakaiḥ varāhakarṇaiḥ nārācaiḥ nālīkaiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ vatsadantaiḥ vipāṭhaiḥ ca kṣurapraiḥ caṭakā mukhaiḥ nānā praharaṇaiḥ ca ugraiḥ ratha hasti aśva sādinaḥ sarvatas abhyādravan karṇam parivārya jighāṃsayā sa pāṇḍavānām pravaraiḥ sarvatas samabhidrutaḥ udairayat brāhmam astram śaraiḥ saṃpūrayan diśaḥ tatas śara mahā jvālaḥ vīrya ūṣmā karṇa pāvakaḥ nirdahan pāṇḍava vanam cāru paryacarat raṇe sa saṃvārya mahā astrāṇi mahā iṣvāsaḥ mahātmanām tatas saṃdhāya navatim nimeṣān nata parvaṇām bibheda kavacam rājñaḥ raṇe karṇaḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ sa vidyut abhram savituḥ śiṣṭam vāta hatam yathā ratnaiḥ alaṃkṛtam divyaiḥ vyabhram niśi yathā nabhaḥ sa vivarmā śaraiḥ pārthaḥ rudhireṇa samukṣitaḥ kruddhaḥ sarva āyasīm śaktim cikṣepa ādhirathim prati tām jvalantīm iva ākāśe śaraiḥ ciccheda saptabhiḥ sā chinnā bhūmim apatat mahā iṣvāsasya sāyakaiḥ tatas bāhvoḥ lalāṭe ca hṛdi ca eva yudhiṣṭhiraḥ caturbhiḥ tomaraiḥ karṇam tāḍayitvā mudā anadat evam pārthaḥ vyapāyāt sa nihata prārṣṭisārathiḥ aśaknuvan pramukhatas sthātum karṇasya durmanāḥ tam abhidrutya rādheyaḥ skandham saṃspṛśya pāṇinā prajahyāt samare śatrūn prāṇān rakṣan mahā āhave na bhavān kṣatra dharmeṣu kuśalaḥ asi iti me matiḥ brāhme bale bhavān yuktaḥ svādhyāye yajña karmaṇi mā sma yudhyasva kaunteya mā ca vīrān samāsadaḥ mā ca enān apriyam brūhi mā ca vraja mahā raṇam evam uktvā tatas pārtham visṛjya ca mahā balaḥ nyahanat pāṇḍavīm senām vajrahastaḥ iva āsurīm tatas prāyāt drutam rājan vrīḍan iva janeśvaraḥ cedi pāṇḍava pāñcālāḥ sātyakiḥ ca mahā rathaḥ draupadeyāḥ tathā śūrāḥ mādrī putrau ca pāṇḍavau tatas yudhiṣṭhira anīkam dṛṣṭvā karṇaḥ parāṅmukham kurubhiḥ sahitaḥ vīraiḥ pṛṣṭha gaiḥ pṛṣṭham anvayāt śaṅkha bherī ninādaiḥ ca kārmukāṇām ca nisvanaiḥ babhūva dhārtarāṣṭrāṇām siṃhanāda ravaḥ tadā śruta kīrteḥ mahā rāja dṛṣṭavān karṇa vikramam kālyamānam balam dṛṣṭvā dharmarājaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ tatas rājñā abhyanujñātāḥ pāṇḍavānām mahā rathāḥ abhavat tumulaḥ śabdaḥ yodhānām tatra bhārata hasti aśva ratha pattīnām śastrāṇām ca tatas tatas iti bruvāṇāḥ anyonyam jaghnuḥ yodhāḥ raṇa ajire vipatākā dhvaja chatrāḥ vyaśva sūta āyudhāḥ raṇe vyaṅga aṅga avayavāḥ petuḥ kṣitau kṣīṇāḥ hata īśvarāḥ pravarāṇi iva śailānām śikharāṇi dvipa uttamāḥ sa ārohāḥ nihatāḥ petuḥ vajra bhinnāḥ iva adrayaḥ sa ārohāḥ turagāḥ petuḥ hata vīrāḥ sahasraśas vipraviddha āyudha aṅgāḥ ca dvirada aśva rathaiḥ hatāḥ prativīraiḥ ca saṃmarde patti saṃghāḥ sahasraśas viśāla āyata tāmra akṣaiḥ padma indu sadṛśa ānanaiḥ śirobhiḥ yuddha śauṇḍānām sarvatas saṃstṛtā mahī tathā tu vitate vyomni nisvanam śuśruvuḥ janāḥ hatān kṛttān abhimukhān vīrān vīraiḥ sahasraśas āropya āropya gacchanti vimāneṣu apsaraḥ gaṇāḥ tat dṛṣṭvā mahat āścaryam pratyakṣam svarga lipsayā prahṛṣṭa manasaḥ śūrāḥ kṣipram jagmuḥ parasparam pattayaḥ pattibhiḥ nāgāḥ nāgaiḥ saha hayaiḥ hayāḥ evam pravṛtte saṃgrāme gaja vāji jana kṣaye muṣṭi yuddham niyuddham ca deha pāpma vināśanam nara aśva gaja dehebhyaḥ prasṛtā lohita āpagā nara aśva gaja dehān sā vyuvāha patitān bahūn nara aśva gaja saṃbādhe nara aśva gaja sādinām nara aśva gaja dehān sā vahantī bhīru bhīṣaṇī tasyāḥ parama pāram ca vrajanti vijaya eṣiṇaḥ te tu lohita digdha aṅgāḥ rakta varma āyudha ambarāḥ sasnuḥ tasyām papuḥ ca asṛj mamluḥ ca bharata ṛṣabha rathān aśvān narān nāgān āyudha ābharaṇāni ca vasanāni atha varmāṇi hanyamānān hatān api bhūmim kham dyām diśaḥ ca eva prāyas paśyāma lohitam viṣādaḥ su mahān āsīt prāyas sainyasya bhārata bhūyas samādravan vīrāḥ sātyaki pramukhāḥ rathāḥ teṣām āpatatām vegam a viṣahya mahātmanām putrāṇām te mahat sainyam āsīt rājan parāṅmukham tat prakīrṇa ratha aśva ibham nara vāji samākulam vyadravat tāvakam sainyam loḍyamānam samantataḥ siṃha arditam mahā araṇye yathā gaja kulam tathā saṃjayaḥ uvāca tān abhidravataḥ dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavān tāvakam balam tatas pakṣāt prapakṣāt ca prapakṣaiḥ ca api dakṣiṇāt karṇaḥ api dṛṣṭvā dravataḥ dhārtarāṣṭrān parāṅmukhān haṃsa varṇān haya agryān tān praiṣīt yatra vṛkodaram te preṣitāḥ mahā rāja śalyena āhava śobhinā dṛṣṭvā karṇam samāyāntam bhīmaḥ krodha samanvitaḥ matim dadhre vināśāya karṇasya bharata ṛṣabha saḥ abravīt sātyakim vīram dhṛṣṭadyumnam ca pārṣatam enam rakṣata rājānam dharma ātmānam yudhiṣṭhiram hantā vā asmi raṇe karṇam sa vā mām nihaniṣyati saṃgrāmeṇa su ghoreṇa satyam etat bravīmi vaḥ rājānam adya bhavatām nyāsa bhūtam dadāmi vai asya saṃrakṣaṇe sarve yatadhvam vigata jvarāḥ evam uktvā mahā bāhuḥ prāyāt ādhirathim prati siṃhanādena mahatā sarvāḥ saṃnādayan diśaḥ dṛṣṭvā tvaritam āyāntam bhīmam yuddha abhinandinam sūtaputram athā uvāca madrāṇām īśvaraḥ vibhuḥ paśya karṇa mahā bāhum kruddham pāṇḍava nandanam dīrgha kāla arjitam krodham moktu kāmam tvayi dhruvam īdṛśam na asya rūpam me dṛṣṭa pūrvam kadā cana bibharti yādṛśam rūpam kālāgni sadṛśam śubham iti bruvati rādheyam madrāṇām īśvare nṛpa tathāgatam tu saṃprekṣya bhīmam yuddha abhinandinam abravīt vacanam śalyam rādheyaḥ prahasan iva bhīmasenam prati vibho tat satyam na atra saṃśayaḥ eṣa śūraḥ ca vīraḥ ca krodhanaḥ ca vṛkodaraḥ nirapekṣaḥ śarīre ca prāṇataḥ ca bala adhikaḥ ajñāta vāsam vasatā virāṭa nagare tadā draupadyāḥ priya kāmena kevalam bāhu saṃśrayāt gūḍha bhāvam samāśritya kīcakaḥ sa gaṇaḥ hataḥ saḥ adya saṃgrāma śirasi saṃnaddhaḥ krodha mūrcchitaḥ kiṃkara udyata daṇḍena mṛtyunā api vrajet raṇam cira kāla abhilaṣitaḥ mama ayam tu manorathaḥ arjunam samare hanyām mām vā hanyāt dhanaṃjayaḥ uvāca vacanam śalyaḥ sūtaputram tathāgatam abhiyāsi mahā bāho bhīmasenam mahā balam yaḥ te kāmaḥ abhilaṣitaḥ cirāt prabhṛti hṛd gataḥ evam ukte tatas karṇaḥ śalyam punar abhāṣata hantā aham arjunam saṃkhye mām vā hantā dhanaṃjayaḥ yuddhe manaḥ samādhāya yāhi yāhi iti acodayat tatas prāyāt rathena āśu śalyaḥ tatra viśām pate yatra bhīmaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ vyadrāvayata vāhinīm tatas tūrya ninādaḥ ca bherīṇām ca mahā svanaḥ udatiṣṭhata rāja indra karṇa bhīma samāgame nārācaiḥ vimalaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ diśaḥ prādrāvayat balī sa saṃnipātaḥ tumulaḥ bhīma rūpaḥ viśām pate āsīt raudraḥ mahā rāja karṇa pāṇḍavayoḥ mṛdhe tatas muhūrtāt rāja indra pāṇḍavaḥ karṇam ādravat tam āpatantam saṃprekṣya karṇaḥ vaikartanaḥ vṛṣaḥ punar ca enam ameya ātmā śara varṣaiḥ avākirat sa viddhaḥ sūtaputreṇa chādayām āsa patribhiḥ nārācena su tīkṣṇena sarva āvaraṇa bhedinā saḥ anyat kārmukam ādāya sūtaputram vṛkodaraḥ rājan marmasu marma jñaḥ viddhvā su niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ tam karṇaḥ pañcaviṃśatyā nārācānām samārdayat tatas sāyaka bhinna aṅgaḥ pāṇḍavaḥ krodha mūrcchitaḥ saṃrambha amarṣa tāmra akṣaḥ sūtaputra vadha icchayā girīṇām api bhettāram sāyakam samayojayat vikṛṣya balavat cāpam ā karṇāt ati mārutiḥ tam mumoca mahā iṣvāsaḥ kruddhaḥ karṇa jighāṃsayā sa visṛṣṭaḥ balavatā bāṇaḥ vajra aśani svanaḥ niṣasāda rathopasthe visaṃjñaḥ pṛtanāpatiḥ tatas madra adhipaḥ dṛṣṭvā visaṃjñam sūtanandanam tatas parājite karṇe dhārtarāṣṭrīm mahā camūm dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca su duṣkaram idam karma kṛtam bhīmena saṃjaya yena karṇaḥ mahā bāhuḥ rathopasthe nipātitaḥ karṇaḥ hi ekaḥ raṇe hantā sṛñjayān pāṇḍavaiḥ saha iti duryodhanaḥ sūta prābravīt mām muhur muhur parājitam tu rādheyam dṛṣṭvā bhīmena saṃyuge saṃjayaḥ uvāca vibhrāntam prekṣya rādheyam sūtaputram mahā āhave mahatyā senayā rājan sodaryān samabhāṣata śīghram gacchata bhadram vaḥ rādheyam parirakṣata bhīmasena bhaya agādhe majjantam vyasana arṇave te tu rājñā samādiṣṭāḥ bhīmasena jighāṃsavaḥ śrutāyuḥ durdharaḥ krāthaḥ vivitsuḥ vikaṭaḥ samaḥ niṣaṅgī kavacī pāśī tathā nanda upanandakau duṣpradharṣaḥ subāhuḥ ca vātavega suvarcasau ete rathaiḥ parivṛtāḥ vīryavantaḥ mahā balāḥ bhīmasenam samāsādya samantāt paryavārayan te vyamuñcan śara vrātān nānā liṅgān samantataḥ teṣām āpatatām kṣipram sutānām te narādhipa rathaiḥ pañcāśatā sārdham pañcāśat nyahanat rathān sa kuṇḍala śirastrāṇam pūrṇa candra upamam tadā tam dṛṣṭvā nihatam śūram bhrātaraḥ sarvatas prabho tatas aparābhyām bhallābhyām putrayoḥ te mahā āhave jahāra samare prāṇān bhīmaḥ bhīma parākramaḥ tau dharām anvapadyetām vāta rugṇau iva drumau hāhākāraḥ tatas tīvraḥ saṃbabhūva janeśvara vadhyamāneṣu te rājan tadā putreṣu dhanviṣu teṣām saṃlulite sainye bhīmasenaḥ mahā balaḥ tatas te prādravan bhītāḥ putrāḥ te vihvalīkṛtāḥ bhīmasenam raṇe dṛṣṭvā kāla antaka yama upamam putrān te nihatān dṛṣṭvā sūtaputraḥ mahā manāḥ haṃsa varṇān hayān bhūyas prāhiṇot yatra pāṇḍavaḥ te preṣitāḥ mahā rāja madra rājena vājinaḥ sa saṃnipātaḥ tumulaḥ ghora rūpaḥ viśām pate āsīt raudraḥ mahā rāja karṇa pāṇḍavayoḥ mṛdhe dṛṣṭvā mama mahā rāja tau sametau mahā rathau āsīt buddhiḥ katham nūnam etat adya bhaviṣyati viratham bhīma karmāṇam bhīmam karṇaḥ cakāra ha nāgān saptaśatān rājan īṣā dantān prahāriṇaḥ vyadhamat sahasā bhīmaḥ kruddha rūpaḥ paraṃtapaḥ dantaveṣṭeṣu netreṣu kambheṣu sa kaṭeṣu ca tatas te prādravan bhītāḥ pratīpam prahitāḥ punar tān sa saptaśatān nāgān sa āroha āyudha ketanān bhūmiṣṭhaḥ gadayā jaghne śarad meghān iva anilaḥ pothayām āsa kaunteyaḥ dvāpañcāśatam āhave tathā ratha śatam sāgram pattīn ca śataśas aparān nyahanat pāṇḍavaḥ yuddhe tāpayan tava vāhinīm pratāpyamānam sūryeṇa bhīmena ca mahātmanā rathāḥ pañcaśatāḥ ca anye hrādinaḥ carma varmiṇaḥ bhīmam abhyadravan tūrṇam śara pūgaiḥ samantataḥ tān sa sūta rathān sarvān sa patākā dhvaja āyudhān pothayām āsa gadayā bhīmaḥ viṣṇuḥ iva asurān tatas śakuni nirdiṣṭāḥ sādinaḥ śūra saṃmatāḥ tri sāhasrāḥ yayuḥ bhīmam śakti ṛṣṭi prāsa pāṇayaḥ tān pratyudgamya yavanān aśva ārohān vara ari hā vicaran vividhān mārgān ghātayām āsa pothayan teṣām āsīt mahān śabdaḥ tāḍitānām ca sārvaśaḥ asibhiḥ chidyamānānām naḍānām iva bhārata śaraiḥ pracchādayām āsa sārathim ca api apātayat tatas saṃpradrutam saṃkhye ratham dṛṣṭvā mahā rathaḥ rājānam abhi dhāvantam śaraiḥ āvṛtya rodasī kruddhaḥ pracchādayām āsa śara jālena mārutiḥ saṃnivṛttaḥ tatas tūrṇam rādheyaḥ śatru karśanaḥ bhīmam pracchādayām āsa samantāt niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ bhīmasena ratha vyagram karṇam bhārata sātyakiḥ abhyardayat ameya ātmā pārṣṇigrahaṇa kāraṇāt tau anyonyam samāsādya vṛṣabhau sarva dhanvinām visṛjantau śarān citrān vibhrājetām manasvinau tābhyām viyati rāja indra vitatam bhīma darśanam krauñca pṛṣṭha aruṇam raudram bāṇa jālam vyadṛśyata na eva sūrya prabhām kham vā na diśaḥ pradiśaḥ kutas vayam tābhyām śaraiḥ muktaiḥ sahasraśas hṛtāḥ sarvāḥ śara oghaiḥ taiḥ karṇa mādhavayoḥ tadā saubalam kṛtavarmāṇam drauṇim ādhirathim kṛpam saṃsaktān pāṇḍavaiḥ dṛṣṭvā nivṛttāḥ kuravaḥ punar teṣām āpatatām śabdaḥ tīvraḥ āsīt viśām pate uddhūtānām yathā vṛṣṭyā sāgarāṇām bhaya āvahaḥ te sene bhṛśa saṃvigne dṛṣṭvā anyonyam mahā raṇe yādṛśam na kadā cit hi dṛṣṭa pūrvam na ca śrutam āsīt ninādaḥ su mahān bala oghānām parasparam garjatām sāgara oghāṇām yathā syāt nisvanaḥ mahān tatas pravavṛte yuddham ghora rūpam viśām pate kurūṇām pāṇḍavānām ca lipsatām su mahat yaśaḥ kurūṇām garjatām tatra aviccheda kṛtāḥ giraḥ śrūyante vividhāḥ rājan nāmāni uddiśya bhārata yasya yat hi raṇe nyaṅgam pitṛtaḥ mātṛtaḥ api vā tān dṛṣṭvā samare śūrān tarjayānān parasparam abhavat me matī rājan na eṣām asti iti jīvitam teṣām dṛṣṭvā tu kruddhānām vapūṃṣi amita tejasām tatas te pāṇḍavāḥ rājan kauravāḥ ca mahā rathāḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca kṣatriyāḥ te mahā rāja paraspara vadha eṣiṇaḥ ratha oghāḥ ca haya oghāḥ ca nara oghāḥ ca samantataḥ gaja oghāḥ ca mahā rāja saṃsaktāḥ sma parasparam gadānām parighāṇām ca kaṇapānām ca sarpatām prāsānām bhinḍipālānām bhuśuṇḍīnām ca sarvaśas saṃpātam ca anvapaśyāma saṃgrāme bhṛśa dāruṇe śalabhāḥ iva saṃpetuḥ samantāt śara vṛṣṭayaḥ nāgāḥ nāgān samāsādya vyadhamanta parasparam nāgāḥ ca samare tri aṅgam mamṛduḥ śīghra gāḥ nṛpa patatām tatra śūrāṇām krośatām ca parasparam ghoram āyodhanam jajñe paśūnām vaiśasam yathā rudhireṇa samāstīrṇā bhāti bhārata medinī śakragopa gaṇa ākīrṇā prāvṛṣi iva yathā dharā yathā vā vāsasī śukle mahārajana rañjite bibhṛyāt yuvatiḥ śyāmā tadvat āsīt vasuṃdharā māṃsa śoṇita citrā iva śātakaumbha mayī iva ca chinnānām ca uttamāṅgānām bāhūnām ca ūrubhiḥ saha kuṇḍalānām praviddhānām bhūṣaṇānām ca bhārata niṣkāṇām adhi sūtrāṇām śarīrāṇām ca dhanvinām varmaṇām sa patākānām saṃghāḥ tatra apatan bhuvi gajān gajāḥ samāsādya viṣāṇa agraiḥ adārayan viṣāṇa abhihatāḥ te ca bhrājante dviradāḥ yathā rudhireṇa avasikta aṅgāḥ gairika prasravāḥ iva yathā bhrājanti syandantaḥ parvatāḥ dhātu maṇḍitāḥ tomarān gajibhiḥ muktān pratīpān āsthitān bahūn hastaiḥ viceruḥ te nāgāḥ babhañjuḥ ca apare tathā nārācaiḥ chinna varmāṇaḥ bhrājante sma gaja uttamāḥ hima āgame mahā rāja vyabhrāḥ iva mahīdharāḥ ulkābhiḥ saṃpradīpta agrāḥ parvatāḥ iva māriṣa ke cit abhyāhatāḥ nāgāḥ nāgaiḥ naga nibhāḥ bhuvi apare prādravan nāgāḥ śalya ārtāḥ vraṇa pīḍitāḥ mamluḥ ca bahavaḥ rājan cukūjuḥ ca apare tathā hayāḥ ca nihatāḥ bāṇaiḥ svarṇa bhāṇḍa paricchadāḥ niṣeduḥ ca eva mamluḥ ca babhramuḥ ca diśaḥ daśa apare kṛṣyamāṇāḥ ca viveṣṭantaḥ mahī tale bhāvān bahuvidhān cakruḥ tāḍitāḥ śara tomaraiḥ narāḥ tu nihatāḥ bhūmau kūjantaḥ tatra māriṣa dṛṣṭvā ca bāndhavān anye pitṝn anye pitāmahān dhāvamānān parān ca eva dṛṣṭvā anye tatra bhārata gotra nāmāni khyātāni śaśaṃsuḥ itaretaram teṣām chinnāḥ mahā rāja bhujāḥ kanaka bhūṣaṇāḥ vegān ca anye raṇe cakruḥ sphurantaḥ iva pannagāḥ te bhujāḥ bhogi bhoga ābhāḥ candana aktāḥ viśām pate lohita ārdrāḥ bhṛśam rejuḥ tapanīya dhvajāḥ iva bhaumena rajasā kīrṇe śastra saṃpāta saṃkule śoṇita udāḥ mahā nadyaḥ prasasruḥ tatra ca asakṛt śīrṣa pāṣāṇa saṃchannāḥ keśa śaivala śādvalāḥ asthi saṃghāta saṃkīrṇāḥ dhanuḥ śara vara uttamāḥ māṃsa kardama paṅkāḥ ca śoṇita oghāḥ su dāruṇāḥ nadīḥ pravartayām āsuḥ yama rāṣṭra vivardhanīḥ kravyādānām nara vyāghra nardatām tatra tatra ha nṛtyanti vai bhūta gaṇāḥ saṃtṛptāḥ māṃsa śoṇitaiḥ pītvā ca śoṇitam tatra vasām pītvā ca bhārata medaḥ majjā vasā tṛptāḥ tṛptāḥ māṃsasya ca eva hi dhāvamānāḥ ca dṛśyante kāka gṛdhra balāḥ tathā yodha vrata samākhyātāḥ cakruḥ karmāṇi abhīta vat śara śakti samākīrṇe kravyāda gaṇa saṃkule vyacaranta gaṇaiḥ śūrāḥ khyāpayantaḥ sva pauruṣam anyonyam śrāvayanti sma nāma gotrāṇi bhārata pitṛ nāmāni ca raṇe gotra nāmāni ca abhitas śrāvayantaḥ hi bahavaḥ tatra yodhāḥ viśām pate anyonyam avamṛdnantaḥ śakti tomara paṭṭiśaiḥ vyaṣīdat kauravī senā bhinnā nauḥ iva sāgare saṃjayaḥ uvāca vartamāne tadā yuddhe kṣatriyāṇām nimajjane gāṇḍīvasya mahān ghoṣaḥ śuśruve yudhi māriṣa saṃśaptakānām kadanam akarot yatra pāṇḍavaḥ kosalānām tathā rājan nārāyaṇa balasya ca saṃśaptakāḥ tu samare śara vṛṣṭim samantataḥ apātayan pārtha mūrdhni jaya gṛddhāḥ pramanyavaḥ tām vṛṣṭim sahasā rājan tarasā dhārayan prabhuḥ nigṛhya tu ratha anīkam kaṅka patraiḥ śilā śitaiḥ āsasāda raṇe pārthaḥ suśarmāṇam mahā ratham sa tasya śara varṣāṇi vavarṣa rathinām varaḥ tathā saṃśaptakāḥ ca eva pārthasya samare sthitāḥ suśarmā tu tatas pārtham viddhvā navabhiḥ āśugaiḥ kapeḥ tu ninadam śrutvā saṃtrastā tava vāhinī bhayam vipulam ādāya niśceṣṭā samapadyata tatas sā śuśubhe senā niśceṣṭā avasthitā nṛpa nānā puṣpa samākīrṇam yathā caitraratham vanam arjunam siṣicuḥ bāṇaiḥ parvatam jaladāḥ iva te hayān ratha cakre ca ratha īṣāḥ ca api bhārata nigṛhya balavat tūrṇam siṃhanādam atha anadan pārtham anye mahā rāja ratha stham jagṛhuḥ mudā keśavaḥ tu tadā bāhū vidhunvan raṇa mūrdhani pātayām āsa tān sarvān duṣṭa hastī iva hastinaḥ tatas kruddhaḥ raṇe pārthaḥ saṃvṛtaḥ taiḥ mahā rathaiḥ nigṛhītam ratham dṛṣṭvā keśavam ca api abhidrutam ratha ārūḍhān ca su bahūn padātīn ca api apātayat āsannān ca tatas yodhān śaraiḥ āsanna yodhibhiḥ cyāvayām āsa samare keśavam ca idam abravīt paśya kṛṣṇa mahā bāho saṃśaptaka gaṇān mayā kurvāṇān dāruṇam karma vadhyamānān sahasraśas ratha bandham imam ghoram pṛthivyām na asti kaḥ cana pāñcajanyam ca kṛṣṇaḥ api pūrayan iva rodasī tam tu śaṅkha svanam śrutvā saṃśaptaka varūthinī saṃcacāla mahā rāja vitrastā ca abhavat bhṛśam pada bandham tatas cakre pāṇḍavaḥ para vīra hā nāgam astram mahā rāja saṃprodīrya muhur muhur yān uddiśya raṇe pārthaḥ pada bandham cakāra ha te baddhāḥ pada bandhena pāṇḍavena mahātmanā niśceṣṭāḥ abhavan rājan aśmasāra mayāḥ iva niśceṣṭān tu tatas yodhān avadhīt pāṇḍu nandanaḥ āyudhāni ca sarvāṇi visraṣṭum upacakramuḥ tatas suśarmā rāja indra gṛhītām vīkṣya vāhinīm sauparṇam astram tvaritaḥ prāduścakre mahā rathaḥ tatas suparṇāḥ saṃpetuḥ bhakṣayantaḥ bhujaṃgamān te vai vidudruvuḥ nāgāḥ dṛṣṭvā tān kha carān nṛpa megha vṛndāt yathā muktaḥ bhāskaraḥ tāpayan prajāḥ sasṛjuḥ bāṇa saṃghān ca śastra saṃghān ca māriṣa tām mahā astra mayīm vṛṣṭim saṃchidya śara vṛṣṭibhiḥ vyavātiṣṭhat tatas yodhān vāsaviḥ para vīra hā suśarmā tu tatas rājan bāṇena ānata parvaṇā arjunam hṛdaye viddhvā vivyādha anyaiḥ tribhiḥ śaraiḥ pratilabhya tatas saṃjñām śvetāśvaḥ kṛṣṇa sārathiḥ tatas bāṇa sahasrāṇi samutpannāni māriṣa sarva dikṣu vyadṛśyanta sūdayantaḥ nṛpa dvipān hayān rathān ca samare śastraiḥ śata sahasraśas vadhyamāne tatas sainye vipulā bhīḥ samāviśat saṃśaptaka gaṇānām ca gopālānām ca bhārata paśyatām tatra vīrāṇām ahanyata mahat balam hanyamānam apaśyan ca niśceṣṭāḥ sma parākrame ayutam tatra yodhānām hatvā pāṇḍu sutaḥ raṇe caturdaśa sahasrāṇi yāni śiṣṭāni bhārata rathānām ayutam ca eva tri sāhasrāḥ ca dantinaḥ tatas saṃśaptakāḥ bhūyas parivavruḥ dhanaṃjayam tatra yuddham mahat hi āsīt tāvakānām viśām pate śūreṇa balinā sārdham pāṇḍavena kirīṭinā saṃjayaḥ uvāca kṛtavarmā kṛpaḥ drauṇiḥ sūtaputraḥ ca māriṣa ulūkaḥ saubalaḥ ca eva rājā ca saha sodaraiḥ sīdamānām camūm dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍu putra bhaya arditām samujjihīrṣuḥ vegena bhinnām nāvam iva arṇave bhīrūṇām trāsa jananam śūrāṇām harṣa vardhanam kṛpeṇa śara varṣāṇi vipramuktāni saṃyuge sṛñjayāḥ śātayām āsuḥ śalabhānām vrajāḥ iva vavarṣa śara varṣāṇi samantāt eva brāhmaṇe śikhaṇḍinam raṇe kruddhaḥ vivyādha daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ tatas śikhaṇḍī śaraiḥ saptabhiḥ āhave kṛpam vivyādha su bhṛśam kaṅka patraiḥ ajihmagaiḥ tatas kṛpaḥ śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ saḥ atividdhaḥ mahā rathaḥ vyaśva sūta ratham cakre pārṣatam tu dvijottamaḥ hata aśvāt tu tatas yānāt avaplutya mahā rathaḥ carma khaḍge ca saṃgṛhya sa tvaram brāhmaṇam yayau tam āpatantam sahasā śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ tatra adbhutam apaśyāma śilānām plavanam yathā niśceṣṭaḥ yat raṇe rājan śikhaṇḍī samatiṣṭhata kṛpeṇa chāditam dṛṣṭvā nṛpa uttama śikhaṇḍinam pratyudyayau kṛpam tūrṇam dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ mahā rathaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnam tatas yāntam śāradvata ratham prati yudhiṣṭhiram atha āyāntam śāradvata ratham prati pratijagrāha te putraḥ śara varṣeṇa vārayan bhīmasenam karūṣān ca kekayān saha sṛñjayān śikhaṇḍinaḥ tatas bāṇān kṛpaḥ śāradvataḥ yudhi prāhiṇot tvarayā yuktaḥ didhakṣuḥ iva māriṣa tān śarān preṣitān tena samantāt hema bhūṣaṇān ciccheda khaḍgam āvidhya bhrāmayan ca punar punar vyadhamat sāyakaiḥ tūrṇam tatas uccukruśuḥ janāḥ sa vicarmā mahā rāja khaḍga pāṇiḥ upādravat kṛpasya vaśam āpannaḥ mṛtyoḥ āsyam iva āturaḥ śāradvata śaraiḥ grastam kliśyamānam mahā balam vikiran brāhmaṇam yuddhe bahubhiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ dṛṣṭvā aviṣahyam tam yuddhe brāhmaṇam carita vratam apayātaḥ tatas tūrṇam śikhaṇḍī rāja sattama viddhvā vivyādha saptatyā punar ca enam tribhiḥ śaraiḥ atha asya sa śaram cāpam punar ciccheda māriṣa sārathim ca śareṇa asya bhṛśam marmaṇi atāḍayat suketum triṃśatā bāṇaiḥ sarva marmasu atāḍayat bhūmicāle yathā vṛkṣaḥ calati ākampitaḥ bhṛśam sa uṣṇīṣam sa śirastrāṇam kṣurapreṇa anvapātayat tat śiraḥ prāpatat bhūmau śyena āhṛtam iva āmiṣam tatas asya kāyaḥ vasudhām paścāt prāpa tadā cyutaḥ tasmin hate mahā rāja trastāḥ tasya padānugāḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnam tu samare saṃnivārya mahā balaḥ kṛtavarmā abravīt dhṛṣṭaḥ tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti pārṣatam tat abhūt tumulam yuddham vṛṣṇi pārṣatayoḥ raṇe āmiṣa arthe yathā yuddham śyenayoḥ gṛddhayoḥ nṛpa dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ tu samare hārdikyam navabhiḥ śaraiḥ ājaghāna urasi kruddhaḥ pīḍayan hṛdika ātmajam kṛtavarmā tu
