āsīt krūram viśasanam mahat tathā eva pāṇḍavāḥ śūrāḥ dhṛṣṭadyumna śikhaṇḍinau draupadeyāḥ ca saṃkruddhāḥ abhyaghnan tāvakam balam evam eṣa kṣayaḥ vṛttaḥ pāṇḍavānām tatas tatas tāvakānām api raṇe bhīmam prāpya mahā balam saṃjayaḥ uvāca sūtaputram su saṃrabdham dṛṣṭvā ca eva mahā raṇe śoṇita udām mahīm kṛtvā māṃsa majja asthi vāhinīm vāsudevam idam vākyam abravīt puruṣa ṛṣabha eṣa ketuḥ raṇe kṛṣṇa sūtaputrasya dṛśyate ete dravanti pāñcālāḥ karṇāt trastāḥ janārdana eṣa duryodhanaḥ rājā śveta chatreṇa bhāsvatā karṇena bhagnān pāñcālān drāvayan bahu śobhate kṛpaḥ ca kṛtavarmā ca drauṇiḥ ca eva mahā balaḥ ete rakṣanti rājānam sūtaputreṇa rakṣitāḥ eṣa śalyaḥ rathopasthe raśmi saṃcāra kovidaḥ sūtaputra ratham kṛṣṇa vāhayan bahu śobhate na a hatvā samare karṇam nivartiṣye katham cana rādheyaḥ api anyathā pārthān sṛñjayān ca mahā rathān niḥśeṣān samare kuryāt paśyatoḥ nau janārdana tatas prāyāt rathena āśu keśavaḥ tava vāhinīm karṇam prati mahā iṣvāsam dvairathe savyasācinā prayātaḥ ca mahā bāhuḥ pāṇḍava anujñayā hariḥ āśvāsayan rathena eva pāṇḍu sainyāni sarvaśas ratha ghoṣaḥ sa saṃgrāme pāṇḍaveyasya saṃbabhau mahatā ratha ghoṣeṇa pāṇḍavaḥ satya vikramaḥ tam āyāntam samīkṣya eva śvetāśvam kṛṣṇasārathim madra rājaḥ abravīt karṇam ketum dṛṣṭvā mahātmanaḥ ayam sa rathaḥ āyāti śveta aśvaḥ kṛṣṇa sārathiḥ eṣa tiṣṭhati kaunteyaḥ saṃspṛśan gāṇḍivam dhanuḥ eṣā vidīryate senā dhārtarāṣṭrī samantataḥ arjunasya bhayāt tūrṇam nighnataḥ śātravān bahūn tvām ṛte krodha dīptaḥ hi pīḍyamāne vṛkodare viratham dharmarājam ca dṛṣṭvā su dṛḍha vikṣatam śikhaṇḍinam sātyakim ca dhṛṣṭadyumnam ca pārṣatam na ca asya rakṣām paśyāmi pṛṣṭhatas na ca pārśvatas ekaḥ eva abhiyāti tvām paśya sāphalyam ātmanaḥ tvam hi kṛṣṇau raṇe śaktaḥ saṃsādhayitum āhave tvam kṛtaḥ hi eva bhīṣmeṇa droṇa drauṇi kṛpaiḥ api lelihānam yathā sarpam garjantam ṛṣabham yathā ete dravanti samare dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ mahā rathāḥ arjunasya bhayāt tūrṇam nirapekṣāḥ janādhipāḥ dravatām atha teṣām tu yudhi nā anyaḥ asti mānavaḥ ete tvām kuravaḥ sarve dvīpam āsādya saṃyuge viṣṭhitāḥ puruṣa vyāghra tvattaḥ śaraṇa kāṅkṣiṇaḥ vaideha ambaṣṭha kāmbojāḥ tathā nagnajitaḥ tvayā gāndhārāḥ ca yayā dhṛtyā jitāḥ saṃkhye su durjayāḥ tām dhṛtim kuru rādheya tatas pratyehi pāṇḍavam vāsudevam ca vārṣṇeyam prīyamāṇam kirīṭinā karṇaḥ uvāca prakṛti sthaḥ hi me śalyaḥ idānīm saṃmataḥ tathā pratibhāsi mahā bāho vibhīḥ ca eva dhanaṃjayāt paśya bāhvoḥ balam me adya śikṣitasya ca paśya me ekaḥ adya nihaniṣyāmi pāṇḍavānām mahā camūm kṛṣṇau ca puruṣa vyāghrau tat ca satyam bravīmi te na a hatvā yudhi tau vīrau apayāsye katham cana kṛtārthaḥ vā bhaviṣyāmi hatvā tau atha vā hataḥ na etādṛśaḥ jātu babhūva loke ratha uttamaḥ yāvat anuśrutam naḥ tam īdṛśam pratiyotsyāmi pārtham mahā āhave paśya ca pauruṣam me sa vā adya mām neṣyati kṛcchram etat karṇasya antāt etat antāḥ stha sarve dṛḍha āyudhaḥ kṛtimān kṣipra hastaḥ na pāṇḍaveyena samaḥ asti yodhaḥ gṛhṇāti anekān api kaṅka patrān ekam yathā tān kṣitipān pramathya atoṣayat pāṇḍaveyaḥ hutāśam kṛṣṇa dvitīyaḥ atirathaḥ tarasvī lebhe cakram yatra kṛṣṇaḥ mahātmā dhanuḥ gāṇḍīvam pāṇḍavaḥ savyasācī śveta aśva yuktam ca su ghoṣam agryam ratham mahā bāhuḥ adīna sattvaḥ mahā iṣudhī ca akṣayau divya rūpau śastrāṇi divyāni ca havyavāhāt tathā indra loke nijaghāna daityān asaṃkhyeyān kālakeyān ca sarvān lebhe śaṅkham devadattam sma tatra kaḥ nāma tena abhyadhikaḥ pṛthivyām mahādevam toṣayām āsa ca eva sākṣāt su yuddhena mahā anubhāvaḥ lebhe tatas pāśupatam su ghoram trailokya saṃhāra karam mahā astram pṛthak pṛthak lokapālāḥ sametāḥ daduḥ hi astrāṇi aprameyāṇi yasya yaiḥ tān jaghāna āśu raṇe nṛ siṃhān sa kāla khañjān asurān sametān tam īdṛśam vīrya guṇa upapannam kṛṣṇa dvitīyam varaye raṇāya mahātmanaḥ śaṅkha cakra asi pāṇeḥ viṣṇoḥ jiṣṇoḥ vasudeva ātmajasya bhayam me vai jāyate sādhvasam ca dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇau eka rathe sametau etādṛśau phalguna vāsudevau kaḥ anyaḥ pratīyāt mat ṛte nu śalya etau aham yudhi vā pātayiṣye mām vā kṛṣṇau nihaniṣyataḥ adya kṛpam ca bhojam ca mahā bhujau ubhau tathā eva gāndhāra nṛpam saha anujam guroḥ sutam ca avara jam tathā ātmanaḥ padātinaḥ atha dvipa sādinaḥ anyān nirundhata abhidravata acyuta arjunau śrameṇa saṃyojayata āśu sarvatas tathā iti ca uktvā tvaritāḥ sma te arjunam jighāṃsavaḥ vīratamāḥ samabhyayuḥ na saṃdadhānaḥ na tathā śara uttamān pramuñcamānaḥ ripubhiḥ pradṛśyate dhanaṃjayaḥ tasya śaraiḥ ca dāritāḥ hatāḥ ca petuḥ nara vāji kuñjarāḥ śara arciṣam gāṇḍiva cāru maṇḍalam yugānta sūrya pratimāna tejasam na kauravāḥ śekuḥ udīkṣitum jayam yathā ravim vyādhita cakṣuṣaḥ janāḥ jighāṃsubhiḥ tān kuśalaiḥ śara uttamān mahā āhave saṃjavitān prayatnataḥ sa gāṇḍiva abhyāyata pūrṇa maṇḍalaḥ tapan ripūn arjuna bhāskaraḥ babhau śara ugra raśmiḥ śuci śukra madhya gaḥ yathā eva sūryaḥ pariveṣa gaḥ tathā athā agrya bāṇaiḥ daśabhiḥ dhanaṃjayam parābhinat droṇa sutaḥ acyutam tribhiḥ caturbhiḥ aśvān caturaḥ kapim tathā śaraiḥ sa nārāca varaiḥ avākirat tathā tu tat tat sphurat ātta kārmukam tribhiḥ śaraiḥ yantṛ śiraḥ kṣureṇa sa roṣa pūrṇaḥ aśani vajra hāṭakaiḥ alaṃkṛtam takṣaka bhoga varcasam svam āyudham ca upavikīrya bhū tale dhanuḥ ca kṛtvā sa guṇam guṇa adhikaḥ kṛpaḥ ca bhojaḥ ca tathā ātmajaḥ ca te tamonudam vāridharāḥ iva apatan kṛpasya pārthaḥ sa śaram śarāsanam hayān dhvajam sārathim eva patribhiḥ jaghāna ca aśvān kṛtavarmaṇaḥ śubhān dhvajam ca ciccheda tatas pratāpavān sa vāji sūteṣu asanān sa ketanān jaghāna nāga aśva rathān tvaran ca saḥ tatas prakīrṇam su mahat balam tava pradāritam setuḥ iva ambhasā yathā tatas arjunasya āśu rathena keśavaḥ cakāra śatrūn apasavyam āturān tatas prayāntam tvaritam dhanaṃjayam śatakratum vṛtra nijaghnuṣam yathā athā abhisṛtya prativārya tān arīn dhanaṃjayasya abhi ratham mahā rathāḥ śikhaṇḍi śaineya yamāḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ vidārayantaḥ vyanadan su bhairavam kuru pravīrāḥ saha sṛñjayaiḥ yathā surāḥ purā deva varaiḥ ayodhayan jaya īpsavaḥ svar gamanāya ca utsukāḥ patanti nāga aśva rathāḥ paraṃtapa śara andhakāre tu mahātmabhiḥ kṛte mahā mṛdhe yodha varaiḥ parasparam babhuḥ daśa āśāḥ na divam ca pārthiva prabhā ca sūryasya tamaḥ vṛtā abhavat saṃjayaḥ uvāca vimṛdya sūtaputrasya senām bhārata sāyakaiḥ prāhiṇot mṛtyu lokāya para vīrān dhanaṃjayaḥ tatas asya ambaram āvṛtya śara jālāni bhāgaśas sa pakṣi saṃgha ācaritam ākāśam pūrayan śaraiḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ mahā rāja kurūṇām antakaḥ abhavat gātrāṇi prākṣiṇot pārthaḥ śirāṃsi ca cakarta ha dhanaṃjaya śara abhyastaiḥ syandana aśva nara dvipaiḥ raṇa bhūmiḥ abhūt rājan mahā vaitaraṇī yathā īṣā cakra akṣa bhaṅgaiḥ ca vyaśvaiḥ sa aśvaiḥ ca yudhyatām sa sūtaiḥ hata sūtaiḥ ca rathaiḥ stīrṇā abhavat mahī suvarṇa varma saṃnāhaiḥ yodhaiḥ kanaka bhūṣaṇaiḥ āsthitāḥ kṛta varmāṇaḥ bhadrāḥ nitya madāḥ dvipāḥ kruddhāḥ kruddhaiḥ mahāmātraiḥ preṣitāḥ arjunam abhyayus catur śatāḥ śara varṣaiḥ hatāḥ petuḥ kirīṭinā paryastāni iva śṛṅgāṇi sa sattvāni mahā gireḥ dhanaṃjaya śara abhyastaiḥ stīrṇā bhūḥ vara vāraṇaiḥ tatas prādīryata camūḥ dhanaṃjaya śara āhatā mahā vāta samāviddhā mahā nauḥ iva sāgare nānā rūpāḥ praharaṇāḥ śarāḥ gāṇḍīva coditāḥ mahā girau veṇu vanam niśi prajvalitam yathā saṃpiṣṭa dagdha vidhvastam tava sainyam kirīṭinā hatam pravihatam bāṇaiḥ sarvatas pradrutam diśaḥ mahā vane mṛga gaṇāḥ dāva agni grasitāḥ yathā utsṛjya hi mahā bāhum bhīmasenam tadā raṇe balam kurūṇām udvignam sarvam āsīt parāṅmukham tatas kuruṣu bhagneṣu bībhatsuḥ aparājitaḥ bhīmasenam samāsādya muhūrtam saḥ abhyavartata bhīmasena abhyanujñātaḥ tatas prāyāt dhanaṃjayaḥ nādayan ratha ghoṣeṇa pṛthivīm dyām ca bhārata tatas parivṛtaḥ bhīmaiḥ daśabhiḥ śatru puṃgavaiḥ ātateṣu asanāḥ krūrāḥ nṛtyantaḥ iva bhārata apasavyān tu tān cakre rathena madhusūdanaḥ tatas te prādravan śūrāḥ parāṅmukha rathe arjune teṣām āpatatām ketūn rathān cāpāni sāyakān nārācaiḥ ardhacandraiḥ ca kṣipram pārthaḥ nyapātayat atha anyaiḥ daśabhiḥ bhallaiḥ śirāṃsi eṣām nyapātayat roṣa saṃrakta netrāṇi saṃdaṣṭa oṣṭhāni bhū tale tāni vaktrāṇi vibabhuḥ vyomni tārā gaṇāḥ iva rukma aṅgadān rukma puṅkhaiḥ viddhvā prāyāt amitra hā saṃjayaḥ uvāca yuddhāya abhyadravan vīrāḥ kurūṇām navatī rathāḥ kṛṣṇaḥ śvetān mahā vegān aśvān kanaka bhūṣaṇān muktā jāla praticchannān praiṣīt karṇa ratham prati tatas karṇa ratham yāntam arīn ghnantam dhanaṃjayam bāṇa varṣaiḥ abhighnantaḥ saṃśaptaka rathāḥ yayuḥ tvaramāṇān tu tān sarvān sa sūta iṣvasana dhvajān jaghāna navatim vīrān arjunaḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ te apatanta hatāḥ bāṇaiḥ nānā rūpaiḥ kirīṭinā sa vimānāḥ yathā siddhāḥ svargāt puṇya kṣaye tathā tatas sa ratha nāga aśvāḥ kuravaḥ kurusattama tat āyastam amukta astram udīrṇa vara vāraṇam putrāṇām te mahat sainyam samarautsīt dhanaṃjayaḥ śakti ṛṣṭi tomara prāsaiḥ gadā nistriṃśa sāyakaiḥ prācchādayan mahā iṣvāsāḥ kuravaḥ kuru nandanam tām kurūṇām pravitatām śastra vṛṣṭim samudyatām vyadhamat pāṇḍavaḥ bāṇaiḥ tamaḥ sūryaḥ iva aṃśubhiḥ pārśvatas abhyahanan pārtham tava putrasya śāsanāt karṇi nālīka nārācaiḥ tomaraiḥ prāsa śaktibhiḥ tām astra vṛṣṭim prahitām dvipa sthaiḥ yavanaiḥ smayan atha tān dviradān sarvān nānā liṅgaiḥ mahā śaraiḥ sa patākān saha ārohān girīn vajraiḥ iva abhinat te hema puṅkhaiḥ iṣubhiḥ ācitāḥ hema mālinaḥ hatāḥ petuḥ mahā nāgāḥ sa agni jvālāḥ iva adrayaḥ tatas gāṇḍīva nirghoṣaḥ mahān āsīt viśām pate stanatām kūjatām ca eva manuṣya gaja vājinām kuñjarāḥ ca hatāḥ rājan prādravan te samantataḥ aśvāḥ ca paryadhāvanta hata ārohāḥ diśaḥ daśa rathāḥ hīnāḥ mahā rāja rathibhiḥ vājibhiḥ tathā gandharvanagara ākārāḥ dṛśyante sma sahasraśas aśva ārohāḥ mahā rāja dhāvamānāḥ tatas tatas tatra tatra eva dṛśyante patitāḥ pārtha sāyakaiḥ tasmin kṣaṇe pāṇḍavasya bāhvoḥ balam adṛśyata yat sādinaḥ vāraṇān ca rathān ca ekaḥ ajayat yudhi dṛṣṭvā parivṛtam rājan bhīmasenaḥ kirīṭinam hata avaśeṣān utsṛjya tvadīyān kati cit rathān dṛṣṭvā yat arjunam bhīmaḥ jagāma bhrātaram prati hata avaśiṣṭān turagān arjunena mahā javān bhīmaḥ vyadhamat abhra antaḥ gadā pāṇiḥ mahā āhave kālarātrim iva ati ugrām nara nāga aśva bhojanām prākāra aṭṭa pura dvāra dāraṇīm ati dāruṇām tatas gadām nṛ nāga aśveṣu āśu bhīmaḥ vyavāsṛjat sā jaghāna bahūn aśvān aśva ārohān ca māriṣa kāṃsya āyasa tanutrān tān narān aśvān ca pāṇḍavaḥ pothayām āsa gadayā sa śabdam te apatan hatāḥ hatvā tu tat gaja anīkam bhīmasenaḥ mahā balaḥ punar sva ratham āsthāya pṛṣṭhatas arjunam anvagāt hatam parāṅmukha prāyam nirutsāham param balam vyālambata mahā rāja prāyaśas śastra veṣṭitam dṛṣṭvā prācchādayat bāṇaiḥ arjunaḥ prāṇa tāpanaiḥ tatas kurūṇām abhavat ārta nādaḥ mahā mṛdhe ratha aśva nāga asu haraiḥ vadhyatām arjuna iṣubhiḥ hāhākṛtam bhṛśam tasthau līyamānam parasparam āsīt sva śoṇita klinnam phulla aśoka vanam yathā tat dṛṣṭvā kuravaḥ tatra vikrāntam savyasācinaḥ nirāśāḥ samapadyanta sarve karṇasya jīvite aviṣahyam tu pārthasya śara saṃpātam āhave matvā nyavartan kuravaḥ jitāḥ gāṇḍīvadhanvanā te hitvā samare pārtham vadhyamānāḥ ca sāyakaiḥ pradudruvuḥ diśaḥ bhītāḥ cukruśuḥ ca api sūtajam abhyadravata tān pārthaḥ kiran śara śatān bahūn harṣayan pāṇḍavān yodhān bhīmasena purogamān putrāḥ tu te mahā rāja jagmuḥ karṇa ratham prati agādhe majjatām teṣām dvīpaḥ karṇaḥ abhavat tadā kuravaḥ hi mahā rāja nirviṣāḥ pannagāḥ iva karṇam eva upalīyanta bhayāt gāṇḍīvadhanvanaḥ yathā sarvāṇi bhūtāni mṛtyoḥ bhītāni bhārata tathā karṇam mahā iṣvāsam putrāḥ tava narādhipa upālīyanta saṃtrāsāt pāṇḍavasya mahātmanaḥ tān śoṇita pariklinnān viṣama sthān śara āturān saṃbhagnam hi balam dṛṣṭvā balāt pārthena tāvakam pāñcālān punar ādhāvat paśyataḥ savyasācinaḥ tatas kṣaṇena kṣitipāḥ kṣataja pratima īkṣaṇāḥ karṇam vavarṣuḥ bāṇa oghaiḥ yathā meghāḥ mahīdharam tatas śara sahasrāṇi karṇa muktāni māriṣa vyayojayanta pāñcālān prāṇaiḥ prāṇabhṛtām vara tatas raṇaḥ mahān āsīt pāñcālānām viśām pate vadhyatām sūtaputreṇa mitra arthe amitra ghātinām saṃjayaḥ uvāca tatas karṇaḥ kuruṣu pradruteṣu varūthinā śveta hayena rājan pāñcāla putrān vyadhamat sūtaputraḥ mahā iṣubhiḥ vātaḥ iva abhra saṃghān sūtam rathāt añjalikena pātya jaghāna ca aśvān janamejayasya śatānīkam sutasomam ca bhallaiḥ avākirat dhanuṣī ca api akṛntat dhṛṣṭadyumnam nirbibheda atha ṣaḍbhiḥ jaghāna ca aśvam dakṣiṇam tasya saṃkhye hatvā ca aśvān sātyakeḥ sūtaputraḥ kaikeya putram nyavadhīt viśokam śaraiḥ vibhinnam bhṛśam ugra vegaiḥ karṇa ātmajam saḥ abhyahanat suṣeṇam sa syandanāt gām apatat gatāsuḥ paraśvadhaiḥ śālaḥ iva avarugṇaḥ hata aśvam añjaḥ gatibhiḥ suṣeṇaḥ śini pravīram niśitaiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ pracchādya nṛtyan iva sauti putraḥ śaineya bāṇa abhihataḥ papāta putre hate krodha parīta cetāḥ karṇaḥ śinīnām ṛṣabham jighāṃsuḥ śikhaṇḍinaḥ kārmukam sa dhvajam ca chittvā śarābhyām ahanat sujātam śikhaṇḍinam ṣaḍbhiḥ avidhyat ugraḥ dāntaḥ dhārṣṭadyumna śiraḥ cakarta athā abhinat sutasomam śareṇa sa saṃśitena ādhirathiḥ mahātmā atha ākrande tumule vartamāne dhārṣṭadyumne nihate tatra kṛṣṇaḥ a pāñcālyam kriyate yāhi pārtha karṇam jahi iti abravīt rāja siṃha bhaye teṣām trāṇam icchan su bāhuḥ abhyāhatānām ratha yūthapena visphārya gāṇḍīvam atha ugra ghoṣam jyayā samāhatya tale bhṛśam ca bāṇa andhakāram sahasā eva kṛtvā jaghāna nāga aśva rathān narān ca tam bhīmasenaḥ anu yayau rathena pṛṣṭhe rakṣan pāṇḍavam eka vīram ratha aśva mātaṅga gaṇān jaghāna pracchādayām āsa diśaḥ śaraiḥ ca karṇam vineduḥ sahitāḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ saṃmardamānāḥ saha pārṣatena te pañca pāñcāla rathāḥ su rūpaiḥ vaikartanam karṇam abhidravantaḥ tasmāt rathāt cyāvayitum na śekuḥ dhairyāt kṛta ātmānam iva indriyāṇi teṣām dhanūṃṣi dhvaja vāji sūtān tūṇam patākāḥ ca nikṛtya bāṇaiḥ tān pañcabhiḥ sa tu ahanat pṛṣatkaiḥ karṇaḥ tatas siṃhaḥ iva unnanāda sa adri drumā syāt pṛthivī viśīrṇā iti eva matvā janatā vyaṣīdat sa śakra cāpa pratimena dhanvanā bhṛśa ātatena ādhirathiḥ śarān sṛjan babhau raṇe dīpta marīci maṇḍalaḥ yathā aṃśumālī pariveṣavān tathā śikhaṇḍinam dvādaśabhiḥ parābhinat chitaiḥ śaraiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ atha uttamaujasam parājitāḥ pañca mahā rathāḥ tu te mahā āhave sūta sutena māriṣa tatas śinīnām ṛṣabhaḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ nikṛtya karṇa prahitān iṣūn bahūn vidārya karṇam niśitaiḥ ayasmayaiḥ tava ātmajam jyeṣṭham avidhyat aṣṭabhiḥ kṛpaḥ atha bhojaḥ ca tava ātmajaḥ tathā svayam ca karṇaḥ niśitaiḥ atāḍayat samānatena iṣvasanena kūjatā bhṛśa ātatena amita bāṇa varṣiṇā punar samāsādya rathān su daṃśitāḥ śini pravīram jugupuḥ paraṃtapāḥ sametya pāñcāla rathāḥ mahā raṇe marut gaṇāḥ śakram iva ari nigrahe tatas abhavat yuddham atīva dāruṇam tava ahitānām tava sainikaiḥ saha ratha aśva mātaṅga vināśanam tathā yathā surāṇām asuraiḥ purā bhavat ratha dvipāḥ vāji padātayaḥ api vā bhramanti nānāvidha śastra veṣṭitāḥ tathā gate bhīmam abhīḥ tava ātmajaḥ sasāra rāja avarajaḥ kiran śaraiḥ paraspareṇa abhiniviṣṭa roṣayoḥ udagrayoḥ śambara śakrayoḥ yathā śaraiḥ śarīra anta karaiḥ su tejanaiḥ nijaghnatuḥ tau itaretaram bhṛśam lalāṭam api asya bibheda patriṇā śiraḥ ca kāyāt prajahāra sāratheḥ sa rāja putraḥ anyat avāpya kārmukam vṛkodaram dvādaśabhiḥ parābhinat svayam niyacchan turagān ajihmagaiḥ śaraiḥ ca bhīmam punar abhyavīvṛṣat saṃjayaḥ uvāca tatra akarot duṣkaram rāja putraḥ duḥśāsanaḥ tumule yudhyamānaḥ ciccheda bhīmasya dhanuḥ kṣureṇa ṣaḍbhiḥ śaraiḥ sārathim api avidhyat tayā aharat daśa dhanvantarāṇi duḥśāsanam bhīmasenaḥ prasahya tayā hataḥ patitaḥ vepamānaḥ duḥśāsanaḥ gadayā vegavatyā hayāḥ sa sūtāḥ ca hatāḥ narendra cūrṇīkṛtaḥ ca asya rathaḥ patantyā vidhvasta varma ābharaṇa ambara sraj viceṣṭamānaḥ bhṛśa vedanā ārtaḥ asim samuddhṛtya śitam su dhāram kaṇṭhe samākramya ca vepamānam utkṛtya vakṣaḥ patitasya bhūmau atha apibat śoṇitam asya koṣṇam āsvādya ca āsvādya ca vīkṣamāṇaḥ kruddhaḥ ativelam prajagāda vākyam evam bruvāṇam punar ādravantam āsvādya valgantam ati prahṛṣṭam ye bhīmasenam dadṛśuḥ tadānīm bhayena te api vyathitāḥ nipetuḥ ye ca api tatra āpatitāḥ manuṣyāḥ teṣām karebhyaḥ patitam ca śastram bhayāt ca saṃcukruśuḥ uccakais te nimīlita akṣāḥ dadṛśuḥ ca tat na ye tatra bhīmam dadṛśuḥ samantāt dauḥśāsanam tat rudhiram pibantam sarve palāyanta bhaya abhipannāḥ na ayam manuṣyaḥ iti bhāṣamāṇāḥ śṛṇvatām loka vīrāṇām idam vacanam abravīt eṣa te rudhiram kaṇṭhāt pibāmi puruṣa adhama brūhi idānīm su saṃrabdhaḥ punar gauḥ iti gauḥ iti pramāṇakoṭyām śayanam kālakūṭasya bhojanam daśanam ca ahibhiḥ kaṣṭam dāham ca jatu veśmani dyūtena rājya haraṇam araṇye vasatiḥ ca yā iṣu astrāṇi ca saṃgrāmeṣu asukhāni ca veśmani duḥkhāni etāni jānīmaḥ na sukhāni kadā cana dhṛtarāṣṭrasya daurātmyāt sa putrasya sadā vayam iti uktvā vacanam rājan jayam prāpya vṛkodaraḥ punar āha mahā rāja smayan tau keśava arjunau duḥśāsane yat raṇe saṃśrutam me tat vai sarvam kṛtam adyā iha vīrau adya eva dāsyāmi aparam dvitīyam duryodhanam yajña paśum viśasya śiraḥ mṛditvā ca padā durātmanaḥ etāvat uktvā vacanam prahṛṣṭaḥ nanāda ca uccais rudhira ārdra gātraḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca duḥśāsane tu nihate putrāḥ tava mahā rathāḥ mahā krodha viṣāḥ vīrāḥ samareṣu apalāyinaḥ daśa rājan mahā vīryaḥ bhīmam prācchādayan śaraiḥ ete sametya sahitāḥ bhrātṛ vyasana karśitāḥ bhīmasenam mahā bāhum mārgaṇaiḥ samavārayan sa vāryamāṇaḥ viśikhaiḥ samantāt taiḥ mahā rathaiḥ bhīmaḥ krodha abhirakta akṣaḥ kruddhaḥ kālaḥ iva ābabhau tān tu bhallaiḥ mahā vegaiḥ daśabhiḥ daśabhiḥ śitaiḥ hateṣu teṣu vīreṣu pradudrāva balam tava paśyataḥ sūtaputrasya pāṇḍavasya bhaya arditam tatas karṇaḥ mahā rāja praviveśa mahā raṇam dṛṣṭvā bhīmasya vikrāntam antakasya prajāsu iva tasya tu ākāra bhāva jñaḥ śalyaḥ samiti śobhanaḥ uvāca vacanam karṇam prāpta kālam ariṃdama ete dravanti rājānaḥ bhīmasena bhaya arditāḥ duryodhanaḥ ca saṃmūḍhaḥ bhrātṛ vyasana duḥkhitaḥ duḥśāsanasya rudhire pīyamāne mahātmanā kṛpa prabhṛtayaḥ karṇa hata śeṣāḥ ca sodarāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ labdhalakṣāḥ ca dhanaṃjaya purogamāḥ tvām eva abhimukhāḥ śūrāḥ yuddhāya samupāsthitāḥ sa tvam puruṣa śārdūla pauruṣe mahati sthitaḥ bhāraḥ hi dhārtarāṣṭreṇa tvayi sarvaḥ samarpitaḥ tvayi moha samāpanne pāṇḍavān abhidhāvati hṛdi mānuṣyakam bhāvam cakre yuddhāya su sthiram tatas kruddhaḥ vṛṣasenaḥ abhyadhāvat ātasthivāṃsam sva ratham hata arim vṛkodaram kālam iva ātta daṇḍam gadā hastam tvadīyān tam abhyadhāvan nakulaḥ pravīraḥ roṣāt amitram pratudan pṛṣatkaiḥ karṇasya putram samare prahṛṣṭam jiṣṇuḥ jighāṃsuḥ maghavā iva jambham karṇa ātmajasya iṣvasanam ca citram bhallena jāmbūnada paṭṭa naddham atha anyat ādāya dhanuḥ su śīghram karṇa ātmajaḥ pāṇḍavam abhyavidhyat divyaiḥ mahā astraiḥ nakulam mahā astraḥ duḥśāsanasya apacitim yiyāsuḥ karṇasya putraḥ nakulasya rājan sarvān aśvān akṣiṇot uttama astraiḥ vanāyu jān su kumārasya śubhrān alaṃkṛtān jātarūpeṇa śīghrān tatas hata aśvāt avaruhya yānāt ādāya carma ruciram ca aṣṭa candram ākāśa saṃkāśam asim gṛhītvā poplūyamānaḥ khaga vat cacāra tatas antarikṣe nṛ vara aśva nāgān ciccheda mārgān vicaran vicitrān te prāpatan asinā gām viśastāḥ dvi sāhasrāḥ viditāḥ yuddha śauṇḍāḥ nānādeśyāḥ su bhṛtāḥ satya saṃdhāḥ ekena śīghram nakulena kṛttāḥ sāra īpsunā iva uttama candanāḥ te krīḍantam aṣṭādaśabhiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ vivyādha vīram sa cukopa viddhaḥ tatas abhyadhāvat samare jighāṃsuḥ karṇa ātmajam pāṇḍu sutaḥ nṛ vīraḥ tasya āyasam niśitam tīkṣṇa dhāram asim vikośam guru bhāra sāham kṣipram śaraiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ amitra sāhaḥ cakarta khaḍgam niśitaiḥ su dhāraiḥ punar ca pītaiḥ niśitaiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ stanāntare gāḍham atha abhyavidhyat sa bhīmasenasya ratham hata aśvaḥ mādrī sutaḥ karṇa suta abhitaptaḥ āpupluve siṃhaḥ iva acala agram saṃprekṣamāṇasya dhanaṃjayasya pavana dhuta patākāḥ hrādinaḥ valgita aśvāḥ vara puruṣa niyattāḥ te rathāḥ śīghram īyuḥ drupada suta variṣṭhāḥ pañca śaineya ṣaṣṭhāḥ drupada duhitṛ putrāḥ pañca ca amitra sāhāḥ dvirada ratha nara aśvān sūdayantaḥ tvadīyān bhujaga pati nikāśaiḥ mārgaṇaiḥ ātta śastrāḥ śakuni śuka vṛkāḥ ca krātha devāvṛdhau ca dvirada jalada ghoṣaiḥ syandanaiḥ kārmukaiḥ ca su kalpitāḥ haimavatāḥ mada utkaṭā raṇa abhikāmaiḥ kṛtibhiḥ samāsthitāḥ suvarṇa jāla avatatāḥ babhuḥ gajāḥ tathā yathā vai jaladāḥ sa vidyutaḥ kuṇinda putraḥ daśabhiḥ mahā āyasaiḥ kṛpam sa sūta aśvam apīḍayat bhṛśam tatas kuṇindeṣu hateṣu teṣu atha prahṛṣṭa rūpāḥ tava te mahā rathāḥ bhṛśam pradadhmuḥ lavaṇa ambu saṃbhavān parān ca bāṇāsana pāṇayaḥ abhyayus atha abhavat yuddham atīva dāruṇam punar kurūṇām saha pāṇḍu sṛñjayaiḥ śara asi śakti ṛṣṭi gadā paraśvadhaiḥ nara aśva nāga asu haram bhṛśa ākulam ratha aśva mātaṅga padātibhiḥ tatas parasparam viprahatāḥ apatan kṣitau yathā sa vidyut stanitāḥ balāhakāḥ samāsthitāḥ digbhyaḥ iva ugra mārutaiḥ tatas śatānīka hatān mahā gajān tathā rathān patti gaṇān ca tāvakān jaghāna bhojaḥ ca hayān atha apatan viśastra kṛttāḥ kṛtavarmaṇā dvipāḥ atha apare drauṇi śara āhatāḥ dvipāḥ trayaḥ sa sarva āyudha yodha ketavaḥ nipetuḥ urvyām vyasavaḥ prapātitāḥ tathā yathā vajra hatāḥ mahā acalāḥ tava ātmajam tasya tava ātmajaḥ śaraiḥ śitaiḥ śarīram bibhide dvipam ca tam sa nāga rājaḥ saha rāja sūnunā papāta raktam bahu sarvatas kṣaran sa vāji sūta iṣvasanaḥ tathā apatat yathā mahā vāta hataḥ mahā drumaḥ vṛkaḥ dvipa stham girirāja vāsinam bhṛśam śaraiḥ dvādaśabhiḥ parābhinat tatas vṛkam sa aśva ratham mahā javam tvaran caturbhiḥ caraṇe vyapothayat sa ca api devāvṛdha sūnuḥ arditaḥ papāta nunnaḥ sahadeva sūnunā viṣāṇa potra apara gātra ghātinā gajena hantum śakuneḥ kuṇinda jaḥ jagāma vegena bhṛśa ardayan ca tam tatas asya gāndhāra patiḥ śiraḥ aharat tatas śatānīka hatāḥ mahā gajāḥ hayāḥ rathāḥ patti gaṇāḥ ca tāvakāḥ suparṇa vāta prahatāḥ yathā nagāḥ tathā gatāḥ gām avaśāḥ vicūrṇitāḥ tatas asya kāyāt nicakarta nākuliḥ śiraḥ kṣureṇa ambuja saṃnibha ānanam tatas śatānīkam avidhyat āśugaiḥ tribhiḥ śitaiḥ karṇa sutaḥ arjunam tribhiḥ tribhiḥ ca bhīmam nakulam ca saptabhiḥ janārdanam dvādaśabhiḥ ca sāyakaiḥ tat asya karma ati manuṣya karmaṇaḥ samīkṣya hṛṣṭāḥ kuravaḥ abhyapūjayan tatas kirīṭī para vīra ghātī hata aśvam ālokya nara pravīram tam āpatantam nara vīram ugram mahā āhave bāṇa sahasra dhāriṇam nanāda nādam su mahā anubhāvaḥ viddhvā iva śakram namuciḥ purā vai tathā eva kṛṣṇam navabhiḥ samārdayat punar ca pārtham daśabhiḥ śita agraiḥ tatas kirīṭī raṇa mūrdhni kopāt kṛtvā tri śākhām bhrukuṭim lalāṭe mumoca bāṇān viśikhān mahātmā vivyādha ca enam daśabhiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ marmasu asaktam prasabham kirīṭī sa pārtha bāṇa abhihataḥ papāta rathāt vibāhuḥ viśirāḥ dharāyām su puṣpitaḥ parṇa dharaḥ atikāyaḥ vāta īritaḥ śālaḥ iva adri śṛṅgāt tam prekṣya bāṇa abhihatam patantam rathāt sutam sūtajaḥ kṣiprakārī ratham rathena āśu jagāma vegāt kirīṭinaḥ putra vadha abhitaptaḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca vṛṣasenam hatam dṛṣṭvā śoka amarṣa samanvitaḥ muktvā śoka udbhavam vāri netrābhyām sahasā vṛṣaḥ yuddhāya āmarṣa tāmra akṣaḥ samāhūya dhanaṃjayam tau rathau sūrya saṃkāśau vaiyāghra parivāraṇau śveta aśvau puruṣa ādityau āsthitau ari mardanau śuśubhāte mahātmānau candra ādityau yathā divi tau dṛṣṭvā vismayam jagmuḥ sarva bhūtāni māriṣa hasti kakṣyām ca karṇasya vānaram ca kirīṭinaḥ tau rathau saṃprasaktau ca dṛṣṭvā bhārata pārthivāḥ siṃhanāda ravān cakruḥ sādhuvādān ca puṣkalān śrutvā tu dvairatham tābhyām tatra yodhāḥ samantataḥ ājagmuḥ kuravaḥ tatra vāditra anugatāḥ tadā karṇam praharṣayantaḥ ca śaṅkhān dadhmuḥ ca puṣkalān tathā eva pāṇḍavāḥ sarve harṣayantaḥ dhanaṃjayam tūrya śaṅkha ninādena diśaḥ sarvāḥ vyanādayan kṣveḍita āsphoṭita utkruṣṭaiḥ tumulam sarvatas abhavat bāhu ghoṣāḥ ca vīrāṇām karṇa arjuna samāgame tau dṛṣṭvā puruṣa vyāghrau ratha sthau rathinām varau pragṛhīta mahā cāpau śara śakti gadā āyudhau varmiṇau baddha nistriṃśau śveta aśvau śaṅkha śobhinau tūṇīra vara saṃpannau dvau api sma su darśanau āśīviṣa sama prakhyau yama kāla antaka upamau ubhau ca sadṛśau yuddhe śambara amararājayoḥ sārathī pravarau ca eva tayoḥ āstām mahā balau tau tu dṛṣṭvā mahā rāja rājamānau mahā rathau siddha cāraṇa saṃghānām vismayaḥ samapadyata dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ tatas karṇam sa balāḥ bharata ṛṣabha parivavruḥ mahātmānam kṣipram āhava śobhinam tathā eva pāṇḍavāḥ hṛṣṭāḥ dhṛṣṭadyumna purogamāḥ tāvakānām raṇe karṇaḥ glahe āsīt viśām pate tathā eva pāṇḍaveyānām glahaḥ pārthaḥ abhavat yudhi tatra eṣām glahamānānām dhruvau jaya parājayau tābhyām dyūtam samāyattam vijayāya itarasmai vā asmākam paṇḍavānām ca sthitānām raṇa mūrdhani tau ubhau prajihīrṣetām indra vṛtrau iva abhitas bhīma rūpa dharau āstām mahā dhūmau iva grahau tatas antarikṣe sa ākṣepāḥ vivādāḥ bharata ṛṣabha mithas bhedāḥ ca bhūtānām āsan karṇa arjuna antare vyāśrayanta diśaḥ bhinnāḥ sarva lokāḥ ca māriṣa deva dānava gandharvāḥ piśāca uraga rākṣasāḥ pratipakṣa graham cakruḥ karṇa arjuna samāgame dyauḥ āsīt karṇataḥ vyagrā sa nakṣatrā viśām pate bhūmiḥ viśālā pārthasya mātā putrasya bhārata vṛkṣāḥ ca oṣadhayaḥ tatra vyāśrayanta kirīṭinam asurāḥ yātudhānāḥ ca guhyakāḥ ca paraṃtapa karṇataḥ samapadyanta khecarāṇi vayāṃsi ca ratnāni nidhayaḥ sarve vedāḥ ca ākhyāna pañcamāḥ sa upaveda upaniṣadaḥ sa rahasyāḥ sa saṃgrahāḥ vāsukiḥ citrasenaḥ ca takṣakaḥ ca upatakṣakaḥ parvatāḥ ca tathā sarve kādraveyāḥ ca sa anvayāḥ viṣavantaḥ mahā roṣāḥ nāgāḥ ca arjunataḥ abhavan airāvatāḥ saurabheyāḥ vaiśāleyāḥ ca bhoginaḥ īhāmṛgāḥ vyāḍa mṛgāḥ maṅgalyāḥ ca mṛga dvijāḥ pārthasya vijayam rājan sarve eva abhisaṃśritāḥ vasavaḥ marutaḥ sādhyāḥ rudrāḥ viśve aśvinau tathā dhanaṃjayam upājagmuḥ ādityāḥ karṇataḥ abhavan devāḥ tu pitṛbhiḥ sārdham sa gaṇa arjunataḥ abhavan yamaḥ vaiśravaṇaḥ ca eva varuṇaḥ ca yatas arjunaḥ deva brahma nṛpa ṛṣīṇām gaṇāḥ pāṇḍavataḥ abhavan prāveyāḥ saha mauneyaiḥ gandharva apsarasām gaṇāḥ īhāmṛga vyāḍa mṛgaiḥ dvipāḥ ca ratha pattibhiḥ uhyamānāḥ tathā meghaiḥ vāyunā ca manīṣiṇaḥ didṛkṣavaḥ samājagmuḥ karṇa arjuna samāgamam deva dānava gandharvāḥ nāgāḥ yakṣāḥ patatriṇaḥ tapaḥ vidyāḥ tathā oṣadhyaḥ nānā rūpa ambara tviṣaḥ bhavena avasthitaḥ yānam divyam tam deśam abhyayāt dṛṣṭvā prajāpatim devāḥ svayaṃbhuvam upāgaman karṇa arjuna vināśena mā naśyatu akhilam jagat brahma īśānau atho vākyam ūcatuḥ tridaśeśvaram manasvī balavān śūraḥ kṛtāstraḥ ca tapodhanaḥ atikramet ca māhātmyāt diṣṭam etasya paryayāt na vidyate vyavasthānam kṛṣṇayoḥ kruddhayoḥ kva cit sraṣṭārau hi asataḥ ca ubhau sataḥ ca puruṣa ṛṣabhau nara nārāyaṇau etau purāṇau ṛṣi sattamau karṇaḥ lokān ayam mukhyān prāpnotu puruṣa ṛṣabhaḥ vīraḥ vaikartanaḥ śūraḥ vijayaḥ tu astu kṛṣṇayoḥ vasūnām ca sa loka tvam marutām vā samāpnuyāt sahitaḥ droṇa bhīṣmābhyām nāka loke mahīyatām iti uktaḥ devadevābhyām sahasrākṣaḥ abravīt vacaḥ āmantrya sarva bhūtāni brahma īśāna anuśāsanāt tat tathā na anyathā tat hi tiṣṭhadhvam gata manyavaḥ iti śrutvā indra vacanam sarva bhūtāni māriṣa vyasṛjan ca sugandhīni nānā rūpāṇi khāt tathā puṣpa varṣāṇi vibudhāḥ deva tūryāṇi avādayan didṛkṣavaḥ ca apratimam dvairatham nara siṃhayoḥ samāgatāḥ loka vīrāḥ śaṅkhān dadhmuḥ pṛthak pṛthak vāsudeva arjunau vīrau karṇa śalyau ca bhārata karṇasya āśīviṣa nibhā ratna sāravatī dṛḍhā kapi śreṣṭhaḥ tu pārthasya vyādita āsyaḥ bhayaṃkaraḥ bhīṣayan eva daṃṣṭrābhiḥ durnirīkṣyaḥ raviḥ yathā yuddha abhilāṣukaḥ bhūtvā dhvajaḥ gāṇḍīvadhanvanaḥ nakhaiḥ ca daśanaiḥ ca eva garuḍaḥ pannagam yathā su kiṅkiṇīka ābharaṇā kāla pāśa upama āyasī avidhyat puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ śalyam nayana sāyakaiḥ sa ca api puṇḍarīkākṣam tathā eva abhisamaikṣata tatra ajayat vāsudevaḥ śalyam nayana sāyakaiḥ karṇam ca api ajayat dṛṣṭyā kuntī putraḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ atha abravīt sūtaputraḥ śalyam ābhāṣya sa smitam śalyaḥ uvāca yadi karṇa raṇe hanyāt adya tvām śvetavāhanaḥ ubhau eka rathena aham hanyām mādhava pāṇḍavau saṃjayaḥ uvāca tam prahasya abravīt kṛṣṇaḥ pārtham param idam vacaḥ patet divākaraḥ sthānāt śīryeta anekadhā kṣitiḥ hanyām karṇam tathā śalyam bāhubhyām eva saṃyuge iti kṛṣṇa vacaḥ śrutvā prahasan kapiketanaḥ arjunaḥ pratyuvāca idam kṛṣṇam akliṣṭa kāriṇam mama api etau aparyāptau karṇa śalyau janārdana sa patākā dhvajam karṇam sa śalya ratha vājinam draṣṭāsi adya śaraiḥ karṇam raṇe kṛttam anekadhā adya enam sa ratham sa aśvam sa śakti kavaca āyudham na hi me śāmyate vairam kṛṣṇām yat prāhasat purā adya draṣṭāsi govinda karṇam unmathitam mayā adya tāḥ madhurāḥ vācaḥ śrotāsi madhusūdana adya abhimanyu jananīm anṛṇaḥ sāntvayiṣyasi kuntīm pitṛṣvasāram ca saṃprahṛṣṭaḥ janārdana adya bāṣpa mukhīm kṛṣṇām sāntvayiṣyasi mādhava vāgbhiḥ ca amṛta kalpābhiḥ dharmarājam yudhiṣṭhiram saṃjayaḥ uvāca brahmarṣi rājarṣi suparṇa juṣṭam babhau viyat vismayanīya rūpam nānadyamānam ninadaiḥ manojñaiḥ vāditra gīta stutibhiḥ ca nṛttaiḥ sarve antarikṣe dadṛśuḥ manuṣyāḥ kha sthān ca tān vismayanīya rūpān tatas prahṛṣṭāḥ kuru pāṇḍu yodhāḥ vāditra patra āyudha siṃhanādaiḥ nānā aśva mātaṅga ratha ayuta ākulam vara asi śakti ṛṣṭini pāta duḥsaham abhīru juṣṭam hata deha saṃkulam raṇa ajiram lohita raktam ābabhau tathā pravṛtte astrabhṛtām parābhave dhanaṃjayaḥ ca ādhirathiḥ ca sāyakaiḥ diśaḥ ca sainyam ca śitaiḥ ajihmagaiḥ parasparam prorṇuvatuḥ sma daṃśitau bhayāt tu tau eva rathau samāśrayan tamonudau khe prasṛtāḥ iva aṃśavaḥ mṛdaṅga bherī paṇava ānaka svanaiḥ ninādite bhārata śaṅkha nisvanaiḥ sa siṃhanādau babhatuḥ nara uttamau śaśāṅka sūryau iva megha saṃplave didhakṣamāṇau sa carācaram jagat yuga asta sūryau iva duḥsahau raṇe tatas mahā astrāṇi mahā dhanurdharau vimuñcamānau iṣubhiḥ bhayānakaiḥ tatas visasruḥ punar arditāḥ śaraiḥ nara uttamābhyām kuru pāṇḍava āśrayāḥ sa nāga patti aśva rathāḥ diśaḥ gatāḥ tathā yathā siṃha bhayāt vanaukasaḥ mahā rathāḥ pañca dhanaṃjaya acyutau śaraiḥ śarīra anta karaiḥ atāḍayan dhanūṃṣi teṣām iṣudhīn hayān dhvajān rathān ca sūtān ca dhanaṃjayaḥ śaraiḥ atha abhyadhāvan tvaritāḥ śatam rathāḥ śatam ca nāga arjunam ātatāyinaḥ śakāḥ tukhārāḥ yavanāḥ ca sādinaḥ saha eva kāmboja varaiḥ jighāṃsavaḥ vara āyudhān pāṇi gatān karaiḥ saha kṣuraiḥ nyakṛntan tvaritāḥ śirāṃsi ca hayān ca nāgān ca rathān ca yudhyatām dhanaṃjayaḥ śatru gaṇam tam akṣiṇot tatas antarikṣe sura tūrya nisvanāḥ sa sādhuvādāḥ hṛṣitaiḥ samīritāḥ nipetuḥ api uttama puṣpa vṛṣṭayaḥ su rūpa gandhāḥ pavana īritāḥ śivāḥ tat adbhutam deva manuṣya sākṣikam samīkṣya bhūtāni visiṣmiyuḥ nṛpa athā bravīt droṇa sutaḥ tava ātmajam karam kareṇa pratipīḍya sāntvayan aham tu avadhyaḥ mama ca api mātulaḥ praśādhi rājyam saha pāṇḍavaiḥ ciram tvayā ca pārthaiḥ ca paraspareṇa vrajantu śeṣāḥ sva purāṇi pārthivāḥ nivṛtta vairāḥ ca bhavantu sainikāḥ idam ca dṛṣṭam jagatā saha tvayā kṛtam yat ekena kirīṭamālinā tava anuyātrām ca tathā kariṣyati prasīda rājan jagataḥ śamāya vai mama api mānaḥ paramaḥ sadā tvayi bravīmi atas tvām paramāt ca sauhṛdāt nivārayiṣyāmi hi karṇam api aham yadā bhavān sa praṇayaḥ bhaviṣyati pratāpataḥ ca upanatam caturvidham tat asti sarvam tvayi pāṇḍaveṣu ca yathā bhavān āha sakhe tathā eva tat mama api ca jñāpayataḥ vacaḥ śṛṇu nihatya duḥśāsanam uktavān bahu prasahya śārdūla vat eṣa durmatiḥ tam evam uktvā abhyanunīya ca asakṛt tava ātmajaḥ svān anuśāsti sainikān samāghnata abhidravata ahitān imān sa bāṇa śabdān kim u joṣam āsyate saṃjayaḥ uvāca balāhakena iva yathā balāhakaḥ yadṛcchayā vā giriṇā giriḥ yathā pravṛddha śṛṅga druma vīrudh oṣadhī pravṛddha nānāvidha parvata okasau śaraiḥ vibhugna aṅga niyantṛ vāhanaḥ su duḥsahaḥ anyaiḥ paṭu śoṇita udakaḥ bhujāḥ sa vajra aṅgulayaḥ samucchritāḥ sa siṃhanādāḥ hṛṣitaiḥ didṛkṣubhiḥ chindhi asya mūrdhānam alam cireṇa śraddhām ca rājyāt dhṛtarāṣṭra sūnoḥ tathā asmākam bahavaḥ tatra yodhāḥ karṇam tadā yāhi yāhi iti avocan jahi arjunam karṇa tatas sa cīrāḥ punar vanam yāntu cirāya pārthāḥ parasparam tau viśikhaiḥ su tīkṣṇaiḥ tatakṣatuḥ sūtaputraḥ arjunaḥ ca a mṛṣyamāṇaḥ ca mahā vimarde tatra akrudhyat bhīmasenaḥ mahātmā atha abravīt pāṇinā pāṇim āghnan saṃdaṣṭa oṣṭhaḥ nṛtyati vādayan iva katham nu tvām sūtaputraḥ kirīṭin mahā iṣubhiḥ daśabhiḥ avidhyat agre yayā dhṛtyā sarva bhūtāni ajaiṣīḥ grāsam dadat vahnaye khāṇḍave tvam tayā dhṛtyā sūtaputram jahi tvam aham vā enam gadayā pothayiṣye athā bravīt vāsudevaḥ api pārtham dṛṣṭvā ratheṣūn pratihanyamānān amīmṛdat sarvathā te adya karṇaḥ hi astraiḥ astrāṇi kim idam kirīṭin sa vīra kim muhyasi na avadhīyase yayā dhṛtyā nihatam tāmasa astram yuge yuge rākṣasāḥ ca api ghorāḥ dambhodbhavāḥ ca asurāḥ ca āhaveṣu tayā dhṛtyā tvam jahi sūtaputram mayā nisṛṣṭena sudarśanena kirāta rūpī bhagavān yayā ca tvayā mahatyā paritoṣitaḥ abhūt tām tvam dhṛtim vīra punar gṛhītvā saha anubandham jahi sūtaputram tatas mahīm sāgara mekhalām tvam sa pattanām grāmavatīm samṛddhām prayaccha rājñe nihata ari saṃghām yaśaḥ ca pārtha atulam āpnuhi tvam saṃcoditaḥ bhīma janārdanābhyām smṛtvā tadā ātmānam avekṣya sattvam prāduṣkaromi eṣa mahā astram ugram śivāya lokasya vadhāya sauteḥ tatas diśaḥ ca pradiśaḥ ca sarvāḥ samāvṛṇot sāyakaiḥ bhūri tejāḥ sasarja bāṇān bharata ṛṣabhaḥ api śataṃśatān eka vat āśu vegān vaikartanena api tathā āji madhye sahasraśas bāṇa gaṇāḥ visṛṣṭāḥ te ghoṣiṇaḥ pāṇḍavam abhyupeyuḥ parjanya muktāḥ iva vāri dhārāḥ sa bhīmasenam ca janārdanam ca kirīṭinam ca api amanuṣya karmā sa karṇa bāṇa abhihataḥ kirīṭī bhīmam tathā prekṣya janārdanam ca amṛṣyamāṇaḥ punar eva pārthaḥ śarān daśa aṣṭau ca samudbabarha tatas ratha agrāt apatat prabhagnaḥ paraśvadhaiḥ śālaḥ iva abhikṛttaḥ punar ca karṇam tribhiḥ aṣṭabhiḥ ca dvābhyām caturbhiḥ daśabhiḥ ca viddhvā catuḥśatān dviradān sa āyudhīyān hatvā rathān aṣṭaśatam jaghāna sahasram aśvān ca punar ca sādīn aṣṭau sahasrāṇi ca pattivīrān dṛṣṭvā āji mukhyau atha yudhyamānau didṛkṣavaḥ śūra varau ari ghnau karṇam ca pārtham ca niyamya vāhān kha sthāḥ mahī sthāḥ ca jana avatasthuḥ tatas dhanuḥ jyā sahasā atikṛṣṭā su ghoṣam ācchidyata pāṇḍavasya tasmin kṣaṇe sūtaputraḥ tu pārtham samācinot kṣudrakāṇām śatena ṣaṣṭyā nārācaiḥ vāsudevam bibheda tad antaram somakāḥ prādravanta su saṃrabdhaḥ karṇa śara kṣata aṅgaḥ raṇe pārthaḥ somakān pratyagṛhṇāt na pakṣiṇaḥ saṃpatanti antarikṣe kṣepīyasā astreṇa kṛte andhakāre śalyam ca pārthaḥ daśabhiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ bhṛśam tanutre prahasan avidhyat sa pārtha bāṇāsana vega nunnaiḥ dṛḍha āhataḥ patribhiḥ ugra vegaiḥ vibhinna gātraḥ kṣataja ukṣita aṅgaḥ karṇaḥ babhau rudraḥ iva ātata iṣuḥ śarān tu pañca jvalitān iva uragān vegena gām āviviśuḥ su vegāḥ snātvā ca karṇa abhimukhāḥ pratīyuḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ te nyapatan pṛthivyām mahā ahayaḥ takṣaka putra pakṣāḥ tatas prajajvāla kirīṭamālī krodhena kakṣam pradahan iva agniḥ sa karṇam ākarṇa vikṛṣṭa sṛṣṭaiḥ śaraiḥ śarīra anta karaiḥ jvaladbhiḥ tatas śara oghaiḥ pradiśaḥ diśaḥ ca ravi prabhā karṇa rathaḥ ca rājan adṛśyaḥ āsīt kupite dhanaṃjaye tuṣāra nīhāra vṛtam yathā nabhaḥ sa cakrarakṣān atha pādarakṣān puraḥsarān pṛṣṭhagopān ca sarvān dvi sāhasrān samare savyasācī kuru pravīrān ṛṣabhaḥ kurūṇām kṣaṇena sarvān sa ratha aśva sūtān nināya rājan kṣayam eka vīraḥ atha apalāyanta vihāya karṇam tava ātmajāḥ kuravaḥ ca avaśiṣṭāḥ hatān avākīrya śara kṣatān ca lālapyamānān tanayān pitṝn ca sa sarvatas prekṣya diśaḥ viśūnyāḥ bhaya avadīrṇaiḥ kurubhiḥ vihīnaḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca tatas apayātāḥ śara pāta mātram avasthitāḥ kuravaḥ bhinna senāḥ vidyut prakāśam dadṛśuḥ samantāt dhanaṃjaya astram samudīryamāṇam kruddhena pārthena tadā āśu sṛṣṭam vadhāya karṇasya mahā vimarde rāmāt upāttena mahā mahimnā ātharvaṇena ari vināśanena anyonyam āsādayatoḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ viṣāṇa ghātaiḥ dvipayoḥ iva ugraiḥ sadā arcitam candana cūrṇa śāyinam suvarṇa nālī śayanam mahā viṣam pradīptam airāvata vaṃśa saṃbhavam śiraḥ jihīrṣuḥ yudhi phalgunasya na karṇa grīvām iṣuḥ eṣa prāpsyate saṃlakṣya saṃdhatsva śaram śiraḥ ghnam atha abravīt krodha saṃrakta netraḥ karṇaḥ śalyam saṃdhita iṣuḥ prasahya na saṃdhatte dvis śaram śalya karṇaḥ na mādṛśāḥ śāṭhya yuktāḥ bhavanti tathā evam uktvā visasarja tam śaram balāhakam varṣa ghana abhipūjitam saṃdhīyamānam bhujagam dṛṣṭvā karṇena mādhavaḥ ākramya syandanam padbhyām balena balinām varaḥ avagāḍhe rathe bhūmau jānubhyām agaman hayāḥ tatas śaraḥ saḥ abhyahanat kirīṭam tasya dhīmataḥ atha arjunasya uttama gātra bhūṣaṇam viśrutam divākara indu jvalana graha tviṣam suvarṇa muktā maṇi jāla bhūṣitam puraṃdara artham tapasā prayatnataḥ svayam kṛtam yat bhuvanasya sūnunā mahārha rūpam dviṣatām bhayaṃkaram vibhāti ca atyartha sukham sugandhi tat nijaghnuṣe deva ripūn sureśvaraḥ svayam dadau yat su manāḥ kirīṭine hara ambupa ākhaṇḍala vittagoptṛbhiḥ pināka pāśa aśani sāyaka uttamaiḥ tatas kirīṭam bahu ratna maṇḍitam jahāra nāgaḥ arjuna mūrdhataḥ balāt mahī viyat dyauḥ salilāni vāyunā vibhāti saṃpūrṇa marīci bhāsvatā śiraḥ gatena udaya parvataḥ yathā tam abravīt viddhi kṛta āgasam me kṛṣṇa adya mātuḥ vadha jāta vairam tatas kṛṣṇaḥ pārtham uvāca saṃkhye mahā uragam kṛta vairam jahi tvam saḥ evam uktaḥ madhusūdanena gāṇḍīvadhanvā ripuṣu ugra dhanvā uvāca kaḥ nu eṣa mama adya nāgaḥ svayam yaḥ āgāt garuḍasya vaktram kṛṣṇaḥ uvāca yaḥ asau tvayā khāṇḍave citrabhānum saṃtarpayānena dhanurdhareṇa tatas tu jiṣṇuḥ parihṛtya śeṣān ciccheda ṣaḍbhiḥ niśitaiḥ su dhāraiḥ tasmin muhūrte daśabhiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ śilā śitaiḥ barhiṇa vājitaiḥ ca vivyādha karṇaḥ puruṣa pravīram dhanaṃjayam tiryak avekṣamāṇam nārācam āśīviṣa tulya vegam ākarṇapūrṇa āyatam utsasarja karṇasya pītvā rudhiram viveśa vasuṃdharām śoṇita vāja digdhaḥ tatas vṛṣaḥ bāṇa nipāta kopitaḥ mahā uragaḥ daṇḍa vighaṭṭitaḥ yathā tathā āśukārī vyasṛjat śara uttamān mahā viṣaḥ sarpaḥ iva uttamam viṣam śareṇa ghoreṇa punar ca pāṇḍavam vibhidya karṇaḥ abhyanadat jahāsa ca tam asya harṣam mamṛṣe na pāṇḍavaḥ bibheda marmāṇi tatas asya marma vid tatas śarāṇām navatīḥ nava arjunaḥ sasarja karṇe antaka daṇḍa saṃnibhāḥ śaraiḥ bhṛśa āyasta tanuḥ pravivyathe tathā yathā vajra vidāritaḥ acalaḥ maṇi praveka uttama vajra hāṭakaiḥ alaṃkṛtam ca asya varāṅga bhūṣaṇam su dīrgha kālena tat asya pāṇḍavaḥ kṣaṇena bāṇaiḥ bahudhā vyaśātayat sa tam vivarmāṇam atha uttama iṣubhiḥ śaraiḥ caturbhiḥ kupitaḥ parābhinat dṛḍha āhataḥ patribhiḥ ugra vegaiḥ pārthena karṇaḥ vividhaiḥ śita agraiḥ sa aśvam tu karṇam sa ratham kirīṭī samācinot bhārata vatsadantaiḥ pracchādayām āsa diśaḥ ca bāṇaiḥ sarva prayatnāt tapanīya puṅkhaiḥ sa vatsadantaiḥ pṛthu pīna vakṣāḥ samācitaḥ sma ādhirathiḥ vibhāti su puṣpita aśoka palāśa śālmaliḥ yathā acalaḥ spandana candana āyutaḥ śaraiḥ śarīre bahudhā samarpitaiḥ vibhāti karṇaḥ samare viśām pate mahīruhaiḥ ācita sānu kandaraḥ yathā mahā indraḥ śubha karṇikāravān sa bāṇa saṃghān dhanuṣā vyavāsṛjan vibhāti karṇaḥ śara jāla raśmivān bāhu antarāt ādhiratheḥ vimuktān bāṇān mahā ahīn iva dīpyamānān vyadhvaṃsayan arjuna bāhu muktāḥ śarāḥ samāsādya diśaḥ śita agrāḥ ghūrṇe rathe brāhmaṇasya abhiśāpāt rāmāt upātte apratibhāti ca astre a mṛṣyamāṇaḥ vyasanāni tāni hastau vidhunvan sa vigarhamāṇaḥ evam bruvan praskhalita aśva sūtaḥ vicālyamānaḥ arjuna śastra pātaiḥ indra aśani samān ghorān asṛjat pāvaka upamān kampita ātmā tathā karṇaḥ śaktyā ceṣṭām adarśayat aindra astram arjunaḥ ca api tat dṛṣṭvā abhinyamantrayat gāṇḍīvam jyām ca bāṇān ca anumantrya dhanaṃjayaḥ asṛjat śara varṣāṇi varṣāṇi iva puraṃdaraḥ tatas tejaḥ mayāḥ bāṇāḥ rathāt pārthasya niḥsṛtāḥ prādurāsan mahā vīryāḥ karṇasya ratham antikāt tān karṇaḥ tu agratas abhyastān moghān cakre mahā rathaḥ tatas abravīt vṛṣṇi vīraḥ tasmin astre vināśite visṛja astram param pārtha rādheyaḥ grasate śarān chādayitvā tatas bāṇaiḥ karṇam prabhrāmya ca arjunaḥ tasya karṇaḥ śaraiḥ kruddhaḥ ciccheda jyām su tejanaiḥ tatas jyām avadhāya anyām anumṛjya ca pāṇḍavaḥ śaraiḥ avākirat karṇam dīpyamānaiḥ sahasraśas tasya jyā chedanam karṇaḥ jyā avadhānam ca saṃyuge cakre ca abhyadhikam pārthāt sva vīryam pratidarśayan tatas kṛṣṇaḥ arjunam dṛṣṭvā karṇa astreṇa abhipīḍitam tatas anyam agni sadṛśam śaram sarpa viṣa upamam raudram astram samādāya kṣeptu kāmaḥ kirīṭavān saḥ abravīt arjunam ca api muhūrtam kṣama pāṇḍava madhye cakram avagrastam dṛṣṭvā daivāt idam mama pārtha kāpuruṣa ācīrṇam abhisaṃdhim vivarjaya prakīrṇa keśe vimukhe brāhmaṇe ca kṛtāñjalau a bāṇe bhraṣṭa kavace bhraṣṭa bhagna āyudhe tathā na śūrāḥ praharanti ājau na rājñe pārthivāḥ tathā na vāsudevāt tvattaḥ vā pāṇḍaveya bibhemi aham tvam hi kṣatriya dāyādaḥ mahā kula vivardhanaḥ smṛtvā dharma upadeśam tvam muhūrtam kṣama pāṇḍava saṃjayaḥ uvāca prāyeṇa nīcāḥ vyasaneṣu magnāḥ nindanti daivam kukṛtam na tat tat yat draupadīm eka vastrām sabhāyām ānāyya tvam ca eva suyodhanaḥ ca duḥśāsanaḥ śakuniḥ saubalaḥ ca na te karṇa pratyabhāt tatra dharmaḥ yadā sabhāyām kaunteyam an akṣa jñam yudhiṣṭhiram akṣa jñaḥ śakuniḥ jetā tadā dharmaḥ kva te gataḥ yadā rajasvalām kṛṣṇām duḥśāsana vaśe sthitām sabhāyām prāhasaḥ karṇa kva te dharmaḥ tadā gataḥ rājya lubdhaḥ punar karṇa samāhvayasi pāṇḍavam gāndhāra rājam āśritya kva te dharmaḥ tadā gataḥ manyuḥ abhyāviśat tīvraḥ smṛtvā tat tat dhanaṃjayam tam samīkṣya tatas karṇaḥ brahmāstreṇa dhanaṃjayam tat astram astreṇa āvārya prajahāra asya pāṇḍavaḥ vāruṇena tatas karṇaḥ śamayām āsa pāvakam jīmūtaiḥ ca diśaḥ sarvāḥ cakre timira durdināḥ pāṇḍaveyaḥ tu asaṃbhrāntaḥ vāyavya astreṇa vīryavān apovāha tadā abhrāṇi rādheyasya prapaśyataḥ tam hasti kakṣyā pravaram ca bāṇaiḥ suvarṇa muktā maṇi vajra mṛṣṭam tatas kṣureṇa ādhiratheḥ kirīṭī suvarṇa puṅkhena śitena yattaḥ yaśaḥ ca dharmaḥ ca jayaḥ ca māriṣa priyāṇi sarvāṇi ca tena ketunā tadā kurūṇām hṛdayāni ca apatan babhūva hāhā iti ca nisvanaḥ mahān atha tvaran karṇa vadhāya pāṇḍavaḥ mahā indra vajra anala daṇḍa saṃnibham ādatta pārthaḥ añjalikam niṣaṅgāt sahasraraśmeḥ iva raśmim uttamam marma chidam śoṇita māṃsa digdham vaiśvānara arka pratimam mahārham nara aśva nāga asu haram tri aratnim ṣaṣ vājam añjaḥ gatim ugra vegam pināka nārāyaṇa cakra saṃnibham bhayaṃkaram prāṇabhṛtām vināśanam yuktvā mahā astreṇa pareṇa mantra vid vikṛṣya gāṇḍīvam uvāca sa svanam ayam mahā astraḥ apratimaḥ dhṛtaḥ śaraḥ śarīra bhid ca asu haraḥ ca durhṛdaḥ tapaḥ asti taptam guravaḥ ca toṣitāḥ mayā yat iṣṭam suhṛdām tathā śrutam anena satyena nihantu ayam śaraḥ su daṃśitaḥ karṇam arim mama ajitaḥ iti ūcivān tam sa mumoca bāṇam dhanaṃjayaḥ karṇa vadhāya ghoram kṛtyām atharva āṅgirasīm iva ugrām dīptām asahyām yudhi mṛtyunā api bruvan kirīṭī tam ati prahṛṣṭaḥ ayam śaraḥ me vijaya āvahaḥ astu jighāṃsuḥ arka indu sama prabhāvaḥ karṇam samāptim nayatām yamāya tena iṣu varyeṇa kirīṭamālī prahṛṣṭa rūpaḥ vijaya āvahena jighāṃsuḥ arka indu sama prabheṇa cakre viṣaktam ripum ātatāyī varāṅgam urvyām apatat camū pateḥ divākaraḥ astāt iva rakta maṇḍalaḥ pareṇa kṛcchreṇa śarīram atyajat gṛham mahā ṛddhi iva sa saṅgam īśvaraḥ dehāt tu karṇasya nipātitasya tejaḥ dīptam kham vigāhya acireṇa tam somakāḥ prekṣya hatam śayānam prītāḥ nādam saha sainyaiḥ akurvan tūryāṇi ca ājaghnuḥ atīva hṛṣṭāḥ vāsāṃsi ca eva ādudhuvuḥ bhujān ca bala anvitāḥ ca api apare hi anṛtyan anyonyam āśliṣya nadantaḥ ūcuḥ dṛṣṭvā tu karṇam bhuvi niṣṭanantam hatam rathāt sāyakena avabhinnam mahā anilena agnim iva apaviddham yajña avasāne śayane niśā ante śaraiḥ ācita sarva aṅgaḥ śoṇita ogha pariplutaḥ vibhāti dehaḥ karṇasya sva raśmibhiḥ iva aṃśumān pratāpya senām āmitrīm dīptaiḥ śara gabhastibhiḥ balinā arjuna kālena nītaḥ astam karṇa bhāskaraḥ evam jīvitam ādāya karṇasya iṣuḥ jagāma ha aparāhṇe parāhṇasya sūtaputrasya māriṣa upari upari sainyānām tasya śatroḥ tat añjasā saṃjayaḥ uvāca karṇam tu śūram patitam pṛthivyām śara ācitam śoṇita digdha gātram dṛṣṭvā śayānam bhuvi madra rājaḥ chinna dhvajena apayayau rathena karṇe hate kuravaḥ prādravanta bhaya arditāḥ gāḍha viddhāḥ ca saṃkhye avekṣamāṇāḥ muhur arjunasya dhvajam mahāntam vapuṣā jvalantam saṃjayaḥ uvāca śalyaḥ tu karṇa arjunayoḥ vimarde balāni dṛṣṭvā mṛditāni bāṇaiḥ duryodhanam yāntam avekṣamāṇaḥ saṃdarśayat bhārata yuddha bhūmim nipātita syandana vāji nāgam dṛṣṭvā balam tat hata sūtaputram karṇam tu śūram patitam pṛthivyām śara ācitam śoṇita digdha gātram yadṛcchayā sūryam iva avani stham didṛkṣavaḥ saṃparivārya tasthuḥ prahṛṣṭa vitrasta viṣaṇṇa vismṛtāḥ tathā apare śoka gatāḥ iva abhavan pare tvadīyāḥ ca paraspareṇa yathā yathā eṣām prakṛtiḥ tathā abhavan niśamya karṇam kuravaḥ pradudruvuḥ hata ṛṣabhāḥ gāvaḥ iva a kula ākulāḥ kṛtvā vimardam bhṛśam arjunena karṇam hatam kesariṇā iva nāgam dṛṣṭvā śayānam bhuvi madra rājaḥ bhītaḥ apasarpat sa rathaḥ su śīghram madra adhipaḥ ca api vimūḍha cetāḥ tūrṇam rathena apahṛta dhvajena duryodhanasya antikam etya śīghram saṃbhāṣya duḥkha ārtam uvāca vākyam viśīrṇa nāga aśva ratha pravīram balam yama rāṣṭra kalpam anyonyam āsādya hatam mahadbhiḥ nara aśva nāgaiḥ giri kūṭa kalpaiḥ na etādṛśam bhārata yuddham āsīt yathā adya karṇa arjunayoḥ babhūva daivam tu yat tat sva vaśam pravṛttam tat pāṇḍavān pāti hinasti ca asmān kubera vaivasvata vāsavānām tulya prabhāva ambu pateḥ ca vīrāḥ avadhya kalpāḥ nihatāḥ narendrāḥ tava artha kāmāḥ yudhi pāṇḍaveyaiḥ etat vacaḥ madra pateḥ niśamya svam ca apanītam manasā nirīkṣya duryodhanaḥ dīna manāḥ visaṃjñaḥ punar punar nyaśvasat ārta rūpaḥ tam dhyāna mūkam kṛpaṇam bhṛśa ārtam ārtāyaniḥ dīnam uvāca vākyam śara avabhinnaiḥ patitaiḥ ca vājibhiḥ śvasadbhiḥ anyaiḥ kṣatajam vamadbhiḥ dīnaiḥ stanadbhiḥ parivṛtta netraiḥ mahīm daśadbhiḥ kṛpaṇam nadadbhiḥ nara aśva nāgaiḥ ca rathaiḥ ca marditaiḥ mahī mahā vaitaraṇī iva durdṛśā yaśasvibhiḥ nāga ratha aśva yodhibhiḥ padātibhiḥ ca abhimukhaiḥ hataiḥ paraiḥ viśīrṇa varma ābharaṇa ambara āyudhaiḥ vṛtā niśāntaiḥ iva pāvakaiḥ mahī śara prahāra abhihataiḥ mahā balaiḥ avekṣyamāṇaiḥ patitaiḥ sahasraśas pranaṣṭa saṃjñaiḥ punar ucchvasadbhiḥ mahī babhūva anugataiḥ iva agnibhiḥ śarāḥ tu karṇa arjuna bāhu muktāḥ vidārya nāga aśva manuṣya dehān prāṇān nirasya āśu mahīm atīyuḥ mahā uragāḥ vāsam iva abhitas astraiḥ rathaiḥ vara iṣūn mathitaiḥ ca yodhaiḥ saṃsyūta sūta aśva vara āyudha dhvajaiḥ viśīrṇa śastraiḥ vinikṛtta bandhuraiḥ nikṛtta cakra akṣa yuga triveṇubhiḥ prabhagna nīḍaiḥ maṇi hema maṇḍitaiḥ stṛtā mahī dyauḥ iva śāradaiḥ ghanaiḥ manuṣya mātaṅga ratha aśva rāśibhiḥ drutam vrajantaḥ bahudhā vicūrṇitāḥ sa hema paṭṭāḥ parighāḥ paraśvadhāḥ kaḍaṅgara ayaḥ musalāni paṭṭiśāḥ petuḥ ca khaḍgāḥ vimalāḥ vikośāḥ gadāḥ ca jāmbūnada paṭṭa baddhāḥ cāpāni rukma aṅgada bhūṣaṇāni śarāḥ ca kārtasvara citra puṅkhāḥ ṛṣṭyaḥ ca pītāḥ vimalāḥ vikośāḥ prāsāḥ sa khaḍgāḥ kanaka avabhāsāḥ chatrāṇi vāla vyajanāni śaṅkhāḥ srajaḥ ca puṣpa uttama hema citrāḥ kuthāḥ patākā ambara veṣṭitāḥ ca kirīṭa mālāḥ mukuṭāḥ ca śubhrāḥ prakīrṇakāḥ viprakīrṇāḥ kuthāḥ ca pradhāna muktā taralāḥ ca hārāḥ āpīḍa keyūra vara aṅgadāni graiveya niṣkāḥ sa suvarṇa sūtrāḥ maṇi uttamāḥ vajra suvarṇa muktāḥ ratnāni ca uccāvaca maṅgalāni gātrāṇi ca atyanta sukha ucitāni śirāṃsi ca indu pratima ānanāni dehān ca bhogān ca paricchadān ca tyaktvā manojñāni sukhāni ca api svadharma niṣṭhām mahatīm avāpya vyāptān ca lokān yaśasā samīyuḥ iti evam uktvā virarāma śalyaḥ duryodhanaḥ śoka parīta cetāḥ hā karṇa hā karṇa iti bruvāṇa ārtaḥ visaṃjñaḥ bhṛśam aśru netraḥ tam droṇaputra pramukhāḥ narendrāḥ sarve samāśvāsya saha prayānti nirīkṣamāṇāḥ muhur arjunasya dhvajam mahāntam yaśasā jvalantam nara aśva mātaṅga śarīra jena raktena siktā rudhireṇa bhūmiḥ rakta ambara sraj tapanīya yogāt nārī prakāśā iva sarva gamyā pracchanna rūpāḥ rudhireṇa rājan raudre muhūrte ativirājamānāḥ na eva avatasthuḥ kuravaḥ samīkṣya pravrājitāḥ deva lokāḥ ca sarve vadhena karṇasya su duḥkhitāḥ te hā karṇa hā karṇa iti bruvāṇāḥ drutam prayātāḥ śibirāṇi rājan divākaram raktam avekṣamāṇāḥ gāṇḍīva muktaiḥ tu suvarṇa puṅkhaiḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ śoṇita digdha vājaiḥ śaraiḥ cita aṅgaḥ bhuvi bhāti karṇaḥ hataḥ api san sūryaḥ iva aṃśumālī spṛṣṭvā karaiḥ lohita rakta rūpaḥ siṣṇāsuḥ abhyeti param samudram iti iva saṃcintya sura ṛṣi saṃghāḥ saṃprasthitāḥ yānti yathā niketam tat adbhutam prāṇabhṛtām bhayaṃkaram niśamya yuddham kuru vīra mukhyayoḥ dhanaṃjayasya ādhiratheḥ ca vismitāḥ praśaṃsamānāḥ prayayuḥ tadā janāḥ śaraiḥ saṃkṛtta varmāṇam vīram viśasane hatam gatāsum api rādheyam nā eva lakṣmīḥ vyamuñcata nānā ābharaṇavān rājan mṛṣṭa jāmbūnada aṅgadaḥ kanaka uttama saṃkāśaḥ pradīptaḥ iva pāvakaḥ sa putraḥ puruṣa vyāghraḥ saṃśāntaḥ pārtha tejasā pratāpya pāṇḍavān rājan pāñcālān ca astra tejasā sadbhiḥ sadā sat puruṣaḥ sa hataḥ dvairathe vṛṣaḥ yasya brāhmaṇasāt sarvam ātma artham na mahātmanaḥ na a deyam brāhmaṇeṣu āsīt yasya svam api jīvitam sadā nṝṇām priyaḥ dātā priya dānaḥ divam gataḥ ādāya tava putrāṇām jaya āśām śarma varma ca nabhaḥ paphāla atha nanāda ca urvī diśaḥ sa dhūmāḥ ca bhṛśam prajajvaluḥ mahā arṇavāḥ cukṣubhire ca sa svanāḥ sa kānanāḥ sa adri cayāḥ cakampuḥ pravivyathuḥ bhūta gaṇāḥ ca māriṣa bṛhaspatiḥ rohiṇīm saṃprapīḍya babhūva candra arka samāna varṇaḥ hate karṇe na diśaḥ viprajajñuḥ tamaḥ vṛtā dyauḥ vicacāla bhūmiḥ papāta ca ulkā jvalana prakāśā niśācarāḥ ca api abhavan prahṛṣṭāḥ śaśi prakāśa ānanam arjunaḥ yadā kṣureṇa karṇasya śiraḥ nyapātayat patākinā bhīma nināda ketunā hima indu śaṅkha sphaṭika avabhāsinā suvarṇa muktā maṇi vajra vidrumaiḥ alaṃkṛtena apratimāna raṃhasā raṇa ajire vīta bhayau virejatuḥ samāna yānau iva viṣṇu vāsavau saṃsādhayitvā eva kurūn śara oghaiḥ kapidhvajaḥ pakṣi vara dhvajaḥ ca prasahya śaṅkhau dhamatuḥ su ghoṣau manāṃsi arīṇām avasādayantau suvarṇa jāla avatatau mahā svanau hima avadātau parigṛhya pāṇibhiḥ cucumbatuḥ śaṅkha varau nṛṇām varau vara ānanābhyām yugapad ca dadhmatuḥ pṛthivīm antarikṣam ca dyām apaḥ ca api apūrayat tau śaṅkha śabdena ninādayantau vanāni śailān saritaḥ diśaḥ ca tatas prayātāḥ kuravaḥ javena śrutvā eva śaṅkha svanam īryamāṇam vihāya madra adhipatim patim ca duryodhanam bhārata bhāratānām mahā āhave tam bahu śobhamānam dhanaṃjayam bhūta gaṇāḥ sametāḥ samācitau karṇa śaraiḥ paraṃtapau ubhau vyabhātām samare acyuta arjunau tamaḥ nihatya abhyuditau yathā amalau śaśāṅka sūryau iva raśmi mālinau vihāya tān bāṇa gaṇān atha āgatau suhṛd vṛtau apratimāna vikramau sukham praviṣṭau śibiram svam īśvarau sadasya hūtau iva vāsava acyutau jaya abhivṛddhyā parayā abhipūjitau nihatya karṇam parama āhave tadā saṃjayaḥ uvāca āśliṣya pārtham dāśārhaḥ harṣāt vacanam abravīt vadham vai karṇa vṛtrābhyām kathayiṣyanti mānavāḥ vajriṇā nihataḥ vṛtraḥ saṃyuge bhūri tejasā tvayā tu nihataḥ karṇaḥ dhanuṣā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ vadham karṇasya saṃgrāme dīrgha kāla cikīrṣitam nivedya dharmarājasya tvam ānṛṇyam gamiṣyasi dhṛṣṭadyumnam yudhāmanyum mādrī putrau vṛkodaram parān abhimukhāḥ yattāḥ tiṣṭhadhvam bhadram astu vaḥ yāvat āvedyate rājñe hataḥ karṇaḥ arjunena vai sa taiḥ śūraiḥ anujñātaḥ yayau rāja niveśanam pārtham ādāya govindaḥ dadarśa ca yudhiṣṭhiram śayānam rāja śārdūlam kāñcane śayana uttame agṛhṇītām ca caraṇau muditau pārthivasya tau tayoḥ praharṣam ālakṣya prahārān ca ati mānuṣān rādheyam nihatam matvā samuttasthau yudhiṣṭhiraḥ tatas asmai tat yathāvṛttam vāsudevaḥ priyaṃvadaḥ īṣat utsmayamānaḥ tu kṛṣṇaḥ rājānam abravīt yudhiṣṭhiram hata amitram kṛtāñjaliḥ atha acyutaḥ diṣṭyā gāṇḍīvadhanvā ca pāṇḍavaḥ ca vṛkodaraḥ tvam ca api kuśalī rājan mādrī putrau ca pāṇḍavau muktāḥ vīra kṣayāt asmāt saṃgrāmāt loma harṣaṇāt kṣipram uttara kālāni kuru kāryāṇi pārthiva hataḥ vaikartanaḥ krūraḥ sūtaputraḥ mahā balaḥ diṣṭyā jayasi rāja indra diṣṭyā vardhasi pāṇḍava yaḥ sa dyūta jitām kṛṣṇām prāhasat puruṣa adhamaḥ tasya adya sūtaputrasya bhūmiḥ pibati śoṇitam śete asau śara dīrṇa aṅgaḥ śatruḥ te kuru puṃgava tam paśya puruṣa vyāghra vibhinnam bahudhā śaraiḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ tu dāśārham prahṛṣṭaḥ pratyapūjayat diṣṭyā diṣṭyā iti rāja indra prītyā ca idam uvāca ha pragṛhya ca kuruśreṣṭhaḥ sa aṅgadam dakṣiṇam bhujam asakṛt ca api medhāvī kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ mama kathām etām mahā bāho divyām akathayat prabhuḥ tava kṛṣṇa prabhāveṇa gāṇḍīvena dhanaṃjayaḥ jayati abhimukhān śatrūn na ca āsīt vimukhaḥ kva cit jayaḥ ca eva dhruvaḥ asmākam na tu asmākam parājayaḥ evam uktvā mahā rāja tam ratham hema bhūṣitam āsthāya puruṣa vyāghraḥ sva balena abhisaṃvṛtaḥ kṛṣṇa arjunābhyām vīrābhyām anumanya tatas priyam āgataḥ bahu vṛttāntam draṣṭum āyodhanam tadā ābhāṣamāṇaḥ tau vīrau ubhau mādhava phalgunau sa dadarśa raṇe karṇam śayānam puruṣa ṛṣabham gāṇḍīva muktaiḥ viśikhaiḥ sarvatas śakalīkṛtam sa putram nihatam dṛṣṭvā karṇam rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ praśaśaṃsa nara vyāghrau ubhau mādhava pāṇḍavau adya rājā asmi govinda pṛthivyām bhrātṛbhiḥ saha tvayā nāthena vīreṇa viduṣā paripālitaḥ hatam dṛṣṭvā nara vyāghram rādheyam abhimāninam nirāśaḥ adya durātmā asau dhārtarāṣṭraḥ bhaviṣyati jīvitāt ca api rājyāt ca hate karṇe mahā rathe tvad prasādāt vayam ca eva kṛtārthāḥ puruṣa ṛṣabha tvam ca gāṇḍīvadhanvā ca vijayī yadu nandana diṣṭyā jayasi govinda diṣṭyā karṇaḥ nipātitaḥ evam sa bahuśas hṛṣṭaḥ praśaśaṃsa janārdanam arjunam ca api rāja indra dharmarājaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ tatas bhīma prabhṛtibhiḥ sarvaiḥ ca bhrātṛbhiḥ vṛtam vardhayanti sma rājānam harṣa yuktāḥ mahā rathāḥ nakulaḥ sahadevaḥ ca pāṇḍavaḥ ca vṛkodaraḥ sātyakiḥ ca mahā rāja vṛṣṇīnām pravaraḥ rathaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca pāṇḍu pāñcāla sṛñjayāḥ te vardhayitvā nṛpatim pāṇḍu putram yudhiṣṭhiram jita kāśinaḥ labdhalakṣāḥ yuddha śauṇḍāḥ prahāriṇaḥ stuvantaḥ stava yuktābhiḥ vāgbhiḥ kṛṣṇau paraṃtapau jagmuḥ sva śibirāya eva mudā yuktāḥ mahā rathāḥ evam eṣa kṣayaḥ vṛttaḥ su mahān loma harṣaṇaḥ vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ uvāca śrutvā tat apriyam rājan dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ mahīpatiḥ papāta bhūmau niśceṣṭaḥ kauravyaḥ parama ārtivān tathā satyavratā devī gāndhārī dharma darśinī tam pratyagṛhṇāt viduraḥ nṛpatim saṃjayaḥ tathā paryāśvāsayataḥ ca evam tau ubhau eva bhūmipam tathā evā utthāpayām āsuḥ gāndhārīm rāja yoṣitaḥ tābhyām āśvāsitaḥ rājā tūṣṇīm āsīt vicetanaḥ
